Catalog number: M00501
Uniform title: ācārasāratantra
Main title: ācārasāratantram
Secondary title: haṭhapradīpakā
Secondary title: samayācāra
Author : svātmārāma
Manuscript : NGMCP 3-325 Reel B 116/8

Description: 
The manuscript contains 4 chapters of the haṭhapradīpakā   followed by the acārasāratantra which teachs a form of extreme Kaulism called cīnācāra.   This is followed by a tract of 300 verses called samayācāra .    Followed by a hymn to a goblet of wine used in this Kaula ritual attributed to the rudrayāmala . Then the ulūkalpa

32)

* * * * ścalaulyaṃ ca ṣaḍbhiryogo vinaśyati || 15 || 

utsāhāt sāhasādhairyāt tatvajñānāśca niścayāt |
janasaṃgaparityāgāt ṣaḍbhiryogaḥ prasidhyati || 16 ||

vasiṣṭhādyaiśca munibhirmatsyendrādyaiśca yogibhiḥ |
aṃgīkṛtānyāsanāni kathyaṃte kāni cinmayā || 17 ||

haṭhasya prathamāṃ gatvā dāsanaṃ pūrvamucyate |
tat kuryādāsanasthairyamārogyaṃ cāṃgalāghavaṃ || 18 ||

jānūrdhvoraṃtare samyak kṛtvā pādatale ubhe |
ṛjukāyaḥ samāsīta svastikaṃ tat pracakṣyate || 19 ||

savye dakṣiṇagulphaṃ tu pṛṣṭhapārśve niyojayet |
dakṣiṇe tu tathā savyaṃ gomukhaṃ gomukhaṃ yathā || 20 ||

ekaṃ pādaṃ tathaikasmin vinyasyoruṇi saṃsthitaṃ |
itarasmistathā coruṃ vīrāsanamitīritaṃ || 21 ||

guḍaṃ nivadhya gulphābhyāṃ vyutkrameṇa samāhitaḥ |
kūrmāsanaṃ bhavedetaditi yogavido viduḥ || 22 ||

padmāsanaṃ tu saṃyojya jānūrvoraṃtare karau |
vinyasya bhūmau saṃsthāpya vyomasthaḥ kukkuṭāsanaṃ || 23 ||

kukkuṭāsanavaṃdhastho dorbhyāṃ saṃvadhyakaṃdharaṃ |
śeve kūrmavaduttānametaduttānakūrmakaṃ || 24 ||

pādāṃguṣṭau tu pāṇibhyāṃ gṛhītvā śravaṇāvadhi |
dhanurākarṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā dhanurāsanamīritaṃ || 25 ||

vāmorumūlārpitadakṣapādo jānvorbahirveṣṭita dakṣadoṣṇā |
pragṛhya tiṣṭhan parivartitāṃgaḥ śrīmatsyanāthoditamāsanaṃ syāt || 26 ||

matsyendrapīṭhaṃ jaṭharapracaṃpipracaṃḍarunmaṃḍalakhaṃḍanāstraṃ |
abhyasya tāṃ kuṃḍalinīṃ pravodhaṃ daṃḍasthiratvaṃ ca dadāti puṃsāṃ || 27 
||

prasārya pādau bhuvi daṇḍarūpau dorbhyāṃ ca pāda dvitayaṃ gṛhītvā |
jānū parinyastalalāṭa deśoviśedidaṃ paścimatā na vāhuḥ || 28 ||

33a)

iti paścimatā na māsanāgryaṃ pavanaṃ paścimavāhanaṃ karoti |
udaraṃ jaṭharānalasya kuryādudare kārśpamarogatāṃ ca puṃsāṃ || 29 ||

dharāmavaṣṭabhya karasthalābhyāṃ tatkūrparasthāpita nāmi pārśvaḥ |
uccāsanodaṃḍa vadutthitaḥ khemāyūra metatpravadaṃti pīṭhaṃ || 30 ||

harati sakalarogānāśu gulmodarādīnabhi bhavati ca doṣānāsanaṃ śrīmayūraṃ 
|
bahukadaśana bhuktaṃ bhasmakuryādaśeṣe janayati jaṭharāgni jārayet 
kālakūṭaṃ || 31 ||

uttāna śavavadbhūmau śayanaṃ tu śavāsanaṃ |
sarvāsana bhrāṃti haraṃ citta vibhrāṃti sādhanaṃ || 32 ||

caturāśītyāsanāni śivena kathitāni tu |
tebhyaścatuṣkamādāya sārabhūtaṃ vravīmyahaṃ || 33 ||

siddhaṃ padmaṃ tathā bhadraṃ siṃhaṃ ceti catuṣṭayaṃ |
śreṣṭhaṃ tatrāpi ca sakhe tiṣṭha siddhāsane sadā || 34 ||

siddhāsanaṃ ||

yonidvārakamaṃghri mūlaghaṭitaṃ kṛtvā dṛḍhaṃ trinyase meḍhre 
pādamayaikameva hṛdaye dhṛtvāsanaṃ vigrahaṃ |
sthāṇuḥ saṃyamitendriyo caladṛśāpaśyedbhruvoraṃtaraṃ caitanmokṣakapāṭa 
bhedajanakaṃ siddhāsanaṃ procyate || 35 ||

matāṃtare ||

meḍhrādhaḥ parivinyasya vāmagulphaṃ tayopari |
gulphāṃtaraṃ ca nikṣipya siddhāsanamidaṃ bhavet || 36 ||

pūrvoktameva matsyendra stanaṃ etasiddhāsanaṃ prāhuranyevajñāsanaṃ viduḥ 
|
muktāprāṇaṃ vadatyanye prāhurguptāsanaṃ pare || 37 ||

yameṣvevamitāhāramahiṃsā niyameṣvapi |
mukhyaṃ sarvāsaneṣvekaṃ siddhāḥ siddhāsanaṃ viduḥ || 38 ||

caturāśīti pīṭheṣu siddhameva sadābhyaset |
dvāsaptati sahasreṣu suṣumṇāmiva nāḍiṣu || 39 ||

33b)

ātmadhyāyī mitāhārī yāvad dvādaśa vatsaraṃ |
sadā siddhāsanābhyāsādyoginīpyaṃti māpnuyāt || 40 ||

śramadairvahubhiḥ pīṭhaiḥ kiṃ syāt siddhāsane sati |
prāṇānile sāvadhānaṃ vaddhe kevala kuṃbhataḥ || 41 ||

utpadyate nirāyāsā svayamevonmanīyathā |
athekasminneva dṛḍhaṃ vaddhe siddhāsane sadā || 42 ||

vaṃdhatrayamanāyāsāt svayamevopajāyate |
nāsanaṃ siddhasadṛśaṃ na kuṃbhaḥ kevaloyamaḥ |
na khecarī samā mudrā na nāda sadṛśolayaḥ || 43 ||

atha padmāsanaṃ ||

vāmārūpari dakṣiṇaṃ ca caraṇaṃ saṃsthāpya vāmaṃ tathāyāmyorūpari 
paścimena vidhinā dhṛtvā karābhyāṃ dṛḍhaṃ |
aṃguṣṭho hṛdaye nidhāya civukaṃ nāsāgramālokayedetadvyādhi 
vināśakāriyamināṃ padmāsanaṃ procyate || 44 ||

matāṃtare tu ||

uttānau caraṇau kṛtvā ūrusaṃsthau prayatnataḥ |
ūru madhye tayottānau pāṇī kṛtvā tato dṛḍhau || 45 ||

nāsāgre vinyasedrāja daṃtamūlaṃ ca jihvayā |
uttabhya civukaṃ vakṣasphacchāpya pavanaṃ śanaiḥ || 46 ||

idaṃ padmāsanaṃ proktaṃ sarvavyādhi vināśanaṃ |
durlabhaṃ yena kenāpi dhīmatā labhyate bhuvi || 47 ||

paścāduktaṃ matsyendramaṃtaṃ ||

kṛtvā saṃghaṭitau karau dṛḍhataraṃ padhvā?tu padmāsanaṃ |
gāṃḍhaṃ vakṣasi saṃnidhāya civukaṃ dhyānaṃ ca taccaitasi ||

vāraṃvāramapānamūrddhamanilaṃ proccālayan pūrayan muṃcan 
prāṇāmupaiti vodhamatulaṃ śaktipramāvādataḥ || 48 ||

padmāsana sthito yogī nāḍī dvāreṣu pūrayet |
mārutaṃ dhārayedyastu samukto nātra saṃśayaḥ || 49 ||

atha siṃhāsanaṃ ||

gulphau ca vṛṣanasyādhaḥ śīvanyāḥ pārśvato nyaset |
dakṣiṇe savyagulpha ca dakṣagulphaṃ ca savyake || 50 ||

34a)

hastau jānostu saṃsthāpya svāṃgulīḥ saṃprasārya ca |
vyātta vaktro nirīkṣena nāsāgaṃ susamāhitaḥ || 51 ||

siṃhāsanaṃ bhavedetat pūjitaṃ yogibhiḥ sadā |
vaṃdhasya saṃdhānaṃ kurute cāsanottamaṃ || 52 ||

atha bhadrāsanaṃ || 

gulphau ca vṛṣaṇasyādhaḥ sīvanyāḥ pārśvayoḥ kṣipet |
pārśvapādau ca pāṇibhyāṃ dṛḍhaṃ vadhvā suniścalaṃ || 53 ||

bhadrāsanaṃ bhavedetat sarvavyādhivināśanaṃ |
gorakṣāsanamidaṃ vai prāhuste siddhayoginaḥ || 54 ||

evamāsana vaṃdhyeṣu yogīndro vijitaśramaḥ |
athābhyasennāḍi śuddhaṃ mudrādi pavana kriyāṃ || 55 ||

āsanaṃ kuṃbhakaścitraṃ mudrāsvīkaraṇaṃ tathā |
atha nādānusaṃdhānamabhyāsānukramo haṭhe || 56 ||

brahmacārī mitāhāro yogīyogaparāyaṇaḥ |
avdādūrdhvaṃ bhavet siddho nātrakāryāvicāraṇā || 57 ||

susnigdha madhurāhāra caturthāṃśa vivarjitaṃ |
bhujyate śivasaṃprītyai mitāhāraḥ sa ucyate || 58 ||

kaṭvamlatiktalavaṇoṣṇaharītathā śāka sauvīra tailatilasarṣapamatsyamaghāḥ |
ājādi māṃsadadhitakra kulacchakolapipākahiṃgulasunāghame pathyamāhuḥ || 
59 ||

bhojanaṃ sahita viṃdyā punarapyuṣṭī kṛtaṃ rūkṣaṃ |
atilavaṇāsavapalalaṃkadaśanaśākotkaṭapiṣṭaṃ || 60 ||

varjaye durjana prītiṃ vahnistrīpathi sevanaṃ |
prātaḥ snānopavāsādi kāyaṃ kleśa vidhiṃ tathā || 61 ||

godhūmaśāliyavaṣaṣṭika śobhanānnaṃ kṣīrājya khaṃḍanavanīta 
sitāmadhūni |
śuṃṭhī phaṭolaphalakādi ca paṃcaśākaṃ mudrādi gavyamuditaṃ ca yamīndra 
pathyaṃ || 62 ||

34b)

miṣṭaṃ sumadhura snigdhaṃ gavyaṃ dhātu prapoṣakaṃ |
manobhilaṣitaṃ yogyaṃ yogī bhojanamācaret || 63 ||

yuvāvṛddhoti vṛddho vā vyādhito durvalopi vā | 
abhyāsāt siddhimāpnoti sarvayogeṣvataṃdritaḥ || 64 ||

pīṭhāni kuṃbhakaścitrā divyāni karaṇāni ca |
sarvopyayaṃ haṭhābhyāso rājayoga phalāvadhiḥ || 65 ||

iti svātmārāmayogīndraviracitāyāṃ haṭhapradīpakāyāṃ 
yamaniyamāsanopadeśalakṣaṇo nāma prathamopadeśaḥ ||


athāsane dṛḍhe yogīvasīhi namitāśanaḥ |
gurūpadiṣṭamārgeṇa prāṇāyāmān samabhyaset || 1 ||

cale vāte calaṃ sarvaṃ niścale niścalaṃ tathā |
yogī sthāṇutvamāpnoti tato vāyuṃ nirodhayet || 2 ||

jñānaṃ kuto manasi jīvati devi yāvat prāṇopi jīvati mano mriyatena tāvat |
prāṇaṃ mano dvayamiti pralayaṃ nayeta mokṣaṃ tu gacchati naro na kathaṃ 
cidanyaḥ || 3 ||

yāvadvāyuḥ sthiro dehe tāvajjīvitamucyate |
maraṇaṃ tasya niḥkrāṃtistanovāyuṃ nirodhayet || 4 ||

malākulāsu nāḍīṣu māruto naiva madhyagaḥ |
kathaṃ syādunmanī bhāvaḥ kāyasiddhiḥ kathaṃ bhavet || 5 ||

 buddhimeti yadā sarvaṃ nāḍīcakraṃ malākulaṃ |
tadaiva jāyate yogī prāṇasaṃgrahaṇe kṣamaḥ || 6 ||

prāṇābhyāsaṃ tataḥ kuryān nityaṃ sātvikayādhiyā |
yathā suṣumṇā nāḍīsthā malāśeṣaṃ prayāṃti ca || 7 ||

vaddha padmāpadmāsano yogī prāṇaṃ caṃdreṇa pūrayet |
dhārayitvā yathāśaktirbhūyaḥ sūryeṇa recayet || 8 ||

vidhivat kuṃbhakaṃ kṛtvā punaścaṃdreṇa recayet || 9 ||

35a)

yena tyajet tena pūrvaṃ dhārayedanirodhataḥ |
recayecca tatonyevaśanaireva na vegataḥ || 10 ||

prāṇaṃ cediḍayā pivenniyamitaṃ bhūyo'nyayā recayet |
pītvā piṃgalayā samīraṇamatho vaddhvā tyajedvāmayā || 11 ||

sūryācaṃdramasoranena vidhinābhyāsaṃsamātanvaṃtāṃ |
śuddhānāḍī gaṇā bhavati yamināṃ māsatrayādūrdhvataḥ || 12 ||

prātarmadhyadine sāyaṃ madhyarātre ca kuṃbhakān |
śanairaśīti paryaṃtaṃ caturvāraṃ samabhyaset || 

kanīyasī bhavet svedakaṃpo bhavati madhyame |
uttiṣṭhatyuttame prāṇarodhe padmāsanaṃ mahuḥ || 13 ||

jalena śramajātena gātramardanamācaret |
dṛḍhatā laghunā vāpi tena gātrasya jāyate || 14 ||

abhyāsakāle prathame śastaṃ kṣīrājya bhojanaṃ |
tatobhyāsedṛḍhībhūtena tathā niyamagrahaḥ || 15 ||

yathā siṃhogajovyāghro bhavedvaśya śanaiḥ śanaiḥ |
tathaiva sādhito vāyuranyathā haṃti sādhakaṃ || 16 ||

prāṇāyāmena yuktena sarvarogakṣayo bhavet |
ayuktābhyāsa yogeṇa sarvarogasamudbhavaḥ || 16 ||

hikkā śvāsaśca kāśaśca śirakarṇākṣi vedanā |
bhavaṃti vividhā doṣāḥ pavanasya vyatikramāt || 17 ||

yuktaṃ yuktaṃ tyajedvāyuṃ yuktaṃ yuktaṃ ca pūrayet |
yuktaṃ yuktaṃ ca vadhnīyādevaṃ śuddhimavāpnuyāt || 18 || 

yadā tu nāḍī śuddhiḥ syāt tadā cihnāni vāhyataḥ |
kāyasya kṛśatākāṃtistadājāyata niścitaṃ || 19 ||

yatheṣṭaṃ dhāraṇaṃ vāyoḥ analasya pradīpanaṃ |
nādābhivyaktirārogyaṃ jāyate nāḍi śodhanāt || 20 ||

medaśleṣmādi saṃpūrṇaḥ ṣaṭkarmāṇi samācaret |

35b)

anyastu nācaret tāni doṣāṇāṃ samabhāgikaḥ || 21 ||

dhautirvastiśca nītiśca trāṭakaṃ naulikā tathā |
kapāli bhāti caitāni ṣaṭkarmāṇi pracakṣate || 22 ||

karmaṣaṭkamidaṃ proktaṃ ghaṭaśodhanakārakaṃ |
vicitraguṇasaṃdhāyi pūjaye stuti puṃgavaiḥ || 23 ||

tatradhauti ||

caturaṃgulavistāraṃ vastrāṃsanairgraset |
tataḥ pratyāhareccaitaduditaṃ dhauti karma tat || 24 ||

kāsaḥ śvāsaḥ plīhakuṣṭaṃ kapharogāśca viṃśati |
dhauti karma prabhāvena gacchaṃtyeva na saṃśayaḥ || 25 ||

atha vasti ||

nābhidadhnajale pāna nyastanālotkaṭāsanaḥ |
ādhārākuṃcana kuryā kṣālanaṃvasti karmakṛt || 26 ||

gulmaplīhodaraṃ vāpi vātapittakaphodbhavā |
vastikarmaprabhāveṇa vāryaṃte sa kalāmayāḥ || 27 ||

dhātviṃdriyātaḥ karaṇapramodaṃ dadyācca kāṃtiṃ dahanapradīptiṃ |
aśeṣa doṣopacayaṃmihanyādabhyasya mānaṃ jalavasti karma || 27 ||

udaragatapadārthaśuddhamaṃtī pavanamapānamudīrya kaṃṭhanāle |
kramaparicaya vaśya vāyumārgā gajakaraṇīti gadyate haṭhajñaiḥ || 28 ||

athanitī sūtraṃ vitasti susnigdhaṃ nāsānāle praveśayet |
naśāmukhānnirgamayeccaiṣānīti siddhairnigadyate || 29 ||

kapālaśodhanī kaṃṭhaddivyadṛṣṭi pradāyinī |
jānūrdhvajātarogaughaṃ jagatyāśu satīnati || 30 ||

atha trāṭaka ||

nirīkṣenniścala dṛśā sūkṣmaṃ lakṣaṃ samāhitaḥ |
aśru saṃpātaparyaṃtamācāryaistrāṭakaṃ smṛtaṃ || 31 ||

moṭakaṃ netrarogānāṃ taṃdrādīnāṃ kapāṭakaṃ |
yatnataḥ trāṭakaṃ gopyaṃ yathā hāṭakapeṭakaṃ || 32 ||

atha nauliḥ ||

36a)

āmaṃdāvartavegena tuṃdaṃ savyāpasavyataḥ |
natāṃso bhramayed deṣānauligauḍaiḥ prakāśyate || 33 ||

maṃdāgni saṃdīpana pācanādi saṃdhāyikānandakarī sadaiva |
aśeṣadoṣāmaya śoṣaṇī ca haṭhakriyā mauliriyaṃ ca naulī || 34 ||

atha kapālabhāti ||

bhastrevalohakārasya recapūrau sa saṃbhramau |
kapālabhātī vikhyātā kaphadoṣo viśoṣiṇī || 35 ||

ṣaṭkarma nirgatasthaulya kaphamedomalānūjayet |
prāṇāyāmaṃ tataḥ kuryādanāyāsena sidhyati || 36 ||

prāṇāyāmaireva dṛḍhaṃ prabhuṣyaṃti malā iti |
ācāryāṇāṃ tu keṣāṃ cidanyat karma na saṃmataṃ || 37 ||

brahmādayopi tridaśāḥ pavanābhyāsa tatparāḥ |
abhūvannaṃtakabhayāstasmāt pavanamabhyaset || 39 ||

vahvāmayopi nāpnoti pavanābhyāsa tatparaḥ |
samanaskoṃtakabhayaṃ tasmāt pavanamabhyaset || 40 ||

yāvadvaddho maruddehe tāvaccittaṃ nirāśrayaḥ |
yāvat paścodbhruvormadhyaṃ tāvat kālabhayaṃ kutaḥ || 41 ||

vidhivat prāṇasaṃpākairnāḍī cakre viśodhite |
suṣumṇā vadanaṃ bhitvā mukhādviśati mārutaḥ || 42 ||

mārute madhyasaṃcāre manaḥ sthairyaṃ prajāyate |
yo manaḥ susthirī bhāvaḥ saiṣāvasthā manonmanī || 43 ||

tatsiddhaye vidhānajñaścitrān kurvīta kuṃbhakān |
vicitra kuṃbhakābhyāsādvicitrāṃ siddhimāpnuyāt || 44 ||

sūryabhedanamujjāyī sītkārī śītalī tathā |
bhastrikā bhramarī mūrchā kevalaścāṣṭakuṃbhakāḥ || 45 ||

pūrakāṃte ca kartavyo vaṃdho jālaṃdharābhidhaḥ |
kuṃbhakāṃte recakādau kartavyaḥ sūḍiyāṇakaḥ || 46 ||

ādhārā kuṃcanenāśu kaṃṭhasaṃkocane kṛte |
madhye paścimatānena syāt prāpyo brahmanāḍigaḥ || 47 ||

36b)

apāna mūrdhvamucchāpya prāṇaṃ kaṃṭhādadho nayet |
yogījarā vinirmuktaḥ ṣoḍaśīvayasā bhavet || 48 ||

tatra sūryabhedanaṃ ||

asane sukhade yogī vadhvā vajrāsanaṃ tataḥ |
dakṣanāḍyā samākṛṣya bahisthaṃ pavanaṃ śanaiḥ || 49 ||

ākeśādānakhāgrācca nirodhāvadhi kuṃbhayet |
tataḥ śanairvāmanāḍyā recayet pavanaṃ śanaiḥ || 50 ||

kapālaśodhanaṃ vātadoṣaghnaṃ kṛmidoṣanut |
punaḥ punaridaṃ kāryaṃ sūryabhedenamuttamaṃ || 51 ||

athojāyī ||

mukhaṃ niyamya nāḍī syāmāṃ kṛṣyapavanaṃ śanaiḥ |
yathālagati kaṃṭhāttu hṛdayāvadhi sasvanaṃ || 52 ||

pūrvavat kuṃbhavat prāṇaṃ recayediḍayā tataḥ |
śleṣadoṣaharaṃ caivaṃ dehānalavivardhanaṃ || 53 ||

nāḍījalodrā dhātu gata doṣa vināśanaṃ |
gacchatāṃ gacchatāṃ kāryamujjāpyākhyaṃ tu kuṃbhakaṃ || 54 ||

atha sītkārī ||

chikāṃ dadyāt sadā vaktre ghrāṇe caiva vijṛṃbhakāṃ |
evamabhyāsa yogena kāmadevo dvitīyakaḥ || 55 ||

yoginīcakra sāmānya sṛṣṭisaṃhārakārakaḥ |
na kṣudhā na tṛṣā nidrā naivālasya prajāyate || 56 ||

bhavet svacchaṃda dehastu sarvopadravavarjitaḥ |
anena vidhinā nityaṃ yogīṃdro bhuvimaṇḍale || 57 ||

evamevokta gorakṣeṇa rasanā tālumūlena yaḥ prāṇaṃ satataṃ pivet |
aṣṭhāddūrdhva bhavet tasya sarvaroga parikṣayaḥ || 58 ||

atha śītalī ||

jihvayā vāyumākṛṣya pūrvavat kuṃbhakādanu |
śanaistu ghrāṇaraṃdhrābhyāṃ recayedanilaṃdhiyā || 59 ||

gulmaplīhādikān doṣān jvarapittaṃ kṣudhāṃ tṛṣā |
viṣāṇī śītalīnāma kuṃbhakāyaṃ nihaṃti ca || 60 ||

atha bhastrikā ||

37a)

ūrvoru recayeddhattenobhe pādatale yadā |
padmāsanaṃ bhavet samyak sarvapāpa pranāśanaṃ || 61 ||

samyak padmāsanaṃ vadhvā samagrīvodaraḥ sudhīḥ |
mukha niyamya yatnena prāṇaṃ ghrāṇena recayet || 62 ||

yathā lagati hṛtkaṃṭha kapole sasvanaṃ tataḥ |
vegena pūrayet kiṃciddhṛdayāvadhi mārutaṃ || 63 ||

punarvirecayet tadvat pūrayecca punaḥ punaḥ |
yathaivalohakārāṇāṃ bhastrāvegeṇa cālpate || 64 ||

yathodaraṃ bhavet pūrṇaṃ pavanena tathā laghuḥ |
dhārayennāsikāṃ madhya tarjanībhyāṃ vinā dṛḍhaiḥ || 66 ||

kuṃbhakaṃ pūrvavat kṛtvā recayediḍayānilaṃ |
vātapittaśleṣmaharaṃ dehānalavivardhanaṃ || 67 ||

kuṃḍalī vodhanaṃ sarva doṣaghnaṃ sukhadaṃ śubhaṃ |
brahmanāḍī mukhāṃtastha kaphādyārgalanāśanaṃ || 68 ||

guṇatrayasamudbhūtaṃ graṃthitrayavibhedakaṃ |
viśeṣeṇa tu kartavyaṃ bhastrākhyaṃ kuṃbhakaṃ tvidaṃ || 69 ||

atha bhramarī || 

vegoghoṣaṃ pūrakaṃ bhṛṃganādaṃ bhṛṃgīnādaṃ recakaṃ 
maṃdamaṃdaṃ |
yogīṃdrāṇāmevamabhyāsa yogāccittejātākā cidānaṃdamūrchā || 70 ||

atha mūrchā ||

pūrakāṃte gāḍhataraṃ vadhvā jālāṃdharaṃ śanaiḥ |
recayen mūrchanākhyeyaṃ manomūrchā sukhapradā || 71 ||

aṃtaḥ pravartitā dhīrāmārutā pūritodaraḥ |
payasyagādhepi sukhāt plavate padmapatravat || 72 ||

atha kevalakuṃbhakaḥ ||

prāṇāyāma tridhā prokto rece pūraka kuṃbhakaiḥ |
sahitaḥ kevalaśceti kuṃbhako vividho mataḥ || 73 ||

recakaḥ sapūrakaḥ kārya śanai sahita kuṃbhakaḥ |
yāvat kevalasiddhiḥ syāt tāvadevaṃ samabhyaset || 74 ||

recakaṃ pūrakaṃ muktvā sukhaṃ yadvāyu dhāraṇaṃ |

37b)

prāṇāyāmo yamityuyuktaḥ savai kevalakuṃbhakaḥ || 75 ||

kevale kuṃbhake siddhe reca pūraka varjite |
na kiṃtu durlabhaṃ tasyā triṣu lokeṣu vidyate || 76 ||

śaktaḥ kevala kuṃbhena yatheṣṭaṃ vāyudhāraṇaṃ |
rājayogapadaṃ samyak labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ || 77 ||

haṭhaṃ vinārājayogo rājayogaṃ vinā haṭhaḥ |
na sidhyaṃti tato yugmamāniḥṣyanteḥ samabhyaset || 78 ||

kuṃbhitaḥ prāṇarecāṃte kuryāccitaṃ nirāmayaṃ |
evamabhyāsa yogena rājayogapadaṃ vrajet || 79 ||

kuṃbhakāt kuṃḍalī bodha kuṃḍalī bodhato bhavet |
anargalā suṣumnā ca haṭhasiddhiśca jāyate || 80 ||

vapuḥ kṛśatvaṃ vadane prasannatā nāḍī sphuṭatvaṃ nayane ca nirmale |
arogatā viṃdujayogni dīrghatā bhaveyuretāni kṛtetra kuṃbhake || 81 ||

ityātmārāmayogīndraviracitāyāṃ haṭhapradīpikāyāṃ 
citrakuṃbhakaprāṇāyāmalakṣaṇaṃ nāmādvitīya upadeśaḥ || 


sa śailavana dhātrīṇāṃ yathādhāro hi nāyakaḥ |
sarveṣāṃ yogataṃtrāṇāṃ tathāraudho hi kuṃḍalī || 1 ||

suptāguru prasādena yena jāgarti kuṃḍalī |
tadā sarvāṇi padmāṇi bhidyate graṃthayopi ca || 2 ||

prāṇasya śūnyapadavī tathā rājapathāyate |
yata cittaṃ nirālambaṃ tathā kālasya vaṃcanaṃ || 3 ||

tasmāt sarvaprayatnena pravādhayitumīśvarīṃ |
brahmadvāramukhe suptāṃ mudrābhyāsaṃ samabhyaset || 4 ||

mahāmudrāmaḍā vaṃdho mahāvedhaśca khecarī |
ūḍīyāṇo mūlavaṃdho vaṃdhojālaṃ dharābhidhaḥ || 5 ||

karaṇī viparītākhyā vajrolī śakticālanaṃ |
idaṃ hi mudrā daśakaṃ jarāmaraṇanāśakaṃ || 6 ||

38a)

ādināthoditaṃ samyagaṣṭaiśvarya pradāyakaṃ |
vallabhaṃ sarvasiddhānāṃ durlabhaṃ marutānapi || 7 ||

gopanīyaṃ prayatnena yathā ratnarakaraṃḍakaṃ |
kasyacinnaiva vaktavyaṃ kulastrī surataṃ yathā || 8 ||

tatra mahāmudrā ||

pādamūjena vāmeṇa yoniṃ saṃpīḍya dakṣiṇaṃ |
pādaṃ prasāritaṃ kṛtvā karābhyāṃ dhārayed dṛḍhaṃ || 9 ||

kaṃṭhe vaṃdhaṃ samāropya dhārayed vāyumūrdhvataḥ |
yathā daṃḍahataḥ sarpo daṃḍākāraḥ prajāyate || 10 ||

ṛjvī bhūtā tathā śakti kuṃḍalī sahasā bhavet |
tadāsau maraṇāvasthā jāyate dvipuṭāśritā || 11 ||

tataḥ śanaiḥ śanaireva recayenna tu vegataḥ |
iyaṃ khalu mahāmudrā mahāsiddhaiḥ praśasyate || 12 ||

mahākleśāyato doṣā jīyaṃti maraṇādayaḥ |
mahāmudrā ca te naiva vadaṃti vivudhottamāḥ || 13 ||

caṃdrāṃge tu samabhyasya sūryāṃge punarabhyaset |
yāvatulyā bhavet saṃkhyā tato mudrāṃ visarjayet || 14 ||

nahi paśyamapaśyaṃ vā rasāḥ sarvepi nīrasāḥ |
api bhuktaṃ rasayoraṃ * pīyūṣamivajīryate || 15 ||

kṣayakuṣṭagadāvarta gulmaplīhapurogamāḥ |
tasya rogāḥ kṣayaṃ yāṃti mahāmudrāṃ ca yo bhyaset || 16 ||

kathite yaṃ mahāmudrā mahāsiddhikarī nṛṇāṃ |
gopanīyā prayatnena na deyā yasya kasyacit || 17 ||

atha mahāvaṃdhaḥ ||

pārṣṇi vāmasya pādasya yoni sthāne niyojayet |
vāmorūpari saṃsthāpya dakṣiṇaṃ caraṇaṃ tathā || 18 ||

pūrayitvā tato vāyuṃ hṛdaye cikukaṃ dṛḍhaḥ |
niḥpīḍyayonimākucyamanormadye niyojayet || 19 ||

dhārayitvā yathāśakti recayedanilaṃ śanaiḥ |

38b)

savyāṃge ca samabhyasya gakṣāṃge punarabhyaset || 20 ||

matamatra ca keṣāṃcit kaṃṭhavaddhaṃ tu varjayet |
rājadaṃtadvayaṃ tatra jihvayāttaṃ bhayediti || 21 ||

ayaṃ khalu mahāvaṃdho mahāsiddhi pradāyakā |
kālapāśa mahāvaṃdho vimocana vicakṣaṇaḥ || 22 ||

ayaṃ tu sarvanāḍīnāmūrddhaṃ gati vivodhakaḥ |
triveṇī saṃgamaṃ dhatte kedāraṃ prāpayenmanāḥ || 24 ||

rūpalāvaṇyasaṃpannā yathā strī puruṣaṃ vinā |
mahāmudrā mahāvaṃdhau niḥphalau vidhivarjitau || 25 ||

atha mahāvedhaḥ ||

mahāvaṃdha sthito yogī kṛtvā pūrakamekadhīḥ |
vāyūnāṃgati māvṛtya nibhaṃtaṃ kaṇṭhamudrayā || 26 ||

nyasta hasta yugo bhūmau prāṇaṃ saṃtāḍayecchanaiḥ |
jaṃghā dvayaṃ samākṛṣya vāyuḥ sphurati satvaraṃ || 27 ||

somasūryāgni saṃvaṃdhā jāyate cāmṛtāyavai |
mṛtāvasthā samutpannā tato vāyuṃ virecayet || 28 ||

mahāvedhā samabhyasya mahāsiddhi pradāyakaḥ |
valīpalita vedhaghnaḥ kathyate sādhakottamaiḥ || 29 ||

vaṃdhatrayaṃ mahāguhyaṃ jarāmṛtyu vināśanaṃ |
vahni vṛddhikaraṃ ciṃtadaṇimādiśunapradaṃ || 30 ||

aṣṭadhā kriyate caiva yāmaṃ yāmaṃ dine dine |
puṇyasaṃbhārasaṃbhāvi pāpaughabhiduraṃ tathā || 31 ||

samyak śikṣāvatāmeva svalpaṃ prathamasādhanaṃ |
vahnistrīpatha sevānāṃmādau varjana mācaret || 32 ||

atha khecarī || 

chedanaṃ cālanaṃ dohaiḥ kalā krameṇa varddhayet | 
tāvadyāvat bhrūmadhyaṃ rasanāspṛśati khecarī || 33 ||

siddhiḥ kapāle kuhare jihvā praviṣṭā viparītagā |
bhruvoraṃtargatā dṛṣṭirmudrā bhavati khecarī || 34 ||

39a)

kalā parāṅmukhī nītvā kṣaṇārdhaṃ yadi tiṣṭhati |
kṣaṇena mucyate vyādhi jarāmṛtyu bharādikaiḥ || 35 ||

na rogo maraṇaṃ tasyā na nidrā na kṣudhā tṛṣā |
na ca mūrchā bhavet tasya yo mudrāvetti khecarī || 36 ||

pīḍyatena sarogeṇa lipyatena sakarmaṇā |
vādhyatena sakālena yasya mudrāsti khecarī || 37 ||

cittaṃ carati khe yasya jihvā carati khe gatā |
tenaiṣā khecarī nāma mudrāsiddhairnamaskṛtā || 38 ||

khecaryā mudritaṃ yena vivaraṃ laṃvikordhataḥ |
na tasya kṣarate viṃduḥ kāminyā śleṣitasya ca || 39 ||

calitopi yadā viṃduḥ saṃprāpto yonimaṃḍalaṃ |
nayedūrdhvaṃ haṭhācchaktyā nivaddhe yoni mudrayā || 40 ||

ūrdhvaṃ jihvā sthiro bhūtvā somapānaṃ karoti yaḥ |
māsārdheṇa na saṃdeho mṛtyuṃ jayati yogavit || 41 ||

nityaṃ somakalpapūrṇe śarīraṃ yasya yoginaḥ |
takṣakenāpi daṣṭasya viṣaṃ tasya na sarpati || 42 ||

iṃdhanāni tathā vahnistailavartī ca dīpakaṃ |
tathā somakalāpūrṇaṃ dehī dehaṃ na muṃcati || 43 ||

gomāṃsaṃ bhakṣayedyogī pivedamaruvāriṇīṃ |
kulīnaṃ tamahaṃmanye tvitare kulaghātakaḥ || 44 ||

gośabdenoditā jihvā tatpraveśo hi tāluni |
gomāṃsa bhakṣaṇaṃ tattu mahāpātaka nāśanaṃ || 45 ||

jihvāpraveśasaṃbhūtā vahninotpāditā khalu |
caṃdrādravati yaḥ sāraḥ sasyādamaravāruṇī || 46 ||

ūrddhaṃ ṣoḍaśa padmapatra galitaṃ prāṇādavāptaṃ haṭhādūrdhvaṃse 
rasanāniyamya vivare śaktiṃ parāṃ ciṃtayan || 47 ||

ukta lolakalāṃjala vimalaṃ dhārāmṛtayaḥ pivet |
nirdoṣaḥ samṛṇālakomalatanuryogī ciraṃ jīvati || 48 ||

39b)

cuṃvutī yadi laṃvikāgramaniśaṃ jihvārasaspaṃdanī sakṣārākaṭukāmla 
dugdhasadṛśāmadhvājya tulyātha vā |
vyādhīnāṃ haraṇaṃ jarāmaraṇaṃ śāstrādgamodgīraṇaṃ tasya 
syādamaratvamaṣṭaguṇitaṃ siddhāṃgaṇākarṣaṇaṃ || 48 ||

ekaṃ sṛṣṭamayaṃ vījamekā mudrā ca khecarī |
eko devo nirālaṃvo ekāvasthā manonmanī || 49 ||

pātāle yadviśati sukhiraṃ meru mūle yadasti taddṛccaitat pravadati 
sudhīstanmukhaṃ nimnagānāṃ |
caṃdrāsāraḥ sravati vapuṣastena mṛtyurnnarāṇāṃ 
tadvadhnīyāsukaraṇamathonānyathākāya siddhiḥ || 50 ||

atha mūlavaṃdhāḥ ||

pārṣṇibhāgena saṃpīḍya yonimākuṃcaye dṛḍhaṃ |
apānamūrdhvamākṛṣya mūlavaṃdho nigadyate || 51 ||

adhogatimapānaṃ vai ūrdhvagaṃ kurute valāt |
ākuṃcanena taṃ prāhurmūlavaṃdhaṃ ca yoginaḥ || 52 ||

gudaṃ pārṣṇyā tu saṃpīḍya vāyumākuṃcayed valāt |
vāraṃvāraṃ yathā cordhvaṃ samoyāti samīraṇaḥ || 53 ||

prāṇāpānau nādaviṃdū mūlavaṃdhena caikatāṃ |
gatvā yogasya saṃsiddhaṃ gacchato nātra saṃśayaḥ || 54 ||

apāṇa prāṇayoraikyaṃ kṣaye mūtrapurīṣayoḥ |
yuvā bhavati vṛddhopi satataṃ mūlavandhanāt || 55 ||

apāne cārdhagoyāte prayāte vahnimaṃḍale |
tadānala sikhaṃ dīrghāvardhate vāyunāhatā || 56 ||

tatau yātau vahnā pāṇauprāṇāmuṣṇāti rūpakaṃ |
tenātyaṃta pradīptaśca jvalano dehagastathā || 57

tena kuṃḍalinī suptā saṃtaptā saṃpravudhyate |
daṃḍāhatā bhujagīvaniḥśvasya ṛtujā vrajet || 58 ||

40a)

vilaṃ praviṣṭe pavane brahmanāḍyaṃtare vrajet |
tasmānnityaṃ mūlavaṃdhaḥ kartavyo yogibhiḥ sadā || 59 ||

athoḍiyāṇavaṃdhaḥ ||

vaddho yena suṣumṇāyāṃ prāṇastaddīyate yataḥ |
tasmāduḍyāpākākhyoyaṃ yogibhiḥ samudāhṛtaḥ || 60 ||

uḍyānaṃ kurute yasmādaviśrāṃto mahākhagaḥ |
uḍyāṇaṃ tu tadeva syāt tatra vaṃdhobhidhīyate || 61 ||

udare paścimāṃtānaṃ nābherūrdhvaṃ tu kārayet |
uḍḍiyāṇo hyayaṃ vaṃdho mṛtyumātaṃga kesarī || 62 ||

uḍḍiyāṇaṃ tu sahajaṃ guruṇā kathitaṃ sadā |
abhyasedaniśaṃ yogī vṛddhopi taruṇo bhavet || 63 ||

nābherūrdhvamadhaścāpi tānaṃ kuryāt prayatnataḥ |
ṣaṇmāsābhyāsayogeṇa jarāmṛtyuṃ na saṃśayaḥ || 64 ||

sati vajrāsanā pādau karābhyāṃ dhāraye dṛḍhaṃ |
gulphadeśa samīpe ca kaṃpaṃ tatra prapīḍyate || 65 ||

paścimaṃtāna mudare kārayeddhṛdaye gale |
śanaiḥ śanairyathā prāṇaḥ skaṃdhasaṃdhi na gacchati || 66 ||

sarveṣāmeva vaṃdhānāṃ uttamo hyuḍiyāṇakaḥ |
uḍiyāṇe kṛte vaṃdhe muktiḥ svābhāvikīṃ bhavet || 67 ||

atha jālāṃdharabaṃdhaḥ ||

kaṃṭhamākuṃcya hṛdaye sthāpayeccivukaṃ dṛḍhaṃ |
vaṃdho jālāṃdharākhyoyaṃ mṛtyormṛtyuparo mataḥ || 68 ||

vadhnāti hi śirājālamadhojāti nabho jalaṃ |
tato jālādhano vaṃdhaḥ kaṃṭha duḥkhaughanāśanaṃ || 69 ||

jālaṃdhare kṛte vaṃdhe kaṃṭhasaṃkoca lakṣaṇe |
na pīyūṣaṃ pacatyagnau na ca vāyuḥ pradhāvati || 70 ||

kaṃṭhasaṃkocane naivaddenāḍyau staṃbhaye dṛḍhaṃ |
madhya cakramidaṃ jñeyaṃ ṣoḍaśādhāravaṃdhanaṃ || 71 ||

vaṃdhatrayamidaṃ śreṣṭa mahāsiddhairniṣevitaṃ | 
sarveṣāṃ yogataṃtrāṇāṃ sādhanaṃ yogināṃ viduḥ || 72 ||

adhasthā kuṃcane naiva kaṃṭhasaṃkocanena ca |

40b)

madhye paścimatāne syāt prāṇaraṃdhre brahmaraṃdhragaḥ || 73 ||

mūlasthānaṃ samākuṃcya uḍiyāṇaṃ tu kārayet |
iḍā ca piṃgalā vadhvā vāhayet paścimaṃ payaṃ || 74 ||

anenaiva vidhānena prayāti pavanolayaṃ |
tato na jāyate mṛtyurjarārogādikaṃ tathā || 75 ||

atha viparīta lakṣaṇaṃ ||

ūrdhvanābhiradhastā tu rūrddhabhānuradhaḥ śaśī |
karaṇaṃ viparītākhyaṃ guruvākyena labhyate || 76 ||

nityamabhyāsa yuktena jaṭharāgni vivardhanaṃ |
āhāro vahulastasya saṃpādyaḥ sādhakasya tu || 77 ||

alpāhāre bhavedagni dehaṃ bhavati tatkṣaṇāt |
adhaḥ śiraścorddhapādaḥ kṣaṇaṃ syāt prathame dine || 78 ||

kṣaṇāt tu kiṃcidadhikaṃmabhyasecca dine dine |
balitaṃ palitaṃ caiva ṣaṇmāsārdhena duṣyate || 79 ||

yāmamātraṃ tu yo nityaṃmabhyaset sa tu kālajit |

athavajjolī ||

svecchayā vartamānopi yogoktairniyamairvinā || 80 ||

vajjolīṃyobhi jānāti sa yogī siddhibhājanaṃ |
tatra vastu dvayaṃ manye durlabhaṃ yasya kasyacit || 81 ||

kṣīramekaṃ dvitīyaṃ tu nārī ca vaśavartinī |
mohanairna śanaiḥ samyagūrdhvā kuṃcanamabhyaset || 82 ||

puruṣo vātha nārī vā vajjālī siddhimāpnuyāt |
yatnataḥ śarajālena phūtkāraṃ kajjakaṃdharaṃ || 83 ||

śanaiḥ śanaiḥ prakurvīta vāyuḥ saṃcārakāraṇāt |
cakritanijaviṃduṃ ca ūrdhvamākṛṣya rakṣayet || 84 ||

evaṃ sarakṣayedviṃduṃ mṛtyuṃ jayati yogavit |
maraṇaṃ viṃdupātena jīvitaṃ viṃdudhāraṇāt || 85 ||

sugaṃdhiryogino deho jāyate viṃdudhāraṇāt |
sugaṃdhiryogino deho jāyate viṃdudhāraṇāt || 86 ||

41a)

yāvadviṃdusthiro dehe tāvanmṛtyu bhayaṃ kutaḥ |
cittāyattaṃ nṛṇāṃ śukraṃ śukrāyattaṃ ca jīvati || 86 ||

tasmācchukraṃ manaścaiva rakṣaṇīyaṃ prayatnataḥ |
ṛtumatyārajopyevaṃ nijaviṃduṃ ca rakṣayet || 87 ||

meḍhreṇākarṣayedūrdhva samyagabhyāsayogataḥ |
ayaṃ yogaḥ puṇyavatāṃ dhanyānāṃ tatvaśālināṃ || 88 ||

nirmatsarāṇāṃ siddheta na tu matsara śālināṃ |
sahajoliśrāmarolirvajjālpā eva vodhataḥ || 89 ||

jale bhasma vinikṣipya dagdhagomaya saṃbhavaṃ |
vajjolīmehanādūrdhvaṃ strīpuṃso svāṃga lepanaṃ || 90 ||

āsīnayoḥ sukhe naiva muktavyāparayo kṣaṇaṃ |
sahajauliriyaṃ proktā śraddhayā yogibhiḥ sadā || 91 ||

ayaṃ śubhakaro yogo bhoge muktepi muktidaḥ |
puṃso viṃdu samākuṃcya samyagabhyāsa pāṭavān || 92 ||

yadi nārī rajo rakṣedvajjolyā sahayoginī || 93 ||

tasyāḥ kiṃcidrajonāśaṃ na gacchaṃti na saṃśayaḥ |
tasyāḥ śarīre nādastu viṃdunāmava gacchati || 94 ||

sa viṃdustadrajaścaiva ekībhūyau svadehayau |
vajjolyābhyāsa yogena sarvasiddhiṃ prakurvate || 96 ||

atītānāgataṃ vetti khecarī ca prajāyate |
dehasiddhiṃ ca labhate vajjolyābhyāsayogataḥ || 96 ||

tasmādayaṃ sādhakāya bhoge muktepi suktidaḥ |
tasmāt puṇya vatāmeva hyayaṃ yogaḥ prasidhyati || 97 ||

atha śakticālanaṃ ||

kuṭilāṃgī kuḍalinī bhujaṃgī śaktirīśvarī |
kuṃḍalyaruṃdhatī hyeva śabdāparyāya vācakāḥ || 98 ||

udghāṭayet kapāṭaṃ tu yathā kuṃcikayā haṭhāt |
kuṃḍalinyā tathā yogī mokṣadvāraṃ vibhedaye || 99 ||

41b)

yena mārgeṇa gaṃtavyaṃ brahmadvāranirāmayaṃ |
mukhenācchādyate dvāraṃ prasuptā parameśvarī || 100 ||

kuṃḍordhvaṃ kuṃḍalī śaktiraṣṭhayā kuṃḍalī kṛtā |
vaṃdhanā yaṃtramūḍhānāṃ yogināṃ mokṣadāyikā || 101 ||

kuṃḍalī kuṭilākārā sarpivat parivartitā |
sā śaktiścālitā yena samukto nātra saṃśayaḥ || 102 ||

gaṃgāyamunayormadhye vālaraṃḍā tapasvinī |
valātkāreṇa gṛhṇīyāt tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padāṃ || 103 ||

pucchaṃ pragṛhya bhujagī suptā muddhodhayedabhīḥ |
nidrāṃ vihāya sā ṛjvī urdhvamuttiṣṭhate haṭhāt || 104 ||

savyāsanasthasya phaṇavatī sāṃprataśca sāyaṃ praharārdhamātraṃ |
prasūrya sūryāt paridhāna yuktā pragṛhya nityaṃ paricālanīyā || 105 ||

vitasti pramitaṃ dairghe vistāraṃ caturaṃgulaṃ |
mṛdulaṃ dhavalaṃ proktaṃ ceṣṭatāṃvara lakṣaṇaṃ || 106 ||

bhānorākuṃcanaṃ kuryā kuṃḍalī cālayet tataḥ |
mṛtyucakra gatasyāpi tasya mṛtyubhayaṃ kutaḥ || 107 ||

nāsādakṣiṇamārgavāhi pavanā'tprāṇoti dīrghī kṛtaścaṃdrāṃbhaḥ 
paripūritā mṛtatanuḥ prāgghaṃṭikāyāḥ sadā ||
chaṃdakāle viśālavahni vaśagādrūraṃdhanāḍī gaṇātkāyaṃ kurute punarna 
vitaraṃ chinnadrumaskaṃdhavat || 108 ||

kuṃḍalī cālayitvā tu bhastrīṃ kuryād viśeṣataḥ |
evamabhyāsato nityaṃ yaminaḥ śaṃkate yamaḥ || 109 ||

tathābhyāsāt sūryabhedanamujjāpi cāpi śītalī |
evamabhyāsa yuktasya śaminoyamina kutaḥ || 110 ||

muhūrta dvaya paryaṃtaṃ nirbhayaścālanādasau |
ūrdhvamākṛṣyate kiṃcit suṣumnāgata kuṃḍalī || 111 ||

tena kuṃḍalinī tasyāḥ suṣumnāyāḥ samuddhṛtā |

42a)

jahāti tasmāt prāṇoyaṃ suṣumnāṃ vrajati svataḥ || 112 ||

tasmāt saṃcālayennityaṃ śaṃbhu garbhāmaruṃdhatīṃ |
yasmāt saṃcālenāśu yogī rogairvimucyate || 113 ||

yena saṃcālitā śaktiḥ sa yogī siddhibhājanaṃ |
kimatra vahunoktena kālaṃ jayati līlayā || 114 ||

brahmacarya vratasyainaṃ nityaṃ hitamitāśinaḥ |
maṃḍalāt dṛśyate siddhiḥ kuṃḍalyabhyāsayogataḥ || 115 ||

abhyāsaniḥsṛtāṃ cāṃdrī vibhūtyā sahamiśrayet |
tadvāreduttamāge tu divyadṛṣṭipradāyakaṃ || 116 ||

dvāsaptati sahasrāṇāṃ nāḍīnāṃ malaśodhanāṃ |
kutaḥ prakṣālanopāyaḥ kuṃḍalyābhyāsanā dṛte || 117 ||

iti śakticālanaṃ ||

iti mudrā daśaproktā hyādināthena śaṃbhunā |
karaṇe sarvasiddhīnāmekaikāpi kṣamaiva sā || 118 ||

rājayogaṃ vinā pṛthvī rājayogaṃ vināniśi |
rājayogaṃ vinā mudrā vicitrāpi na rājate || 119 ||

māsatobhyasanaṃ sarva mano yuktaṃ samācaret |
itasrana ca kartavyā manovṛttirmaṇīṣiṇā || 120 ||

khilāpi madhyamānāḍī dṛḍhābhyāsena yoginā |
āsanaṃ prāṇasaṃyāma mudrābhiḥ sakalā bhavet || 121 ||

abhyāseṣu vinidrāṇāṃ manudbhūtasamādiṣu |
rudrāṇī vā parāmudrābhadrāṃ siddhiṃ prayacchati || 122 ||

upadeśaṃ hi mudrāṇāṃ yo datte sāṃpradāyikaṃ |
sa eva suguruḥ svāmī sākṣādīśvara eva saḥ || 123 ||

tasya vākya paromudrāṃ yo bhyasyati samīhitaḥ |
aṇimādi guṇaiḥ soyaṃ jāyate kālavaṃcakaḥ || 124 ||

iti svātmāvaṃdaciṃtāmaṇināsvātmārāmayogīndraviracitāyāṃ 
haṭhapradīpikāyāṃ mudrālakṣaṇaṃ nāma tṛtīya upadeśaḥ ||


42b)

namaḥ śivāya gurave nādaviṃdu layātmane |
niraṃjanaṃ padaṃ yāṃti nityaṃ yatra parāyaṇāḥ || 1 ||

iṃdriyāṇāṃ manonātha manonāthastu mārutaḥ |
mārutasya layo nāthastaṃ nātha mahamāśraye || 2 ||

praṇaṣṭaśca sita śvāsa pradhvasto līna vigrahaḥ |
niśceṣṭo nirvikāraśca layo jayati yogināṃ || 3 ||

ucchinna sarvasaṃkalpo niḥśeṣagata ceṣṭitaḥ |
svāvargalabhyaye jñāpi jīvatyā caṃdratārakaṃ || 4 ||

yatra dṛṣṭirlayastatra bhūtendriya viviktayā |
vedaśāstrapurāṇāni sāmānya gaṇikā iva || 5 ||

ekaiva śāṃbhavī mudrā gopyākulavadhūriva |
aṃtarlakṣaṃ vahirdṛṣṭirnimeṣonmeṣavarjitā || 6 ||

eṣā sā śāṃbhavī mudrā sarvataṃtreṣu varjitā |

aṃtarlakṣavilīna cittapavano yogī yadā vartate dṛṣṭyā ni ścala tārayā 
vahiradhaḥ paśyenna paśye tadā |
mudreyaṃ khalu khecarī bhavati yā prāpyā prasādādguroḥ śūnyāśūnya 
vivarjitaṃ sphurati yat tatvaṃ padaṃ śāṃbhavaṃ || 7 ||

sā bhavyā api khecaryā avagamya ca bhidyate |
bhinne ca sravate caṃdrādamṛtaṃ divyarūpiṇaḥ || 8 ||

tatsarvaṃ grasate sūryastena piṃḍo jarāyutaḥ |
tatrāsti karaṇaṃ divyaṃ sūryasya paripaṃthi ca || 9 ||

gurūpadeśato jñeyaṃ na tu śāstrārtha koṭibhiḥ |
idaṃ sarvātmanā śiṣyai rūpāsīta tato guruṃ || 10 ||

śrī ādināthena tu sārdhakoṭilayaprakārāḥ kathitā jayaṃti |
nādānusaṃdhānakamekamevamanyāmahemukhyatamaṃ layānāṃ || 11 ||

muktāsane sthito yogī mudrāṃ saṃdhāya śāṃbhavīṃ |
śṛṇuyāṃ dakṣiṇe karṇe nādamaṃtasthamekadhīḥ || 12 ||

43a)

kāṣṭha pravartito vahni kāṣṭhena sahasāmyati |
nāda prakartinaṃ cittaṃ nādena saha sāmyati || 13 ||

vismṛtya sakalaṃ vādyaṃ nāde dugdhāṃvuvanmanaḥ |
ekībhūyādatha saha cidākāśena līyate || 14 ||

udāsīna paro bhūyāt sadābhyāsena saṃyamī |
unmanīkaraṇaṃ sadyonāda evāvadhāryate || 15 ||

sarvaciṃtāṃ samutsṛjya sarvaceṣṭāṃ ca sarvadā |
nādasyaivānu saṃvaṃdhā dvidhā cittaṃ pralīyate || 16 ||

āraṃbhaśca ghaṭaściava yathā paricayastathā |
niṣpattiḥ sarvayogeṣu yogāvasthā bhavaṃtitāḥ || 17 ||

brahmagraṃthau bhaved bheda svānaṃdaḥ śūnyasaṃbhavaḥ |
vicitra tatkṣaṇādehe sarvataḥ śrūyate dhvaniḥ || 18 ||

divyadeha svatejasvī divyagaṃdhastvarogavān |
saṃpūrṇe hṛdayaṃ śūnye tvāraṃbho yogino bhavet || 19 ||

atha ghaṭāvasthā ||

dvitīyāyāṃ ghaṭī kṛtya vāyurbhavati madhyagaḥ |
dṛḍhāsano bhavedyogī jñānādeva samestathā || 20 ||

viṣṇugraṃthestadā bhedāt paramānaṃdasūcakaḥ |
atiśūnye mardalasya bherīśabdastathā bhavet || 21 ||

tṛtīyāyāṃ tato bhūtvā siṃhasyeva mahādhvaniḥ |
mahāśūnyaṃ tadā yāti sarvasiddhi samāśrayaḥ || 22 ||

cittānaṃdastathājajñe sahajānaṃdasaṃbhavaḥ |
sukhaduḥkha jarāmṛtyu kṣudhānidrā vivarjitaḥ || 23 ||

rudragraṃthi tato bhitvā sarvaṃ pīḍyagatānilaḥ |

atha niṣpatsavasthā ||

niṣpattau vegataḥ śabdo vaṃśikadhvanivad bhavet |
ekabhūtaṃ tadā cittaṃ rājayogābhidhānakaṃ || 24 ||

sṛṣṭisaṃhārakartāsau yogīśvarasamo bhavet |

43b)

astu vāmastu vā śakti gātre vā khaṃḍitaṃ mahat || 25 ||

laye mṛtamaye saukhyaṃ rājayogādavāpyate |
rājayogamajānaṃtaḥ kevalaṃ haṭhakarmaṇāḥ |
sevakān karṣakān manye prayāse phalavarjitān || 26 ||

tatvaṃ vīja haṭhakṣetramaudāsīnyaṃ jalaṃ tathā |
unmanī kalpalatikā sadya eva bhaviṣyati || 27 ||

rājayogaḥ samādhiśca conmanī ca manonmanī |
amaraścāpi cādvaitaṃ nirālaṃvaṃ niraṃjanaṃ || 28 ||

amanasko manastatvaṃ śūnyaśūnyaṃ paraṃ padaṃ |
jīvanmuktiśca sahajaṃ turīyaṃ tveka vācakaṃ || 29 ||

unmanya vyāptaye śīghramubhau dvau mama sammatau |
tatvaṃ paraṃ tathā śakhyaṃ nādopāsanameva ca || 29 ||

sarvaciṃtāṃ parityajya sāvadhānena cetasā |
nāda eka susaṃdhyeyo yogasāmrājyamicchatā || 30 ||

karṇepidhātha mūle ca yaḥ śṛṇoti dhvaniṃ muniḥ |
tatra cittaṃ sthiraṃ kuryād yāvasthira padaṃ vrajet || 31 ||

abhyasyamāno nādoyaṃ vāhyamāvṛṇāte dhvaniṃ |
tatrāsu prathamābhyāse nādo nānāvidho mahān || 32 ||

vardhamāne tatobhyāse śrūyate sūkṣmasūkṣmakaḥ |
yatra yatrāpi nāde calagati prathamaṃ manaḥ || 33 ||

tatraiva yaḥ sthiro bhūtvā tena sārdhaṃ vilīyate |
manonmatta gajendrasya viśramodyānacāraṇaḥ || 34 ||

niyāmanaḥ prasaṃvaddhe ninādo niśitāṃ kuśaḥ |
śravaṇamukha nayananāsā nirodhane naiva kartavyaṃ || 35 ||

śuddhau suṣumnāsaraṇau sphuṭamamalaḥ śrūyate vādaḥ |
jñātvā suṣumnā saṃbhedaṃ kṛtvā vāyuṃ ca madhyagaṃ || 36 ||

kṛtvā sā caindavasthāne prāṇaraṃdhre niyojayet |

44a)

tathā vasiṣṭavacanaṃ || 36 ||

iḍāyā piṃgalāyāṃ ca carataścaṃdra bhāskarau |
caṃdrastāmasa ityuktaḥ sūryo rājasa ucyate || 37 ||

sarve haṭhalayopāyā rājayogasya siddhaye |
rājayoga samārūḍhaḥ puruṣaḥ kālapaṃcakaḥ || 38 ||

iti śrīsakalaśāstrasamuccaye svātmārāmayogīndraviracitāyāṃ 
haṭhapradīpikāyāṃ caturthaḥ upadeśaḥ samāptaḥ || 


śrīrāmāya namaḥ || 

śrīmatkāmapīṭhakamalāyai namaḥ || 

śrītripurāṃtaka mahārudra sakalamaṃtradīkṣādīkṣaka kāmapīṭha gurave 
namaḥ || 

atha samyak pravakṣyāmi kāmākṣā śavarīritaṃ | 
śāvarītaṃtramatyarthaṃ sadyaḥpratyayakārakaṃ || 

kadāciddhimavat pārśve kārtikeya gaveṣaṇā |
śavarīrūpamāsthāya gaudhitkinnamānasā ||

papracchaśaṃbhuṃ sarveśa sarvāgama phalapradaṃ ||

gauryuvāca ||

devasaṃti samastāni taṃtrāṇi jagatītale |
paurāṇavaidikānyanyānyatulā nirasātale ||

siddhāni yakṣajānyāśu paiśācāni parīṃcihi |
yakṣiṇī paṭalānpatrasauraṃgāṇa carāṇi vai ||

traipurānyatha śaivāni cāṃḍāni cuvukāni ca |
kaulānibhillasaṃjñāni kairātānpathapaṃci ca ||

paṃcārātrāṇi parvāṇi sarvāṇi vihitāni ca |
pihitāni parāṃcīṇi dharmaguptāni yānyapi ||

maṃtra yaṃtrādi saṃbhūta rasauṣadhaśatānyapi |
tāni sarvāṇi giriśa siddhaśāvaramityapi ||

phalaṃti na phalaṃtyāśu tenāviśvāsitānyapi |
kimatra kāraṇaṃ deva tadvrūhi hyaparaṃ ca me ||

jaṃtumātraka taṃ sadyaḥ phalatyāśu mahītale |
jñānināṃ jñāninā vāpi adhikāra vivarjitā || 

44b)

kṛtamātraṃ phale kṛdyantu yanmanasyāgataṃ hi tat |
yena ca prāptamatulaṃ sasiddho nātra saṃśayaḥ || 

brahmakṣatriyaviṭśūdrā ye cānyepyanyajātijāḥ |
adhikāriṇaste sarve sadyaḥ phala vibhūṣitāḥ ||

etadvrūhi mahādeva karuṇā śatasāgara |
tvat prasādādahaṃ sadyaḥ prāpnuyāṃ tadanuttamaṃ || 

śaṃbhuruvāca ||

sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ mahādevi maṃtrayaṃtra rahasyakaṃ |
idaṃ kasyāpi nākhyeyaṃ tathāpi puratastava ||

bhavāni vallabhāsitvaṃ tacchṛṇuṣva varānane |
paṃcataṃtrāṇi sarvāṇi mayāsaṃmathya vai purā ||

niḥsārāṇi kṛtātpāśu na phalaṃti tatastataḥ |
siddhaśāvarasaṃjñaṃ tu vīrabhadrasvarūpiṇā ||

mayā sadagdhavījaṃ tannaphalaṃtyeva kasyacit |
mohārthaṃ racitaṃ devi tattu pāṣaṇḍavardhanaṃ ||

atotraiva phalatyeva tathā kaulāgamādikaṃ |
dakṣeṇa dhūrtarūpeṇa siddhaśāvarasaṃjñakaṃ || 

prayuṃjitaṃ purā tena kṣobhitaṃ jagatītatrayaṃ |
ato mayā mahādevi tasya śaktiḥ praṇāśitā ||

yo yogītyakte ho?hādi viṣayastastha kevalaṃ |
kadācit sidhyatetovā svādhikāra vidūṣitaṃ ||

abhyarhita tamaṃtubhyaṃ taṃtraṃ sarvaphalapradaṃ |
kāmarūpābhidhaṃ tatra kāmakalpavivardhanaṃ ||

tvayāpyetadyadācīrṇaṃ bhaviṣyati varānane |
śavarī taṃtraṃ nāmāgrasaṃ bhaviṣyati ||

devamānuṣabhāṣābhirbhūyāṃso manavastviha |
yakṣarākṣasapaiśāca bhāṣābhirmanavastathā ||

nānādeśodbhavābhāṣā tu lomavilomajā |
tathā kālasya niyamaḥ sūkṣmakālasya niścayaḥ ||

grahayogādi niyamastathauṣadhavidhi niścitiḥ |
etānyatra hi mukhyāni dhyānādi niyamo na hi ||

(dakṣiṇakarṇaśabdena akāraḥ tamārabhya vāmakarṇaśabdena kṣakāraḥ 
tatparyaṃtaṃ japet | punaḥ pratilomavilomenetyādi 
graṃthāṃtaroktarotyākṣamāletyā kṛtamiti |)

45a)

nāpinyā sa vidhiḥ prokto na prāṇasya pratiṣṭhitāḥ |
bhūtaśuddhirna vāhyaṃta mātṛkānyā sa iṣyate ||

akṣamālāvidhānena japaḥ kāryastvayānaghe |
dhyānaṃ vidhāya purato devatāyāstu dakṣiṇāt ||

karṇādādi visargaḥ syād viṃdunā mātṛkākṣaraṃ |
utrā paṃcamanuṃ paścāt punastaṃ mātṛkākṣaraṃ ||

evamagre tato vāma karṇāṃtaṃ prajapenmanuṃ |
evaṃ tu prāti lomena dakṣiṇaśravaṇāvadhi ||

nameruṃ laṃghayet tatra merurdeva śiromataḥ |
ādikṣāṃtaṃ iyaṃ mālā vijñeyā hyakṣamālikā ||

ayaṃ dhyānavidhiḥ proktaḥ sadyo mānasajinmataḥ |
kāmarūpākhya deśe tu kāmākṣā yatra devatā ||

kāmaśailosti tatrāsau kāmapīṭhamiti smṛtaḥ |
tatra saṃlekhya maṃtraṃ hi yatropari yathākramaṃ ||

guruṇā vāvanīyaḥ sasvayaṃ paścāt paṭhenmanuṃ |
gurorabhāve tasyaiva mūle śailasya parvaṇi ||

likhitvā prapaṭhenmaṃtraṃ kāmaṃ pīṭhaṃ gururmataḥ |
atha vā yogīśaile dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśi dhruvaṃ ||

yogāṃ vā yatra devī sā likhitvā prapaṭhenmanuṃ |
jvālāmukhī samīpe vā hiṃgulājasamīpataḥ ||

likhitvā prapaṭhenmaṃtraṃ nānyathaiṣā prasīdati |
mukhyatastrī samīpe hi kāmapīṭhermanorgrahaḥ ||

atrakāṃ āṃkṣamāleti yaduktaṃ tasyāyamathaḥ |
paṃcāśadakṣareṣu akāraṃ prathamuccāryasānusvāraṃ tataḥ ||

śāvarī taṃtra sthitaṃ maṃtraṃ punaḥ aṃkāra sapraṇavaṃ evaṃ dhyānāt 
paraḥ samupasthāpitāyā devatāyā dakṣiṇa śravaṇamārabhya vāma 
śravaṇaparyaṃtaṃ madhye teṣu te svaṃgeṣu varṇān sthāpayan 
kṣakāraparyaṃtaṃ punaḥ vāmaśravaṇāt kṣakāramārabhya aṃkārāṃtaṃ 
dakṣiṇa śravaṇāṃtaṃ iyamakṣamālā prasiddhā tadakṣāṇāṃ sphaṭikādi 
maṇīnāṃ mālā || 

45b)

ayaṃ dhyānavidhiḥ manaḥ samādhi mahān anena mano japo bhavati | devatā ca 
sanmukhā sadyaḥ prasīdati | atra mukhyataḥ kāmarūpadeśe kāmaśaila 
rūpakāmākṣapīṭhe guruṇā mukhyatastrīrūpeṇa puruṣarūpeṇa vā || 

likhitvā yaṃtro parimanuḥ sthāpanīyaḥ guruḥ paṭhati prathamataḥ paścāt 
śiṣyaḥ paṭhat || 

ayaṃ maṃtrasyopadeśavidhiḥ || 

athavā dakṣiṇadeśe yogāṃ vā nagare yogaśaile pūrvavallikhitvā maṃtro 
grāhyaḥ || athavā nagarakoṭe vā hiṃgulājanagare tattadevatā saṃnidhau maṃtro 
grāhyaḥ || 

mukhyataḥ kāmarūpavidhiḥ || 

tatra tathā lokānāṃ siddhayopyanubhūyaṃte || iti śāvarī taṃtramaṃtrāṇāṃ 
grahaṇopāyaḥ || tatrādau maṃtrāṇāṃ saṃgraho vakṣyate || sāmānyataḥ 
sarvamaṃtraśāstreṣu tattanmaṃtrāṇāṃ ṣaḍayogā uktā saṃti 
tattadanuṣṭhāneṣu dakṣiṇapitaramārgavidhānena 
cakramaṃtramudrānirūpabhrameṇa bhrāmitāḥ sādhakābhraṃśitāśca 
tadvadidaṃ na bhavati saphalaṃ ca tatkṣaṇātkālakarmakriyājñānavaśata iti 
nirūpyate || 

bhūyāṃsaḥ saṃti kūṭāni maṃtrāṇāṃ bhraṃśasādhanaṃ |
jātibhraṃśādi hetu tvāt savyetara vidhānataḥ || 

maṃtramudrā prayogādi cakramaṃḍalavibhramaiḥ |
tathopahārastapanaṃ duṣṭadravyādibhirdhruvaṃ ||

brahmakṣatriyaviṭśūdra jāti sādhāraṇa kramāt |
phalabhrama pravṛttāśca kāmāṃdhāmati mohitāḥ ||

iṃdriyādi viduṣṭāśca svecchācāravimohitāḥ |
svapravṛtti pravṛttāśca kevalaṃ pāpa hetavaḥ ||

tenedaṃ dūṣitaṃ devi prājamaṃtrāgamādikaṃ |

46a)

tatotiriktametaddhi sadyaḥ pratyayasuṃdaraṃ ||

pravakṣye maṃtrajātaṃ hi deśakālādi nirṇayāt |
nātra kiṃcidvidhi phalaṃ navājāti viguṃṭhanaṃ ||

duṣṭadravyādibhirnnāpi navāmudrādibhirvidhiḥ |

tatrādāvanukramaṇikā ||

śāṃbhavī paṭalaṃ tatrādau kālikā paṭalaṃ tataḥ |
durgāyāḥ paṭalaṃ paścān maheśī paṭalaṃ tatoṃ ||

bhairavī paṭalaṃ paścāt tripurāpaṭalaṃ tato |
viṃdhyajāpaṭalaṃ paścād vanajā paṭalaṃ tataḥ ||

aiṃdavī paṭalaṃ paścād bhānavī paṭalaṃ tato |
hemaṃtī paṭalaṃ paścāddhemajā paṭalaṃ tataḥ ||

kāminī paṭalaṃ paścāt kāṃtajā paṭalaṃ tataḥ |
kāśmīrī paṭalaṃ paścāt kaṃvujā paṭalaṃ tathā ||

sukeśī paṭalaṃ paścāt saiṃdhavī paṭalaṃ tataḥ |
sākṣiṇī paṭalaṃ paścāt śatākṣī paṭalaṃ tataḥ ||

śatabhāryāstu paṭalaṃ tataḥ sevaṃtī paṭalaṃ tataḥ |
suśīlā paṭalaṃ paścāt śomanā paṭalaṃ tataḥ ||

karuṇā paṭalaṃ paścād varuṇā paṭalaṃ tataḥ |
dāruṇā paṭalaṃ paścād bhayajā paṭalaṃ tataḥ ||

ratnajā paṭalaṃ paścād ravijā paṭalaṃ tataḥ |
rākṣasī paṭalaṃ paścād ramaṇī paṭalaṃ tataḥ ||

vasujā paṭalaṃ paścādavanī paṭalaṃ tataḥ |
sāmudrī paṭalaṃ paścācchatākṣī paṭalaṃ tataḥ ||

sumukhī paṭalaṃ paścād duḥkhaghnī paṭalaṃ tataḥ |
upāṃga lalitā paṭalaṃ lalitā paṭalaṃ tataḥ ||

ṣaṭcatvāriṃśadetāni devīnāṃ paṭalāni vai |
adyāpi kāmarūpesmin kāmaśaile śirastale ||

khelaṃti mātṛkā śailā pratyahaṃ gamamāgamaiḥ |
tathā nagarakoṭesmin jvālā mukhyāśca sannidhau ||

khelati devatāḥ sarvā madhyāhnethadino?daye |
kṛta tretādi sarveṣu pureṣu prokta devatāḥ ||

46b)

ata eva hi kāmākhya śailosau devatāmayaḥ |
tatra pādanidhānena naronāśaṃ prayāti hi ||

sarvalokaistu madhyāhne madhyarātrau tathā dhruvaṃ |
sāyaṃdinodaye tadvadānaṃdabharanirbharaṃ ||

gītanādādi sakalaṃ śrūyatedhityakājanaiḥ |
tathā mātṛ māhāśaile ātreyāśramasaṃnidhau ||

āśvinasyaśite pakṣe divārātrāṃjanaiḥ samaṃ |
ānuśeyasya śikhare janayogibhramena hi ||

yoginīstrī bhrameṇaiva praṇītā pulināvadhiḥ |
tathā gahvarageheṣu nimitteṣu śilāśitaiḥ ||

śailasya hi purobhāge vaṭavṛkṣasya saṃnidhau |
dvāramekaṃ ca gehasya vidyate dakṣiṇāvadhi ||

tatra nṛtyaṃtitāḥ sarvā devatāstu dinodaye |
vālopyatha yuvā vṛddho mūrkhaḥ sujñothavā dhruvaṃ ||

paśyatu svecchayā devī nirmukto maṃtra vidyayā |
yogāṃ vā bhūdhare tadvat vasatantu samāgame ||

yoginī yogasaṃbhrāṃtyāpati brahmiṣṭa saṃbhramāt |
yena kenāpi liṃgeṇa saṃcaraṃtyāśu devatāḥ ||

madhumādhavapūrṇāyāṃ buddhi pūrvaṃ hi sādhakaḥ |
ārūḍhayogaśailāṃtaṃ tatra paśyati niścitaṃ ||

tathā ratnākara girau phālguṇe māsi niścitaṃ |
krīḍaṃti sakalā devyo yogivrāta bhrameṇa ca ||

tvaritā śailaśikhare nyagrodhāṃtara gahvarau |
sarvakāleṣu tā devyaḥ krīḍaṃtī janasaṃbhramaiḥ ||

kuṣṭī khajātidikāṇādivivacarācārādi saṃbhramaiḥ |
śailasya dakṣiṇe bhāge madhu vṛkṣasya saṃnidhau ||

yamunākhye mahātīrthe snātvā sādhakapuṃgavaḥ |
sucittamanasā tasmin striyaṃ kāṃcana paśyati ||

pana paśyati tatkālaṃ sarvadevamayīṃ śivāṃ |
saṃdhyāyāstānamākhyātaṃ yasya kasyāpi dehinaḥ || 

47a)

tasya śailasya nikaṭe dhārāgiririti smṛtaḥ |
mātṛkāḥ sakalā devyaḥ tatra saṃti dinaṃ dinaṃ ||

rāmatīrtha jale snātaḥ brahmakṣatriyaviṭ tathā |
dṛṣṭvā rāmeśvaraṃ devaṃ tathā kādaṃvinī jale ||

susnātaḥ kamalāṃ devīṃ pūjayitvā dinodaye |
abhrabhṛṃgāṃ mahādevīṃ bhṛṃgīvādana tatparā ||

kaṃthākhye mālāṃ lalitāṃ paśyatpāśu na saṃśayaḥ |
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā tatkṣaṇādetat prādau praṇamennaraḥ ||

saṃstaveccitrabhāṣābhiḥ prākṛtābhirathāpi vā |
sā tuṣṭā paramā devī grahītvā tatkare karaṃ ||

pūrvoktā devatāḥ sarvā darśayatyeva tatkṣaṇāt |
atra pūrvokta sthāneṣu devīnāṃ sākṣāt pratyayo darśitāḥ ||

* * cavavādyāpi pūrvokta vidhānena pratyayo valokanīyaḥ | asti 
dakṣiṇasyāṃdiśi viṃdhyāttasasvaśaila iti prasiddhaḥ | tadaṃtaḥ śikharaṃ 
mātṛkā śaila iti prasiddhaḥ maṃtre sthānaṃ tadābhyāsa pratyahaṃ kāmarūpa 
deśāṃtargata kāmaśailāvadhi devyaḥ krīḍaṃti | 
dṛśyaṃte cādyāpi | āśvinasitapakṣe ānūpasthale yoginī yogivyājena krīḍaṃti 
devatāḥ pratītā taṭāvadhi | tatra śailasya ekasmin deśe viśvakarma nirmitaṃ 
tataḥ śailagrahasya dakṣiṇadvāri | asti yakṣiṇī vaṭa ityeko vaṭavṛkṣastasyādhaḥ 
sthitvā sādhakasuṃdhi samayo | dinādauvādinamadhye mahāniśāyāṃ vā 
paśyati pūrvokta devagaṇaṃ | iti pratyayavidhiradyāpyasti | tatra yadā kadācit 
samaye eka eva yogī ātreya parvato paridṛṣṭaḥ sa ātreyaḥ | tannmaskṛtyābhi 
vādayet | sa evoktaṃ devatāgaṇaṃ darśayati || 

tathānyatrāpi nagara || 

koṭādau iti idaṃ pratyayārthaṃ gulyasaṃketa sthāna devīnāṃ proktaṃ |

47b)

etat kasyāpi nākhyeyaṃ || sādhakaḥ svapratyayārtha paśyediti asya 
śāvarītaṃtrasya gurudevavīśvāsavatāṃ phalapratyayārthaṃ devatā 
sākṣātkāra karaṇo pāyo darśitaḥ | kimuta maṃtrānuṣṭhānavatāṃ 
deśakālakarmakriyājñānavatāṃ sādhakānāṃ pratyayo bhaviṣyatyeveti citraṃ 
|| 

tatra śāṃbhavī paṭalavidhiḥ || 

śyāmā śivātha vālā ca vallabhāvetra vāsinī |
sphuṭākṣīharitālākṣī kuṭajākṣī ca kaṃkarī ||

śatākṣīdā netra kuṃḍīnāṃmadhuvāsinī |
meṭhyarāhaṃsagāhaṃsī vicitrāvidhipūrvakā ||

vidhātrī vainateyākṣī virūpāveṇuvāsinī |
kamalāramyāṃ paṃkajākṣī | payodinī pāṃḍavī pṛthumadhyāṃ ca pārthivā 
paṃkavāsinī || 

varāṇanā vidhiśreṣṭā vividhā vāmalocanā |
citrākṣī citrakaṇṭhī ca cihnagamyā trilocanā ||

nārīramyānidhi prāṃtānaṣṭaveṣāninādinī |
dvicatvāriṃśadetāstu śāṃbhavyaḥ saṃti śaktayaḥ ||

tara śyāmāmanuvidhiḥ ||

jyeṣṭhe māsi tva māyā hi nadītīre sunirmale |
tālītālavaneramye japet śyāmāṃ niśāvidhau ||

saṃdhyākāle tu saṃdhyājaṃ nityaṃ karma samāpyahi |
tātaścaṃpaka tailena nīlāṃvara parīvṛtaḥ ||

padmākṣamālā subhago nirbhayaḥ śāṃtamānasaḥ |
tālīmūlekhanityātu paṃcahastamitastataḥ ||

jānudadhnaṃsthalaṃ tasmin kīrakān nuraṣā?tayet |
bhūtāṃkuśasya śākhotthān pūrvādi kramatastataḥ ||

caturdikṣu ca catvāraḥ kīlakāḥ parikīrtitāḥ |
prathamo bhairavastaṃbhaḥ dvitīyaśchinnamastakaḥ ||

krūrakarmā tṛtīyaśca siddhidaśca caturthakaḥ |

pūrvakīlakanikhātana maṃtraḥ || 

kīlakabhairavastaṃbha bhairavastambhaya 2 bhaiṃ svāhā || 

dvitīya kīlakanikhānamaṃtraḥ || 

(tālaphalasyābhyaṃtarato majjāsarasaṃtiṣkāśā tasyāhuti parimitāt golakān 
kṛtveti bhāvaḥ ||)

48a)

citrāṃgacchinnamastabhayaṃ mā kuru 2 piśācān staṃbhaya 2 maṃ svāhā || 

tṛtīya | 

krūrakarmat krauryaṃ mā kuru 2 mā kuru cetaḥ samādhaya 2 krauṃ svāhā || 

caturthaṃ || 

siddhidabhayaṃ mā kuru siddhiṃ dehi 2 anukūlo bhava 2 sīṃdhaṃ svāhā || 

svamūrdhajaṃ samutpādya āveṣṭyaitāṃśca kīlakān | 
daśāvṛtyāmanuṃ japtvā ekaikaṃ pratiropayet || 

raktacaṃdanajaiḥ paścādakṣataiḥ pūjayet tratān |
japākusumagucchaiśca pūjayet kīlakānanu ||

purādhūpaṃ pradatvā tu nārikela jalaṃ tataḥ |
naivedyaṃ parikalpyāśu madhye kīlaṃ tataḥ param ||

suṣāsīnābhidhaṃ nīlaṃ nīlītarusamudbhavaṃ |
ropayet karavīrotthaiḥ kusumaiḥ pūjanaṃ tataḥ ||

kastūrī dhūpamādadyānnaivedyaṃ kadalīphalaiḥ |

maṃtraḥ || 

madhye kīlasukhāsanamamāsanaṃ sthiraya 2 cetaḥ samādhāya khaṃ svāhā || 

tataścopari viśenmaṃtrī tasmin bhūmitale sukhaṃ | 
śyāmāṃ japen mahādevī ayutaṃ śāṃtamānasaḥ ||

ādau dhyānaṃ prakurvīta pūrvokta vidhānā japaḥ |
tālāvanāṃtarekhellaka 2 tālī manoramāṃ ||

ālībhiḥ sahagītālī karaṇī śyāmikāṃ manuṃ |

iti dhyānaṃ ||

japāṃte homamādadhyāt tālī guggulu sugolakaiḥ |
daśāṃśena tataḥ pūrṇāṃ karpūrāgaruṇā saha ||

pradakṣiṇa trayaṃ kuryādetanmadhye vanāṃtare |
jhaṃ jhā mārutavat kaścijjāyate marmaraḥ svaraḥ ||

tasminupari tatkāle saṃpaśyet sādhakottamaḥ |
tato nādātmakaṃtyotirjāyate cukṣuṣo puraḥ ||

tanmadhye tu mahādevī śyāmā ṣoḍaśavārṣikī |
nīlāṃśuka parīdhānā kasturī vaṃdata priyā ||

svatanudyutibhisvacchamiṃdranīlaprabhābharaṃ |
nyakurvati nirātaṃkā nīlotpala vibhūṣaṇā ||

48b)

tāṃ namaskṛtya viśveśīṃ tuṣṭā bhava varānane |
ityuktvā maṃtriṇe tuṣṭā sā dadāti varatrayaṃ ||

paramānasavijñānaṃ vidyāṃ cāti manoramāṃ |
sauṃdaryaṃ ca kurūpasya jagatī mohana kṣamaṃ ||

maṃtraḥ || 

pravalatālatalavāsinī śyāmale śrīsiddhiṃ dehi svāhā || 

asyaiva pratirūpo hi kāmarūpeka bhāṣayā |
procyate tatra naivaiṣā yathāvidhivikalpatā ||

tālīvanāṃtare gatvā jyeṣṭā māyāṃ niśāṃtare |
japet śyāmāmanuṃ tatra sahasra dvitayaṃ kila ||

mahārātrau gate paścāt tālīpatra sudarbhakaiḥ |
homaṃ kuryāt sahasraṃ hi pūrṇātālā phalena ca ||

prasannāvaradā devī atītādi pravodhakaṃ |
anāgata pravodhaṃ ca maṃtriṇe pradadaṃti hi ||

maṃtraḥ || 

āgohānemānaha devo hu hu kali vilivikarivokarivohuṃ || 

atrāyaṃ kramavidhiḥ || 

jyeṣṭhe māsi amāyāṃ kṛta saṃdhyā karmānuṣṭhāno rātrau 
tālītālavanāṃtare gatvā nadītīre tālavanamadhyapradeśe tālamūle samīpa 
bhūmīṃ jānumātraṃ khanitvā itastataścaturasraṃ paṃcahastaṃ viśodhya 
paritaḥ mṛttikāṃ paridhī kṛtya tanmadhye bhūtāṃkuśavṛkṣaṃ 
śākhākṛtāṃtaścaturakīlakān pūrvokta maṃtraiḥ daśavāra paṭhitaiḥ 
pratyekaṃ pūrvādi krameṇa pratiropayet || taireva maṃtraiḥ pūjādi naivedyaṃ 
samarpaṇaṃ raktacaṃdanamiśritākṣataiḥ pūjā japaḥ śyāmā maṃtrasya 
pūrvoktākṣamālavidhānena | etasya pratirūpa maṃtraḥ || kāmarūpa bhāṣayā 
proktaḥ || 

tatra na kīlakādyāropavidhiḥ || 

japaḥ pūrvasmādviguṇaḥ phalasyātītānāgatajñānaṃ | tadevasya bhāṣā 
maṃtrasya pratilomyāt paṭhane phalāṃtaramāha || 

śyāmāmaṃtrastu pūrvoktaḥ kāmarūpaika bhāṣayā |
tasyaiva pratilomyena paṭhanādayutaṃ dhruvaṃ ||

tasmin kāle vane tasmin kapittha phalakāritaḥ |
homastato jagaddhātrī rasasiddhiṃ prayacchati || 

maṃtraḥ || 

huṃ vorikavorika cilivilika hu hu vo deha namā mohayo tuṃ | 

vaiparitye tu yo varṇaḥ ādigaḥ prāṃtagocaraḥ |

49a)

sānusvārāprācācopaḥ pratilomavidhistvayaṃ ||

tatra pratilomyena bhāṣā maṃtrapaṭhane pūrvānupūrvyāyaḥ | prathamo varṇaḥ 
saprāti lomye prāṃtago bhavati | sa ca viṃdunā saha paṭhanīyaḥ | etasyeva phalaṃ 
sasiddhiḥ | tetra kuṣṭakuṇapakhaṃjāndhādayaḥ siddhā bhavaṃti svāṃgāśca 
bhavaṃti || iti śyāmāvidhiḥ || 

atha śivāvidhiḥ || 

śrāvaṇemāsi cāṣṭamyāṃ kṛṣṇapakṣe niśāṃtare |
śatapatrīvanāṃtasthaḥ snātaḥ kausuṃbhatailakaiḥ ||

kausuṃbhavasanāvṛtaḥ | tathā kausuṃbhagaṃdhān atrāpi ca sthalaṃ śodhyaṃ 
pūrvavat kīlasaṃvidhiḥ || homaḥ sahasraṃ tritayaṃ kausuṃbha kusumaiḥ kila 
tatsaṃkhyānako japaḥ | prokto madhyarātre gate sati | 

śataṃ ninādā jāyaṃte maṃḍalādā samaṃ tataḥ |
ghorāḥ karkaśabhāṣiṇyo ḍākinyokta mahābhayāḥ ||

śākinyopi śataṃ tatra nadaṃti bhayadāruṇāḥ |
tatkīla pratiropaistu nāyāṃti japamaṃḍalaṃ ||

idaṃ mithyeti manasā bhāvayan sādhakottamaḥ |
svāṃta dhyānaika nirato japamāloktamānasaḥ ||

na paśyati puro vighnān japahomāṃtarāyakān |
evaṃ yadā yadā tasmin śapatrī vanāṃtare ||

aṃtarāyādikaṃ paśyet tanmithyeti ca bhāvayet |
tasmin tasmin kṣaṇe maṃtrī samāhitamanāḥ svayaṃ ||

devānāṃ dhyānanirato japamālākṛtodyamaḥ |
evaṃ kāle gate tasmin devī devaśatairvṛtā ||

nṛtyaṃ kinnarasaṃyuktā udgāsyadgaṇaśobhitā |
japākusumasaṃkāśa tanu jyotiḥ śatāvṛtā ||

svakarāvasthitaṃ caika phalaṃ tatsādhakāya hi |
prayacchati sadā tuṣṭā te nāsau sādhakottamaḥ ||

dūraṃ yāti kṣaṇaitevamanaḥ pavanavegavān |
adṛśyaḥ sarvalokānāṃ api rājagṛhāṃtare ||

maṃtraḥ ||

oṃ śive śivadūtī śaṃ śaṃ sīkhakarapaṃkajaphale dehi manojavacaraṇayordehi 
bhraṃmabhaṃ namaḥ || 

asyāpi bhāṣā maṃtrosti sa cocyate || pāṃḍya bhāṣayā || 

maṃtraḥ || 

anavilakuṃḍa ili nimātaṃmibhuṃbhaṃ ||

49b)

asyāpi japastadvat ṣaṭsahasraṃ vidhīyate |
tena kārāgrahānmaṃtrī paśyatvādī prayāti hi ||

atyaṃta nigaḍāvaddhaḥ sopi pāti kṣaṇena hi |
tathā rājārājaputrastathāsau vahirudgateḥ ||

na kena pratiruddhosau kṛtāṃta iva dṛśyate |
idamadyāpi sāmudrīḥ pāṃḍyā deśāṃtare sthitāḥ ||

kurvaṃti rājaputrāśca paśyato haraṇaṃ dhruvaṃ |
paśyato haraṇī vidyānāstyanyā jagatī tale ||

dhyānaṃ || 

udyadbhānu sahasrābhāṃ kamalāsana pūjitāṃ |
haste mohamayaṃ pāśaṃ dadhānāṃ prabhajecchivāṃ ||

atra pūrve maṃtre ḍākinyādayaḥ śatamāyāṃti prativaṃdhakāriṇyo 
japamadhye vā tatra akṣamālā samāhito bhūtvā maṃtrī tanmithyeti manasi 
saṃciṃtya japahomādi kārayet || eva muktena prakāreṇa devī prasannā bhavati | 
tena svakara sthita phalaṃ maṃtriṇe prayacchati tenaiva siddhayo bhavaṃti | 
dūragamanaṃ apratyakṣī karaṇaṃ rājādyaṃtara gṛha saṃcaraṇaṃ tathā ca 
pāṃḍyabhāṣayā śivāmaṃtraḥ pūrvoktaḥ sa cakṣaṇaivadīkṛtaṃ mocayati || 
rājāparādhinamapi rājavaddevakāramati | idaṃ paśyato haraṇaṃ nāma 
mahāvidyā || pāṃḍyadeśīya lokānāṃ prasiddhā || ata eva pāṃḍyāḥ 
samudrāṃtaraṃ naukā sthitāḥ | rājānaṃ rājabhaṃḍāraṃ svecchayā 
luṃṭhayaṃti | idamadyāpi prasiddhaṃ tadevānya vidhayā prāha || 

siṃhaladvīpadeśe tu prayāśāratnakāriṇāṃ |
iyaṃ valavatīvidyā sarvasaukhya pradāyinī ||

mohayitvā tu nṛpatiṃ sadyodhanapatiṃ prabhuṃ |
samudramapi bhūśaṃte samastāratnajātayaḥ ||

kaṃdarpya citrakāreṇa bhūtalesmin prakāśitāḥ |
tenaiva yogena tāhi bhūmau samyak caraṃti hi ||

iyaṃ valavatīvidyā kāmarūpepi vartate ||

iti śivāmaṃtravidhiḥ || atha vālāmaṃtravidhiḥ || 

udvasagrāmasadvane hemavṛkṣaśatākule |
hemaṃtartau puṣpamāsi pūrṇamāsyāṃ vidhūdayāt ||

50a)

hemavījasutailena kṛta snāna vidhirnnaraḥ |
kauśeya vasanastadvat kaṣāya vanastathā ||

nagnotha vā japenmaṃtraṃ vālāyā vālakopamaḥ |
gomayena samālipya śūnya gehasya bhūmikāṃ ||

caṃdanena samālipya tatpaścāt kuṃkumeṇa tu |
tatra dūrvādalaiḥ pūjyo bhūtale sukṛtāsanaḥ ||

japedvālāmanuṃ lakṣyaṃ dhattūraṃ kusumaiḥ sakṛt |
homaṃ kuryāt sahasraṃ hi hemavījena cārcanaṃ ||

tato rātreḥ prāṃtabhāge vālāsāpaṃcavārṣikā |
hemavastraparīdhānā muktā bharaṇabhūṣitāḥ ||

dūrānmaṃtridrumārūḍhā lālasāvālabhūṣaṇā |
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā dūrato dhāvan gacche tatsaṃnidhau tadā ||

sāpi modaprahṛṣṭā hi cuṃvaṃtpāśutadānanaṃ |
taccumbanena maṃtrī sa jāyate rasanāyakaḥ ||

sabhā madhye tu yāṃ vārtāṃ karoti sa hi sādhakaḥ |
rasasaṃdohinīsāsyānmohinī sarvasaṃpadaḥ ||

vārtābhirmuhyate rājā muhyate kāminī tathā |
muhyate vāravanitā muhyate rājabhāminī ||

vyāghrādi paśujātīnāṃ mohanaṃ tadvaco bhavet ||

dhyānaṃ ||

kanakakapilamaulī rocanāraṃjita śrīśatamukha mukhadevaiḥ pūjyamānā 
manojñā | 
lalitavacana ceṣṭācāru caṃdrāvataṃ sā nayanasubhagabhālāmanmukhe 
sāstuvālā || 

maṃtraḥ ||

oṃ paṃcavārṣikivālevacanamādhusiṃ mama dehi dehi karuṇāṃ kuru 2 hlīṃ 
hlīṃ || mukhyataścātra maṃtrosyā vāle hlīṃ hlīṃ iti dhruvaṃ || 

dhyānārthaṃ pallavaḥ proktaḥ nāsāvāvasyako mataḥ |
etasya pratirūpo hi maṃtromagadhabhāṣayā ||

tasyā yutaṃ japaḥ proktastasmintu dvasamaṃdire |
japāṃte lalitā devī vālā pratyakṣa gocarā ||

hlīṃ hlīṃ miti vadaṃtyāśu maṃtriṇaḥ karṇamaṃḍale |
tadvīja smaraṇānmaṃtrī trailokyāvaśyakārakaḥ ||

maṃtraḥ ||

oṃ māyī oṃ māyī dāyī mohivasaṃdehi vālike vāli hlīṃ hlīṃ || 

atra vālāmaṃtrasya caturakṣaratvameva mukhyataḥ | 

50b)

anyetūpamaṃtrāḥ | atraiva proktāḥ | tathāhi || 

paṃcavārṣikī hlīṃ hlīṃ ityeko maṃtraḥ || vāle ca vanamādhurīṃ dehi 
hlīmityaparo maṃtraḥ | paṃcavārṣikī karuṇāṃ kuru 2 hlīmityaparaḥ | iti maṃtra 
catuṣṭayī || mahāvidyeti vikhyātā | ata eva mahāmohakarī || nṛpāmātyāstrī 
veśyā rājastrī mohakarī | etasya pratirūpaṃ kaṃmagadhabhāṣayā 
maṃtrātaraṃ tasminneva kāle pauṣapaurṇamāsyāṃ udvāsasadane 
hemavṛkṣāḥ | dhattūravṛkṣāḥ tadā kule tairvāse dhattūrakusumairhomaḥ || 
dhattūravṛkṣavījaiḥ pūjā || 

etasyaiva prathāṃtaramāha || 

māgadheṣu hi deśeṣu śiva yogīti kaścana |
japtvainaṃmatyarthaṃ ca yathoktena vidhinā tataḥ ||

jayasiṃhasya bhūpasya putrī kāmakalābhidhā |
vasī ca kāratāṃ sadyaḥ punnāma dveṣakāriṇī ||

atyaṃtavītarāgāsāsvanāmadveṣakāriṇī |
yogābhyāsaika niratā yogamāyā vinirgatā ||

kṛśāṃgī svaśanāsītā jātāyauvanaśālinī |
tatastāṃ jayasiṃhopi dṛṣṭvā viklinnamānasaḥ ||

varārthaṃ ciṃtayāmāsa bhūpatīnāṃ kumārakān |
kadācidvanitādvārāpapraccha svatanūdbhavāṃ ||

vālekastebhilaṣito rājaputreṣu suṃdaraḥ |
ityuktaṃ tasya cākarṇya devī kāmakalā hi sā ||

nāsya piṃḍasya bhartāsti bhavitāvāna kaścana |
ityuvāca svajanakaṃ viraktā viṣayeṣu sā ||

ityetadvacanaṃ śrutvā nṛpaściṃtā śatā vṛtaḥ |
jagamasaṁghoraṃ mṛgayā vyājato dhruvaṃ ||

vane dūraṃ gato rājādadarśāśramamuttamaṃ |
suvarcaso munīndrasya vedaghoṣasamākulaṃ ||

praśāṃtaścāpadākīrṇaṃmadvaitaṃ sumanoharaṃ |
vāpīkūpasarassaṃghairmadhye madhye virājitaṃ ||

tatrāvatīryacāśvāsaṃtyatirmati suṃdaraḥ |
prativadhyāścamasmihnijagāmāśrama gahvaraṃ ||

sadṛṣṭvāmunirājaṃ hi daṃḍavannipapāta ca |
uttiṣṭottiṣṭha rājendra ityabhāṣya munīśvaraḥ ||

kasya deśasya rājātvaṃ kutaścātra samāgataḥ |

51a)

ityukto muninā tena pratibhāṣata vai nṛpaḥ ||

ahaṃ māgadhadeśasya rājāciṃtā vaśodhruvaṃ |
tvatsamīpamihāyāto yadīcchasi kuruṣva tat ||

putrīkāmakalā me hi tyakta kāmāsti sāṃprataṃ |
ityākarṇya vacastasya bhāvagarbhaṃ munīśvaraḥ ||

dideśamaṃtramenaṃ hi śiṣyāya śivayogine |
rājāpi śivayogīndraṃ dhṛtvā ca karapaṃkaje ||

nirjagāmāśramāt tasmādyātaḥ svanagarī prati |
tatastasmai munīndrāya dadau grāmādvahirgṛhaṃ ||

śoṇabhadrataṭe ramye nivavāsasa yogivān |
rājaputrī sadāsnāte māyāṃtītaṃ mahānadaṃ ||

dadarśa śivayogīndramuhyamānāvabhūvahi |
kāmapīḍita cittāsā jagāmāca tadāśramaṃ ||

taṃ dadarśalasadrūpaṃ lalitāpāṃgasuṃdaraṃ |
prasphuradadharaṃ vaktramāvṛṇoti punaḥ punaḥ ||

pulakāṃkitadordaṇḍa dṛḍhakaṃcuka śālinaṃ |
kaṃpasaṃ sarjitāṃgī ca prasphurallocanāṃcalā ||

svedavindulasadvaṃdadadhānā vadanāṃvuje |
bhītabhīte ca sāvākyaṃ praskhaladvarṇavaṃdharaṃ ||

prahasadvadanāguptaṃ daṃtamāṇikyamālikā |
provāca śivayogīndraṃ bhāvākūtamanoramaṃ ||

mune kutaḥ samāyātaṃ kinnāma bhagavanvada |
darśanīyosi jagatāmānaṃdaśatadāyakaḥ ||

jagadārti haro rājā jagatāṃ hi kalāvatāṃ |
kāminīnāṃ mano bhāvo mūrtimānivalakṣyase ||

kāsti puṇyavatīkāṃtā taktāruṇyanāyakā |
kathaṃ vādyatayā yuktastvaṃnagasamaḥ sadā ||

yopikostubhavānbhavya śrotumicchatimadvacaḥ |
ahaṃ dīnā'valānāthatvaṃdrūpaparimohitā ||

kāmāśugapadīghāta śatacchidrita mānasā |
māmanātha bhaye nātha pāṇau kartu tvamarhasi ||

avalānāṃ valaṃ caitat kāṃ bho pakṣā vidhau dhruvaṃ |
svajīvana parityāgastannimittaṃstvameva hi ||

ityuktaḥ kāmakalayā sa yogī jñātamānasaḥ |
uvāca tāṃ mohanāṃgī kāmoratimivā parāṃ ||

aye bhadrāṃgi bhadraṃ te tvasti lakṣaṇamati dhruvaṃ |

51b)

aviśvāsyāḥ striyaḥ puṃbhirahaṃ kāryā vidhau dhruvaṃ ||

punaḥ kāmakalā prāhastaṃ munīndraṃ sphurāśayā |
aye nātha tvadīyāṃghra chāyāśaityaika jīvinī ||

atha tvameva vadasi viśvāsyāḥ nāstriyastviti |
rāvamuktastayā yogī kāminyā manmathā śriyā ||

provāca sarasaṃ vākyaṃ sadā yādiṣṭa mānasaḥ |
kamale kṣiṇite rūpaṃ dṛśyate sumanoharaṃ ||

asyarādeśasyarājñotvaṃ putrī premavardhitā |
rājāparādhaḥ kartavyaḥ kathaṃ vai yogināmayā ||

ekāṃtavasati puṇyā yogīnāmiti durlabhā |
tapasviṣu parīhāso yanmunīnāṃ parigrahaḥ ||

ityuktā muninā vālā provāca capale kṣaṇā |
ahameva purā brahman tyaktakāṃtakathā yathā ||

iti kṛtvā gururmepi ciṃtā saṃtatamānasaḥ |
adyāpi yatate mehi pāṇigrahavidhau mune ||

iti māṃ tvat saṃgatiḥ śrutvā nṛpopi śruta suṃdaraḥ |
bhadramityutkaṭaṃ citte saṃtoṣaṃ toṣayiṣyati ||

yaduktaṃ nātha yogo hi parigraha vidūṣitaḥ |
yatā nāmeva sargo * parivrajana śobhitāṃ ||

saṃtyanyepi vasiṣṭādyāḥ śrutasaṃtuṣṭa cetasaḥ |
kiṃ parigraha duṣṭāste nātha citte kuruṣva tat ||

ahamepyupavāsādyaiḥ śuddhacittā sadāśayā |
tvaṃ cedupekṣase nātha maraṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ mama ||

ityuktastutayā devyā muniḥ kāmakalākulaḥ |
aśraddheti prativākyena svāsayāmāsatāṃ sakhī ||

tatastau kṛta saṃtoṣo rājadūtībhiḥ parīkṣitau |
anyonyavārtāvijñātaṃ śūnyaṃtā dadhatī dhruvaṃ ||

etasminnaṃtare cāra nārībhiḥ * * * * * |
etasya pratirūpaṃ hi maṃtronya gaṃdhabhāṣayā ||

prajaptastu tathā rātrau tatraiva mṛtabhūmiṣu |
nātra homosti devī sā guptarūpeṇa maṃtriṇe ||

dadāti laghuvetraṃ hi tena vetreṇa sādhakaḥ |
śṛṃkhalāṃ bhaṃjayet sadyo lohakoṭi prakalpitaṃ ||

tathā dvārakapāṭāni kalilāni tathā śataṃ |

52a)

pāṣāṇa kuḍyajātāni kakubhāni śatāvadhi ||

lohakīla sahasrāṇi gajavājīnivaṃdhanaṃ |
nigaḍānāṃ sahasrāṇi bhaṃjayet sādhakaḥ kṣaṇāt ||

pratyayārthaṃ pravakṣyāmi tasya maṃtrasya kīlakaṃ |
yena kenāpi bhāṃḍānāṃ pākaśālānāṃ pragamya hi ||

etanmaṃtreṇa saṃmaṃtrya vījānyaṃvaraśākhinaḥ |
saṃtyajet tatra śālāyāṃ bhāṃḍabhaṃga kṣaṇena hi ||

jāyatedyāpi tasyaiṣā pratīteḥ sarvagocarāḥ ||

athamaṃtraḥ ||

vāṃsathā ugora hi tu kelakelā othātukabhījabhāṃḍāvaḥ | atra phālguṇa 
kṛṣṇapratipadi rātrau vetravāsinī japaḥ | śmaśāna bhūmau kāryaḥ 
pūrvavadbhūmiṃ * tastāḥ || paṃcahastaṃ jānudadhnaṃ khanitvā tatra pūrvokta 
kīlakaṃ catuṣkaṃ caturdikṣunopayitvā madhye cāsanna kīlakaṃ saṃropya 
tadupari saṃsthitvā japaḥ | paṃcasahasraṃ kāryaḥ homo daśāṃśena 
vetramūlaiḥ || tato devī vetraṃ pradadati tena vṛścika sarpaviṣaṃ tadvetra nīreṇa 
pīte naśyati || 

adyāpi vaṃgadeśe purujalāṭhīti prasiddhaḥ | 
tasya daṃḍasya tasyaiva pratirūpaṃ bhāṣāmaṃtraḥ || 

tatra homābhāvepi sāphalyamasti || atra sa eva kramo japasya phalāṃtaraṃ | lohādi 
śṛṃkhalābhaṃgaḥ || bhāṃḍapākaśālā tāmraghaṭīghaṭana haṭhaḥ | tatra 
gatvā amvaraśānākhye khelavṛkṣaḥ | tasya vījāni abhimaṃtrya pākasthale 
cetyaktāni tadā bhāṃḍānāṃ śatacchidrāṇi bhavaṃti || ityadyāpi vaṃgadeśe 
pratītirasti | avalājanaḥ kopo na tathā karoti || etasya prathāṃtaramāha || 

yaṃtrasthānāni yatraitānya tulānyagni bhāvanāt |
jāyate pṛthivīśānāṃ tadbhaṃge yaṃ vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ||

siṃsarūvṛkṣa vījāni mālicūrṇe catudvayaṃ |
saṃmaṃtryānena maṃtreṇa rātrau svakara saṃpuṭe ||

taddvayaṃ mardayen maṃtrī bhajyaṃte tāni tatkṣaṇāt |
rathanirmāṇa kāle hi tatsamīpe tu maṃtriṇā ||

karaṃkī vīja bhasmāśu maṃtrāṃte tu sa nikṣipet |

52b)

tannikṣepanīyaṃ tatsaratho bhajyate |

rājamaṃdiranirmāṇe śākavṛkṣasya bhasma hi |
saṃmaṃtrya maṃtrī tadvāre nikṣipet paṃcamī tithau ||

rātrau kṣaṇena tadgahe kāṣṭhabhaṃgena saṃpatet |
gaṭhadurgāri nirmāṇe prajapenmanumuttamaṃ ||

dvādaśyāṃ niśi bhaume ca tatkāni saṃpaṭheddhi tat |
sāmudravālukāṃ maṃtrī kuḍyādau saṃprati kṣipet ||

tatkāla bhaṃgamāpnoti kuḍyādi pṛthivī tale | 
atra yaṃtra sthānāni rathārohyāgni yatra nirmāṇe sthāne 
bhūpālairyuddhārthaṃ kriyamāṇāgni vāṇayaṃtrasthānā nityarthaḥ || 
atrasijhara vṛkṣavījāni jharjharavṛkṣavījānimālicūrṇagaṃdhe māli 
cūrṇagaṃdhamāli cūrṇaṃ | tadvayamanena maṃtreṇa maṃtritaṃ maṃtrī 
svakare maṃtrayet || mardanakālegni cchāṇadi yaṃtrāṇi majyate | karaṃkī vījaṃ 
tadbhatena maṃtreṇa maṃtritaṃ rathanirmāṇa kālerathopari rātrau cennikṣipte 
tadārathaṃ || kṣaṇādbhajyate śākavṛkṣa prasiddhaḥ || tasya bhasmasaṃmaṃtrya 
rājagehadvāre paṃcamyāṃ rātrau cennikṣiptaṃ tadārājagehaṃ kṣaṇāt patati || 
tathā gaḍa durgādau rājñāṃ dvādaśyāṃ bhaumavāre niśi tatsamīpe 
japtoyaṃ manustatkālaṃ gaḍa durgādi pātayet tithā kuḍyādau 
samudratīravālukāṃ saṃmaṃtrya prakṣipet patati || idaṃ durgādāvapi kāryaṃ 
samāna kriyatvāditi || atra sarvatra vetreṇa devadattena maṃteṇa saṃyojayet || japet 
tena tatkālaṃ siddhyatyāśu yathoditaṃ || atra bhāṣā maṃtra vījādi maṃtreṇa 
samaye devatā dattena vetreṇa sadyonya maṃtrayet || tenokta yaṃtrādi bhaṃgo 
bhavati || iti vetravāsinīvidhiḥ || atha sphuṭākṣīvidhiḥ || 
nāraṃgaranārīkelīnāvane vā vā nadītaṭe mādhavamāsi cāṣṭamyāṃ 
kṛṣṇapakṣe niśāvidhau | atha vā *? tare ramye tādṛgvanavibhūṣite | atha vā 
kamalābhūṣite sa sarastaṭe vāpī kuṭajasaṃyuktā punnāgādi virājitā || 

53a)

tasyā tīre'thavā maṃtraṃ prajapedenamuttamaṃ |
sahasraṃ prajapenmaṃtraṃ khanitvā bhūmimuttamāṃ ||

kīlādi vidhimādhāya japedenaṃ vidhiṃ tataḥ |
atrāyāṃti mahāghorā vetālā kuṃtapāṇayaḥ ||

tānālocya punarmaṃtrī vāmapāṇinā svasṛtā |
tānsasicya tataḥ sadyoyāṃtitekhamanākulaṃ ||

tataḥ punaḥ samāraṃbha kupī maṃtra japasya hi |
evaṃ japet samāraṃbhe punaḥ kātyāyanī svayaṃ ||

āyāti śavamuṃḍāni varṣatī ca punaḥ punaḥ |
bhīṣaṇābhīti nayanā karālā daśanākulā ||

tāmālocya punarmaṃtrī vāmajaṃghāt sṛjādhruvaṃ |
siṃcayet tāṃ tataḥ sāpi prayāti gaganāṃtaraṃ ||

tataḥ punaḥ samāraṃbhe japenmaṃtrī yathāvidhiḥ |
bhairavī punarāyātilaṃvāṃvararadadvayā ||

gajamuṃḍaṃ ceyaṃtī varṣaṃtī śoṇitaṃ bhuvi |
tatsamīpe mahāghorā karālā lamvapāṇayaḥ ||

vīravīreśvarīścānye ca vepaṃtaḥ svaśoṇitaṃ |
bhayanādakarā kecit ḍamaḍḍamarupāṇayaḥ ||

hāheti pratibhāṣaṃtaḥ śastamāṃ dolayaṃtite |
maṃtriṇaṃghnaṃ tu māyāṃti jihvālalanabhīṣaṇā ||

anyonyaṃ ghātayaṃtastevyestamastaka ceṣṭitāḥ |
ātkālitākṣi yugalāmaḍisphālana tatparāḥ ||

te sarve ghorarūpā hi snātyayaṃstu maṃtriṇāṃ |
dhīreṇa sādhakendreṇa tasmin kāle kapālajāṃ ||

sirā māhatya raktena bhairavā bhīṣaṇāśca tān |
āsiṃcyamānā saṃvīkṣya gacchaṃto viyata yathā ||

punaḥ samārabhe maṃtraṃ japaṃ maṃtraṃ yathāvidhi |
tataḥ karoti nirvighnaṃ japaṃ maṃtrī yathāvidhiḥ ||

sahasraṃ prajapitvā tu homaṃ kuryād daśāṃśataḥ |
nāraṃgairnālikelaiśca devi pratyakṣa gocarā ||

dadāti maṃtriṇe caikaṃ nārikelaṃ manoramaṃ || 

tatpūjayet sadā maṃtrī tenāsya sadanaṃ sadā |
gajāṃta lakṣmīkrīḍābhi naṃdayed gajamaṃdiraṃ ||

53b)

jayeti ca mahālakṣmī saṃstauti prativāsaraṃ |
api dāsī kule jātaḥ sopi dhananāyakaḥ || 

vikrama prathito lokeśūraḥ saṃjitasaṃgaraḥ |
jāyate pṛthivīyaṃ hi dvitīyaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ ||

yāvat tiṣṭhati medinyāṃ tāvatsodhananāyakaḥ |
striyaḥ pūjyā sadā tena jitendreṇa vidhānataḥ ||

bhramaṃti ca sarvanāryastaṃ prekṣya dhananāyakaṃ |
mahādānādi kartā sa jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ||

dhyānaṃ ||

caṃdrasūrya sphuṭālola nayanāmaruṇaprabhāṃ |
aruṇāṃvarasaṃśobhāṃ sphuṭākṣīṃ prabhajet sadā ||

maṃtraḥ ||

viśālākṣi gajāṃta lakṣmīṃ dehi 2 dāridryaṃ dūraya 2 hrīṃ sphuṭā bhuṃ 
svāhā || 

etasya pratirūpaṃ hi maṃtrassopyaṃgabhāṣayā |
pūrvokta vanamadhye tu japaḥ kārya sahasrakaṃ ||

homopi pūrvavat kāryaḥ paralakṣmīṃ vikarṣati |

atra bhāṣāmaṃtreṇogrābhītayaḥ || nāpi devatāsāṃ mukhyaṃ jape home ca 
pūrvokta samaye kṛte satiyo dhanavāniti stvasya samaṃ tā? * * * * * * * * * * * *? 
nātra saṃdehaḥ || aṃgadeśe cādyāpi vyāpāriṇaḥ | pratijñayā manumenaṃ 
japati maṃtraḥ || vaḍacakhu ālāramā āralakhīdeno pārapāra sphuṭāṃ hrīṃ 
svāhā || iti sphuṭākṣīvidhiḥ || 

atha haritālākṣīvidhiḥ || 

mṛgapraveśe saṃjāte dvitīya caraṇe dhruvaṃ |
ādi me divase rātrau vane kevala nirjane ||

nadīṃ vāpi sarovīkṣya tatra snātva narottamaḥ |
haritālaṃ samālipya svamukhe śuddhamānasaḥ ||

ayutaṃ haritālākṣaḥ prajapet sādhakottamaḥ |
ghṛtakarpūrakāśmīrakausuṃbhairhomamācaret ||

pūrṇāṃ kuryāt kusuṃbhena haritāla rase spṛśā |
tato devī samāyāti lalitā haritālakā ||

bhīṣaṇā haritālākṣī nagnāṃgī vyāghra saṃsthitā |
tāmālocya punarmaṃtrī svākṣamālāṃ hṛdi smaran ||

tadvyāsaṃgaika yogena sā punaścīradhāraṇā |
mohayaṃtī jagatsarvaṃ aruṇadyuti maṃḍalā ||

54a)

tasyā vāme punarbhāge devīrati kalābhidhā |
sāpunarmohayaṃtīva dṛśyate maṃtriṇā svayaṃ ||

kurvaṃtu vacanālāpaṃ vahudhāvahubhāṣayā |
lāvaṇyāmṛtadhārābhirmaṃtrirājaṃ hi devatā ||

mohayaṃtī tato maṃtrī tadvākyāni na viśvaset |
tataḥ prabhātasamaye sā devī mūlamaṃtrajāḥ ||

prāyaso haritālākṣī dvitīyāṃtāṃ hi bhāginīṃ |
gṛhītvā svakare maṃtrī kare samyak prayacchati ||

tato maṃtrī gṛhītvā tāṃ devīṃ rati kalābhidhāṃ |
vaśībhūtā tu sā devī gṛhītvā maṃtriṇāṃ dhruvaṃ ||

khecaraṃ kurvatī sadyo gaṇagaṃdharvakinnarān |
darśayaṃtī kṣaṇe tvaiva punarbhūtamaṃḍalī ||

manaściṃtitaṃ deśaṃ hi kṣaṇānmaṃtrī pradhāvati |
yakṣiṇī bhūtavetāla bhairavānati bhairavān ||

ānayaṃti kṣaṇe naiva maṃtriṇe vaśamādarāt |
padminī strī śatānyāśu darśayaṃti hi maṃtriṇe ||

tadbhogabhoginaṃ sadyaḥ kurvaṃtī maṃtranāyakaṃ |
punarbhūmitalevāṭī vane bhūmiṣu sā dhruvaṃ ||

navanārī gajendraṃ hi darśayaṃtī svamaṃtriṇe |
naravaktra vyāghra dehamevaṃ hi punaradbhutaṃ ||

naraśārdūlamenaṃ hi darśayaṃtī svamaṃtriṇe |
navanārī śarīrākhyaṃ ardhanārīśvaraṃ dhruvaṃ ||

darśayaṃtī punardevī bhūtaleṣu vanāṃtare |
tathā kamalajāṃ daivīṃ darśayaṃtī svamaṃtriṇe ||

tebhyastebhyo phalopāyaṃ punarvakṣyāmi sādaraṃ |
navanārī gajeṃdro hi yo dṛṣṭo maṃtriṇā dhruvaṃ ||

saṃbhāṣyāḥ kilatānāryaḥ sādhakena tadaiva ca |
tathaivatāstuti padaistoṣaṇīyāṃ vanāṃtare ||

saṃtuṣṭā kilatānāryo maṃtriṇaṃ vasanāṃcalaṃ |
saṃprayacchaṃti tenāśu jñāyate jaṃtumānasaṃ ||

ayameva purājanma nyāsīditi ca yonijaṃ |
vijñāyate tasya maṃtriṇaḥ sarvamaṃtriṇaḥ ||

yo dṛṣṭo naraśārdūrastastutiḥ punaruttamā |
kartavyā sa punastuṣṭaḥ khaḍgamekaṃ dadāti hi ||

vajratulyena khaḍgeṇa sa narovīrarād bhavet |
palāyaṃte purastasya yuddhe sarve naṭeśvarāḥ ||

54b)

ardhanārīśvaro dṛṣṭaḥ sastotavyānayāṃgirā |
devakātyāyanī nātha māṃ prasīda priyeśvarī ||

rāvastutaḥ sa bhagavān ardhanārīśvaro dhruvaṃ |
saṃgītavidyāmatulāṃ prayacchatpāśu maṃtriṇe ||

dhyānaṃ ||

japā puṣpa sahasraugha dyotamānāṃ maheśvarī |
dhyāyet tāṃ haritālākṣīṃ siddhi dīkṣāṃ vitanvatīṃ ||

maṃtraḥ || 

oṃ hrīṁ haritālākṣi ratikalāṃ dehi 2 svāhā || 

asyaiva pratirūpaṃ hi maṃtro hehaikabhāṣayā |
pūrvavat sa tu japtavyo nāsti homavidhi dhruvaṃ ||

tena tuṣya jagaddhātrī pradadāti hi maṃtriṇe |
ākarṣaṇīṃ mahāvidyāṃ jagadānaṃdadāyinīṃ ||

patrapuṣpaphalādīnāṃ kāminīnāṃ karoti hi |
ākarṣaṇaṃ kṣaṇai caiva yadi dhattā śivo bhavet ||

maṃtraḥ ||

oṃ haritā iṃgiṇo iṇiṃḍu mecciḍuṃ bhrūṃ bhrīṃ hrūṃ svāhā || 

atrākṣamālāṃ punaḥ smarediti ādikṣāṃtā mālā tatra mano datvā japaḥ 
kāryaḥ tena maṃtriṇe bhayaṃ na bhavati || ayaṃ sahacarī maṃtra iti 
śukrācāryāt || prasiddhaṃ || tathā ca śāvaraśaṃbhuḥ || 

yanmaṃtre khalu siddhe hi sidhyaṃtyanyā hi devatāḥ |
saiṣā sahacarī vidyā sarvāṃgamasugopitā ||

tathā ca gauḍapādācāryaḥ || 

maṃtrāṃtare susiddhe hi siddhetyenyāstu devatāḥ | 
ekāvalī mahāvidyā sahacaryapi gīyate ||

tathā ca etasyāṃ haritālikāyāṃ ratikalā devatā siddhiḥ |
tataśca navanārī kuṃjaradevatā puruṣaśārdūla ceṭakaḥ ||

ardhanārīśvaraśca bhagavān gaurīpatiriti eṣā sahacarī mahāvidyā proktāḥ | 

atha pratirūpakaṃhaiva bhāṣāmaṃtraḥ || 

tena patrapuṣpaphalādīnāmadyāpi rājavinodi yogīśvarā diṣu dṛśyaṃte || 
kāminī cakṣaṇenākarṣayā kāpi svamate viṣayamāgataḥ kāminī tāṃ dṛṣṭvā 
smṛtvā cāyaṃ maṃtrānusaṃdheyastatkālaṃ sā 
kenāpyadṛśyamāṇavadvāyuvaśādaṃvaracarī bhūtvā maṃtrigehamāyāti || 
adyāpi teṣu tathā nīlakaṇṭha nepālādau prasiddheyaṃ 

55a)

vidyājaneṣu rājakumārīmapite aṃteḥ purādānayati kenāpya jñātacarāṃ 
tathā kāmarūpadeśeṣu naukākarṇadhāre śriyaṃ vidyā prasiddhā yathā 
kāpāliṣvapi || iyaṃ tu paramāvidyā siddhā pravarāvara svāmine 
śaṃbhunādattā punargṛhītā tasmāt sapārvatīpati kuṭilavuddhi bhāvanāsīditi 
kāmarūpe prasiddhiḥ || iti haritālākṣīvidhiḥ || 

atha kuṃḍinīvidhiḥ || 

kālaṃjale mahāśaile nīlakaṃṭhasya maṃdire |
rātrau śivacaturdaśyāṃ japed devīṃ ca kuṃḍinīṃ ||

tanmaṃdire pivetāla devatā bhūmimaṃḍale |
japaḥ sahasra tritayaṃ kuṃḍinyā kilamaṃtriṇā ||

kartavyo vilvamūlena homastu taddaśāṃśataḥ |
kālaṃjara mahāśailaṃ nīlakaṃṭhasya maṃdirāt ||

purobhāgesti subhagaḥ kalāṇo nāma śaṃkaraḥ |
tasya devālaye vātha japtavyo yaṃ manustathā ||

jape home kṛte sadyaḥ kuṃḍanāgo mahāvalī |
vistīrṇa vadano laṃvo dṛśyate yugaviṃśati ||

phaṇāṃ prasāryanāgosau sadyastiṣṭhati maṃtriṇaḥ |
purastāt tatra nirbhātyā sthātavyaṃ tena matriṇā ||

phūtkārāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi kurute sa phaṇāṃ dhruvaṃ |
tasya jvālā śataṃ vaktrā niḥsaraṃti punaḥ punaḥ ||

tathā viṣāṇi vahudhā nīlapītacchavīnihi |
palāsāni tato dhūma salilaṃ tadanaṃtaraṃ ||

kāmalaṃ ca tatoṃḍāni pakṣiṇaḥ pakṣaśālinaḥ |
evaṃ vidhānyanekāni citrāṇi ca tadā nanāt ||

tadā nirbhītinābhāvyaṃ sādhakena manasvinā |
tato devī tamārūḍhā dṛśyate sumanoramā ||

pakṣaṇī śatasaṃsevyātakṣakastrībhirāvṛtāḥ |
sā kuṃḍinīti capalā viśālā raktalocanā ||

sāstotavyā munīndreṇa stutyaivaṃvidhayā dhruvaṃ |
namaste jagatāṃdhātri namaste kamalekṣaṇi ||

namaste nādarūpiṇyai bhairavyai te namo namaḥ |
kalākāṣṭhādi rūpāyai svarūpāyai namoṃ śataṃ ||

namaḥ kaiśikī rūpiṇyai hemākṣāyai namo namaḥ |

55b)

rajatādri vidhātryaite viśālāyai namo namaḥ ||

vāmanetryai namastestu vāsuki stuti bhāvane |
namaste nararūpe hi namaste bhāvabhāvini ||

namo nārīsvarūpe te namaste nāradātmake |
namaste lalitāpāṃgī namaste dhūrjaṭī priye ||

namaste kaṃsanāśinyai nāmanītyai namo namaḥ |
vasudhāyai namastestu sudhāyai satataṃ namaḥ ||

akhaṃḍānaṃdadāyiṇyai bhavānyai satataṃ namaḥ |
apārāyai vipārāyai paradāyai namo namaḥ ||

vījadhāma nidhātāyai vidhānavidhaye namaḥ |
vidhātryai vāsudevāyai śivāyai prasabhaṃ namaḥ ||

kaumāryai nārasiṃhyaite aindryai devyai namo namaḥ |
sudhākara mahādhāma chaṭāchurita tejasā ||

vapuṣā viśvamakhilaṃ dyotayaṃtyai namo namaḥ |
vodhavodhita viśvāyai mohakāriṇi te namaḥ ||

ātmajyoti svarūpiṇyai śāśvataṃ namaḥ |
ramāvilāsadāyinyai puṇyadāyai namo namaḥ ||

akhaṃḍalakratu vidhi prastutāyai namo namaḥ |
narendranīti nipuṇe purāṇe tvāṃ bhajāmyahaṃ ||

evaṃ stutā hi sā devī prasīdati tapaśvine |
dadātya mṛtamudgrāhya garutmamaṇinirmite ||

pātre tadā tadāyūya tato maṃtrīsutoṣitaḥ |
karoti kālasaṃprāpti vaṃcanaṃ sa tu yogavān ||

kiṃcidu sthitimālocya svaśarīrasya maṃtriṇaḥ |
viṃdumātraṃ pivenmaṃtrī tenāsāvamaro bhavet ||

devāṃśo yastu manujastasyaivāyaṃ vidhiḥ dhruvaṃ |
sādhyo bhavedidaṃ śāstraṃ labhate devatātmakaḥ ||

atra idaṃ śāstraṃ nānyasya hastagata bhavati śāvarītaṃtraṃ tu tasyaiva haste 
patati yo devatāṃśo bhavet || 

dhyānaṃ || 

ārūḍhaṃ nijanāgamadbhutaphaṇaṃ vyāpāramithyā kṛtaṃ 
trailokyamaṃdhakāra subhagaṃ jihvā sphuradrociṣaṃ || phūtkārāhata 
bhūruhaṃ śaśi śataṃ pradyotamānāṃ śivāmātāmra sphuṭalocanāṃ 
bhajamano hemaṃ kaṣāṃ kuṇḍinīṃ ||

56a)

maṃtraḥ || 

oṃ kuṃḍini nāgavāhane phūḥ phūḥ svāhā || 

etasya pratirūpaṃ hi maṃtraḥ ṭha ṭha ra bhāṣayā |
japosya dviguṇaṃ prokto homo naivātra vidyate ||

cirakālaṃ sa vai jīvet prāyo mṛtyu vibhetitaṃ |
prāyosya japa kartā tu nepālādau kvacit kvacit ||

nīlakaṇṭhepi bhūyāsaḥ parvatāṃtaśca rājanāḥ |
dviśataṃ triśataṃ cāpi vatsarāṇāṃ yathākramaṃ ||

jīvaṃti narayogīndrāstatra tatra guhāṃtare |
devīnātra bhavet sākṣāt pīṃḍīṃ jāpyā tadanaṃtaraṃ ||

svapne vadati sā devī ciraṃjīvī bhaveti hi |
maṃtriṇaṃ kṛtasaṃjāpyaṃ tato mṛtyu dinaṃ dhruvaṃ ||

tamākhyāti ca dhīraṃ hi manoyogaṃ prayacchati |
manoyogaṃ samāsādya saṃyogī jñāta kālakaḥ ||

kālaṃ vaṃcayate sohi vidrāvanmaraṇaṃ kṣaṇaṃ |
anubhūyaṃ tato maṃtrī punarutthiti māpnuyāt ||

punaḥ smarati saṃsāre yatkṛtaṃ sakalaṃ hi tat |
yuvāgalita pālityaḥ vālakāṃti manoramaḥ ||

jāyate yogamāyāvī punarjīvati vai śataṃ |
dvitrivāraṃ yathā kuryādevaṃ maṃtramahimnayā ||

vaudhānāmapyayaṃ maṃtra siddha āsīt purākila |
tatra śrīśaṃkarastebhyo gṛhṇādenaṃ valādapi ||

prāyaśo naiva japtavyo gṛhiṇāyaṃ manu dhruvaṃ |
nissaṃtatirbhavet sadyo yogī tasmādbhavedayaṃ ||

tasmādiyaṃ mahāvidyā japtavyai kākinā bhṛśaṃ ||

maṃtraḥ || 

ṭha ṭha laṃ śa la sorakle iṃjānī daśalakaṃrīdo ṭhaḥ ṭhaḥ || iti kuṃḍinīvidhiḥ 
|| atha madhuvāsinīvidhiḥ || 

madhumāsasitāṣṭamyāṃ gaudātīre vimānuṣe |
kuśatarpaṇa tīrthe hi latāgulmāṃtare dhruvaṃ ||

karaṃjatarutīre vā kiṃ vā kolamahī bhuvaḥ |
chāyāyāṃ samanurjapyaḥ sahasra navasaṃkhyayā ||

athavā madhu vṛkṣasya chāyāyaṃ hi vanāṃtare |
japedenaṃ manuṃ maṃtrī sahasra navasaṃkhyayā ||

godāvarī suvṛkṣasya siddhayogo mahānagha |
prajaptavyā tato devī prasiddhā madhuvāsinī ||

56b)

vāsaṃtī kusumairhomo madhupuṣpairathāpi vā |
karpūrā gurusaṃmiśraiḥ sahasraṃ homamucyate ||

madhunāmā mahākaścidyakṣovighnakarī dhruvaṃ |
tatrāyāti mahālolajihvālalana bhīṣaṇaṃ ||

māhiṣeṇa vidyāraṇena rudhirāpāna tatparaḥ |
vāmena pāṇinānyena surāpāna samārataḥ ||

jihve yaiva sa yakṣo hi latā vṛkṣādi gulmakān |
utpādya carvamāṇo hi bhakṣyaṃ dehīti bhāṣayā ||

saṃllayat sādhakendrasya mithyātrāsana tatparaḥ |
muṣṭiraktaṃ pradātavyaṃ maṃtriṇākarajaṃ dhruvaṃ ||

tatastasmin gate pakṣe devī vṛkṣatale tadā |
pratyakṣā jāyate tasya vasaṃtasya rasaṃyutā ||

dadāti maṃtriṇe tasmai kārmukaṃ puṣpanirmitaṃ |
vitasti mātramatule tadgṛhītvā tu sādhakaḥ ||

kāminī śatasaṃmoha catuḥṣaṣṭhi kalādharaḥ |
jāyatetha pṛthivyāṃ sa madano mūrtimāniva ||

catuḥṣaṣṭhi kalājñātaṃ na kasyādyāpi bhūtale |
manmathotha śivaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ pradyumna itaro mataḥ ||

catvāra eva saṃjātāścatuḥṣaṣṭhi kalādharāḥ |
paṃcamaḥ sasvayaṃ maṃtrī jāyate tatkalādharaḥ ||

dhyānaṃ ||

kusumaśaravasaṃtastūyamānā mṛgākṣī navarasamaya mūrti brahmasaukhya 
pravṛttiḥ |
kanakakamalapāṇirmohamāyā yaśaḥ śrīrmama hi hṛdayasadhye saṃvaset 
kāmadevī ||

maṃtraḥ || 

oṃ madhuvāsini kāmadevi klīṁ svāhā || 

asyaiva pratirūpaṃ hi maṃtro maithilabhāṣayā |
tena kāṃtavarāyāti trisaṃdhyaṃ japa iṣyate ||

na homo nāpi kālādi sādhanaṃ tasya vidyate |
dṛṣṭimātreṇa kāminyaḥ kāmayaṃti hi sādhakaṃ ||

tannāmāpi divārātraṃ japaṃti śatadhāstriyaḥ |
naranārī mahāprīti heturnānyanmahītale ||

prātilomyena saṃjapto bhāṣā maṃtro vasaṃtake |
caturdaśyāṃ śuklapakṣe caitre māsi nadītaṭe ||

tena devyati saṃprītā rājavaśyaṃ prayacchati |
rātraunāma gṛhītvā hi sādhyasya svayamā japet ||

57a)

tato devī tarhi sādhya svapnāṃte vadati sphuṭaṃ |
ayaṃ rājan devadattastesti pūjyo na saṃśayaḥ ||

nocettava bhaveddhāniriti sāsphuṭabhāṣiṇī |
iti svapnāṃtare sādhyaṃ sāvadatpatha devatā || 

maṃtraḥ || 

mādhavīmāhamarāṃ manogata rājavaśyajahanehopite haneṃkara ugu ihāṃ 
sarvasamartha klīṃ hrīṁ svāhā || iti madhuvāsinīvidhiḥ ||

atha maṃtharāmaṃtraḥ || ikṣuvāṭīvanāṃ tarhi guḍapākasya sthalaṃ hita tat || 

rasayaṃtrasamīpe hi racayitvā śubhāṃ sthalīṃ |
japet tatra manuṃ devyāmaṃtharāyaśade dvayā ||

ikṣukhaṃḍairdaśāṃśena homaṃ samyak samācaret |
mallāri ṣaṣṭhīrātrau hi japaḥ some prakīrtitaḥ ||

tataḥ sā maṃtharā devī prasīdati hi maṃtriṇe |
dadāditi madhupātraṃ hi divyamādhvīkamiśritaṃ ||

tatpūjayet trisaṃdhyaṃ hi tanmukhānmaṃtharā śivā |
mukhamātrābhi saṃvyaktā śubhāśubhavidhiṃ tadā ||

yadyacciṃtayate citte syānnaceti ca sā vadet |
yadā yadāti saṃkaṣṭaṃ jāyate maṃtriṇe dhruvaṃ ||

tadā tadā ca sā devī madhupātra prapūjanāt |
ityame veti vadati prītā sā jagadaṃvikā ||

dhyānaṃ ||

karevahaṃtīko daṃḍamaikṣavaṃ lolalocanāṃ |
japākusumaśoṇāṃgīṃ mama citte tu maṃtharā ||

maṃtraḥ ||

oṃ maṃthare ikṣu kṣitivāsini mameṣṭaṃ vada 2 bhuṃ dyaṃ maṃ svāhā || 

asyaiva pratirūpaṃ hi maṃtro mālava bhāṣayā |
tadardhaṃ tu japaḥ prokta pūrvokta vanamaṃḍale ||

rasayaṃtra samīpe tu bhūmipūjā viśeṣataḥ |
kartavyātha japāpuṣpa karavīra prasūnakaiḥ ||

kuṃkumaiścāpi siṃdūrai raktacaṃdanacaṃdanaiḥ |
yāvadā lohitaṃ vastu tāvadbhiḥ paripūjayet ||

tato yaṃtrāvidhau sthitvāyapaḥ kāryo yathāvidhiḥ |
tathaiva rasayaṃtrasya pūjā samyak prakīrtitāḥ ||

te naiva mūlamaṃtreṇa bhāṣā śaktiyutena hi |
tato yaṃtra mukhā devī vadati svaśubhāśubhaṃ ||

vārṣikaṃ ca parasyāpi tadvidhiḥ prativārṣikā |

57b)

atrāpi kālaḥ ṣaṣṭhī syānna ca vāravidhirmataḥ ||

yaṃtravaktrānna ceddevī svapne vāpi vadet tadā |

atha maṃtharā devyā maṃtraḥ || rasaniḥsaraṇayaṃtrarasapākayaṃtra 
madhyabhūmi saṃmārjya tatra jāpaḥ daśadvayamayutadvayaṃ daśaśabdo 
maṃtraḥ ayuta sāstratanāma || mallāri ṣaṣṭhīrātrau 
mallāri ṣaṣṭhīmārgaśīrṣasita ṣaṣṭhī tadrātrau someyaṃyaṃtra anuṣṭheyaḥ 
iks.u ṣaḍaiḥ daśāṃśena home kṛte sā devī prasīdati || āgatya maṃtriṇe 
madhupātraṃ amṛta miśrita madhu yutaṃ dadāti tatastatsaṃkaṭakāla 
trisaṃdhyaṃ tenaiva maṃtreṇa pūjayet || tato devī tanmadhupātra mukhān 
svamukhamāviḥ karoti || tato maṃtriṇaḥ saṃkaṣṭe *? maiva vidhayā hari 
bhaviṣyati || tvamevaṃ prakāraṃ kuru athavā tatra bhaviṣyati tvamasminnarthe 
yatnaṃ mā kurvīti vadati || tathā parasyāpi vadati || asyaiva pratirūpaṃ hi 
mālavabhāṣayā uktaḥ || tasya pūjā sthalaṃ rasayaṃtrasamīpe pūjā tu 
japāpuṣpakaravīrapuṣpaiḥ teneva vakṣyamāṇa bhāṣāmaṃtreṇa tathā 
kuṃkumacaṃdanabhūti yāvadā lohitaṃ tāvadbhiḥ pūjāsthalasya 
rasayaṃtrasyāpi pūrvavanmallāri ṣaṣṭhī rātrau japaḥ navāraniyamaḥ yasmin 
kasmiṃścidvāsarepi sā ṣaṣṭhī bhavatu tathāpi tatra bhāṣā maṃtro vaśyaṃ 
jāpyaḥ || tato devī rasayaṃtramukhānmaṃtriṇaḥ śubhāśubhaṃ vadati tata idaṃ 
vidhānaṃ maṃtriṇā prativarṣaṃ kartavyaṃ | tathā ca svaparasya abhilaṣitaṃ 
vadati || na vadati cettathā tadā svapne vā samāgatya vadatīti tātparyaṃ | 

maṃtraḥ || 

oṃ maṃtha harihmāre śubhaṣācuṃkahakaha hūṃ hūṃ maṃ thaṃ namaḥ || iti 
maṃtharāvidhiḥ || 

atha haṃsagāṇavidhiḥ ||
