hiraṇyakaśipu prāṇanāśakāle tithau dhruvaṃ |
saṃdhyāmārabhya japtavyo haṃsagāṇamanuḥ khalu ||

ayutārdhaṃ tato homaḥ padmākṣaistatra saṃmataḥ |

58a)

japo homaśca kartavyaḥ padmayukta sarastaṭe ||

tato haṃsasamārūḍhā śatacaṃdrasamaprabhā |
sā devī maṃtriṇe tasmai prasīdati sumoditā ||

padmākṣamālāmekāṃ hi dadāti svīyamaṃtriṇe |
tanmālā japato maṃtrī jāyate śāstrapāragaḥ ||

ajñātākṣaravargopi jāyate sa vṛhaspatiḥ ||

dhyānaṃ ||

śatacaṃdrasamajyotsnāṃ caṃdrārdhakṛtaśekharāṃ |
varadā bhayahastāṃtāṃsaṃseve haṃsagāṃ śivāṃ ||

maṃtraḥ || 

oṃ haṃsage vodhaṃ dehiro śrī svāhā || 

asyaiva pratimaṃtro hi jñeyaḥ saurāṣṭra bhāṣayā |
japastadvat samākhyāto nātra homa vidhirmataḥ ||

tatastu gaṇanā vidyāṃ su camatkārakāriṇīṃ |
dadāti maṃtriṇe tasmai rājasaṃsanmanoramāṃ ||

sa bhūbhūdhara vā rāśi carācaramidaṃ jagat |
bhāratī rūpataścāpi gaṇayatyāśu tatkṣaṇāt ||

iyaṃ tu bhāskarī vidyā devānāmapi durlabhā |
yasya kasyāpi bhāgyena vinā kasmān mukhī bhavet ||

guṇaṇāgaṇanātyaktā sadyo vadati niścitaṃ |
idametyevadityeva metāvat parimāṇakaṃ || 

maṃtraḥ || 

oṃ haṃṣā vāhaṇihmārūviṇuvā cū āṃpihāṃro svāhā || iti haṃsagāvidhiḥ ||

atha haṃsīvidhi ||

tuṃgabhadra taṭe ramye yatra lakṣmīśvaraḥ śivaḥ |
tatra snātvā nadītīre hyamāyāmayuta trayaṃ ||

ravivāsararātrau hi yajeddhaṃsīṃ maheśvarīṃ |
mustakaṃdaiḥ sahośīrairdaśāṃśaṃ homamācaret ||

tato devī sudhāmadhyān śubhāṃ tāsu manoramā |
vāmapāṇau svayaṃ haṃsīlālayaṃtī punaḥ punaḥ ||

dadāti maṃtriṇe śīghraṃ syāṭhikākṣaṃ manoramaṃ |
tasmin paśyati bhūtaṃ ca bhaviṣyaṃ vartamānakaṃ ||

tathā svasya parasyāpi sarvajño jāyate naraḥ ||

dhyānaṃ || 

sudhākarasamajyotsnāṃ śukaśobhitakarāṃ | 
vāme haṃsaṃ dadhānā hi pāṇau haṃsīṃ bhajāmitāṃ ||

maṃtrastu || 

oṃ haṃsī sarvavodhaṃ dehi 2 hlī ṭhaḥ svāhā || 

58b)

etasya pratirūpaṃ hi maṃtrohaṃḍīrabhāṣayā |
tena sadyo japaḥ prokto yatra kutrāpi vai tithau ||

kāmaṇīkaphalairamyairāraktairhomamācaret |
tato homāṃta samaye devī saubhāgyarūpiṇī ||

dadāti varamuttānaṃ haṭhayoga gṛhādikaṃ |
sadyo darśayatisvaira yogavān bhava putraka ||

iti datvā varaṃ devī jāyateṃ tarhitā tadā || 

maṃtraḥ || 

haṃsāpi yogāmāhi kalavalamilaṃ hraṃ hūṃ svāhā || 17 || iti haṃsīvidhiḥ ||

atha vicitrāvidhiḥ || 

citra ṛkṣa praveśe hi caturdaśyāṃ niśāṃtare |
sarastīre japenmaṃtraṃ vicitrāyā viśeṣataḥ ||

ayutaṃ kamalākṣaiśca homaṃ kuryād daśāṃśataḥ |
tato devī samāyāti vicitravasanāṃcalā ||

dadāti maṃtriṇe tasmai vicitravasanāṃcalaṃ |
tadaṃcalaṃ tu saṃpūjya rātrau saṃsthāpayed gṛhe ||

tadgṛhaṃ pūryate vastrai rājamaṃdiragairapi ||

dhyānaṃ ||

citracailāṃcala prītiṃ citramālyānulepanāṃ |
vicitrā bharaṇāṃ devīṃ vicitrāṃ bhajamānase ||

maṃtraḥ || 

vicitre citracailāṃcala dehi vāsaḥ pūraya 2 pūṃ svāhā || 32 || 

asyāpi pratirūpaṃ hi maṃtraḥ paṃcāla bhāṣayā |
tathaiva sa tu japtavyo maṃtrastatra niśāṃtare ||

tato devī prasannā sā dadāti hi karaṃḍakaṃ |
tasya pūjā vidhānena jāyate sarva ṛddhimān ||

na kadācid daridraṃ hi sanaraścānu bhūyati ||

maṃtraḥ || 

vicitrīttaṃ vicitra khela 2 ṇī prasanna śrīguru āṇasiddhāvī śrīṃ svāhā || 36 || 
iti vicitrāvidhiḥ ||

atha vidhipūrvakāvidhiḥ ||

kṛṣṇātīre mahātīrtha paṃcagaṃgā samāgame |
māghe māsi dvitīyāyāṃ kṛṣṇapakṣe niśāṃtare ||

kṛtvā tṛṇa kusūlaṃ hi nikṣipeddhi janāṃtare |
kṛtvā sāyāṃtakaṃ karmaṃ kusūlaṃ pūjayet tataḥ ||

tato devīṃ smaranmaṃtrī kusūlāṃtarviśeddhruvaṃ |
tatra vaddhāsano yogī śītavādhāmupekṣya hi ||

59a)

japet paṃca sahasraṃ hi devatāṃ vidhipūrvakāṃ |
tatastasmin kuśūlāṃta vidhinā sahasaṃyutāṃ ||

paṃcavaktrāṃ trinetrāṃ hi paśyedaṣṭa bhujāṃ śivāṃ |
tataḥ sā devatā tasmai dadāti hi kamaṃḍaluṃ ||

jalapūrṇaṃ tatastatstha jalenā secayeddhiyaṃ |
sanarastatkṣaṇādeva saptajanma samudbhavāṃ ||

jātiṃ vadati tatkālaṃ tat tatkarma karoti ca |
patitapālana ityetannāma tasya bhavediha ||

dhyānaṃ ||

amalanīraparīta kamaṇḍaluṃ svakarairdadhatī jagadaṃvikāṃ |
kanakakuṃḍalamaṃḍita gaṃḍaruka sucirāṃbhaje vidhipūrvakāṃ ||

maṃtraḥ || 

vidhipūrvake ācakranakhare hrīṃ srīṃ svāhā || 

asyāpi pratimaṃtrosti samyakkerala bhāṣayā |
tena sadyo hi sā devī jalāṭha kaṣṭiṃ dadāti hi ||

sa tu mādye sitāṣṭamyāṃ japtavyaḥ sarito jale ||

maṃtraḥ || 

araviṃdu idu amalamelamaṃgane vidhi vāhinīṃdu sīlaṃ svāhā || 24 || iti 
vidhipūrvakāvidhiḥ ||

atha vidhātrī || 

nadītīre tu yatrāste dhātrī vṛkṣo manoramaḥ |
saphalastasya bhūmau hi kārtike paurṇamāsike ||

somavāre tadā maṃtrī niśāyāṃ triśataṃ japet |
homodhātrā phalaiḥ kāryastatastattarute dhruvaṃ ||

jāyate tu mahāśabdaḥ prasannāsmīti śobhana |
tanmaṃtra paṭhanānmaṃtrī nīraṃ kṣīraṃ bhavediha ||

ityuktiṃ kila saṃbhūtvā sa paṭhenmaṃtramuttamaṃ |
nīropari tato nīraṃ jāyate kṣīramādanāt ||

dhyānaṃ ||

dhātrī taruśarīrasthāṃ vidhātrīṃ kamalāsanāṃ |
viśālalocanāṃ vaṃde nīrakṣīravidhāyinīṃ ||

maṃtraḥ || 

oṃ vidhātri nīrakṣīra vidhāyini viṭ svāhā || 16 ||

asyaiva pratimaṃtro hi varyovānara bhāṣayā |
tāvāneva japaḥ kāryaḥ na homavidhiriṣyate ||

lavaṇasuratīrthe hi japausya parikīrtitaḥ |
tasmin kāle mahāpuṇye vānaraḥ kaściduttamaḥ ||

āgatya sādhakendrāya dadyāt kāṃcanakuṃḍalaṃ |

59b)

tatkuṃḍalavalānmaṃtrī jāyate hi mahāvalī ||

śilāvṛkṣamahākūpotpāṭanaṃ kurute kṣaṇāt |
hastinaṃ vājinaṃ vāpi kṣaṇāt staṃbhayet kila ||

mahāmallagaṇānsaṃhho jayatyāśu na saṃśayaḥ ||

maṃtraḥ || 

hili vili ke ḍe ke ke ḍe bhīṃ vīṃ bhuṃ svāhā || 14 || iti vidhātrīvidhiḥ ||

athavainateyākṣī ||

śrāvaṇe māsi nāgānāṃ paṃcamīyā prakīrtitā |
tasyāṃ japenmahāmaṃtrī rātrau vālmīka bhūmiṣu ||

ayutaṃ vainate yākṣī homasyānmātu liṃgakaiḥ |
tataḥ sā vainate yākṣī prasannā maṃtriṇe khalu ||

dadāti gāruḍīṃ vidyāṃ sarvasarpaviṣāpahāṃ |
sarpāṃgajāti kathanā sarpadaṣṭasu nṛtyakāṃ ||

sarpākarṣaṇa śaktiṃ ca mahātakṣaka darśanaṃ |
anyamaṃtri sahasrāṇi na jayaṃtiha tatparaḥ ||

dhyānaṃ || 

kamalāsanāṃ hi sarpādi veṣṭitāṃ viṃdhyavāsinīm dhyāyāmi vainate 
yākṣīṃ viṣadoṣa harāṃvikāṃ || 

maṃtraḥ || 

oṃ vainateyākṣi sarpa sevite nāgadevi sphīṃ svāhā || 18 ||

asyāstu pratimaṃtrā hi mahāsiddhi pradāyakāḥ |
gauḍaśrīhaṭṭa śrīkāmabhāṣābhiḥ sumanoharāḥ ||

sadyo gāruḍa cailaṃ hi tadvalāt saṃjayaṃtite |
sarpadaṣṭa pranṛtyaṃ hi tadvārā jāti bhāṣaṇaṃ ||

viṣavelāpranirdhāmaḥ nirviṣa praharādayaḥ |
janaṃti maṃtriṇaḥ sarve sarvadeśagatā imāḥ ||

vidyā pratyayakāriṇyo bhaviṣyaṃti varānane |
gurūpadeśena vinā sarvaṃ syāt tu nirarthakaṃ ||

atreyaṃ gāruḍī vidyā vainate yākṣi nāmataḥ || 

etasyānuṣṭhānena gāruḍino jāyaṃte sahasraśo maṃtriṇaḥ || tatra gāruḍavidyā 
sarpaviṣārpaharaṇe sarpadhāraṇaṃ | sarpadṛṣṭasya śarīrāt śuddha 
nṛtyagānādi | tathā sarpadaṣṭasya mukhena jātyādi kathanaṃ | sarpasya viṣavelā 
nirṇayaḥ nirviṣapraharati nirṇayaḥ | tathā sarpastaṃbhaḥ sarpākarṣaṇamityādi 
gāruḍakhela || he varānane pārvati maṃtriṇaḥ siddhiṣyaṃtīti pārvatīṃ 
pratiśivenopadiṣṭāṃ tataḥ || ete prakārāḥ sarve etasya maṃtrasya saṃtyeva 
sarvadeśeṣu lokaprasiddhāḥ ||

60a)

iti vainateyākṣīvidhiḥ || 

atha rūpā ||

āṣāḍhe māsi rātrau hi kṛṣṇapakṣe'ṣṭamī tithau |
sagarbhīstrī citābhūmāvathavāraṇa bhūmiṣu ||

śastra naṣṭācitā bhūmāvayaṃ jāpyo manuḥ kila |
ayutaṃ ca japaḥ proktaḥ pāmarīvījaguggulaiḥ ||

homo daśāṃśataḥ proktastato homāṃtamāgatā |
yā yatragata himādriṃ laṃghayennātrasaṃśayaḥ ||

abhūmicārī lokeṣu jāyate yogavānasau ||

dhyānaṃ ||

kuṭajānāṃ vanārūḍha rūpasaubhāgyasuṃdarī |
yoginī mama cittestu kuṭajākṣī manoramā || 

maṃtraḥ ||

kuṭajākṣi kaṃvalaṃ dehi 2 bhīṃdhaṃ svāhā || 15 ||

asyāpi pratirūpaṃ hi kugarairala bhāṣayā |
tathaiva sa tu japtavyo rātrau tatra tithau dhruvaṃ ||

dadāti sā jalastaṃbhaṃ devatā kuṭajākṣikā ||

maṃtraḥ || 

iralaṃgahū iti kāminī bhuvaṃ || 17 || iti kuṭajākṣī ||

atha kaṃkarīvidhiḥ || 

avṛṣṭi kāle rātrau hi ravau nadyāṃ jale kila |
prajapan kaṃkarī devīmayutaṃ hi tataḥ paraṃ ||

prabhāte vṛṣṭirāyāti sā hi paṃcadināvadhi |
ahorātraṃ tato bhūmīrāpūrṇā nīradhārayā ||

dhyānaṃ || 

kaṃkarīṃ varuṇāpāṇaṃ dhyāyejjala tanuṃ śivāṃ |
vidyucchata svarūpāṃ tāṃ ghoramārjanabhīṣaṇāṃ ||

maṃtraḥ || 

kaṃkarījalaṃ devījalaṃ pūraya 2 dhaṃ dhaṃ ||

asyaiva pratirūpaṃ hi maṃtraḥ kā urabhāṣayā |
tathaiva phaladaḥ sopi japtaḥ sadyo hi maṃtriṇāṃ ||

atra sadyo japamātraṃ tataḥ phalado bhavati || na tu homādi japasaṃkhya niyamaḥ || 
adyāpi malli deśasya pratīti sarvasaṃmatā || 

maṃtraḥ || 

hili kili kaṃkarī kāmākṣā hamasamamahīmaṃḍalapāṇīthā uthā 
udhaṃrīdhaṃrī svāhā || iti kaṃkarīvidhiḥ ||

atha śubhaṃkarī ||

varadāyāstaṭe ramye dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśi dhruvaṃ |
māsibhādrapade ṣaṣṭhyāṃ kṛṣṇāyāṃ hi niśāṃtare ||

60b)

kṛta saṃdhyāvidhiṃ samyak samāhitamanāḥ kila |
karavīradrumāṃ yatra nirguṃḍī vanameva vā ||

tasmin khanitra vidhinā kṛtakīlakaropaṇaḥ |
prajapedayutaṃ maṃtraṃ karavīra prasūnakaiḥ ||

āraktai kīla homasyāt tato devī manoramā |
āyāti divyarūpeṇa kalikāmavimohinī ||

nīrājayati taṃ devī svahastena ca maṃtriṇaṃ |
tatastaṃ maṃtriṇe divyānmogānāśu dadāti sā ||

yadā yadā hi citte sau yaṃ yaṃ kāmaṃ karoti ca |
taṃ tamā pūrayet sadyo viṣayā pūrayeddhisā ||

sraksugaṃdha kalānārī nirmāṇa kurute kṣaṇāt ||

dhyānaṃ || 

kalākalāpaṃ paripūrayaṃtī vibhāvayaṃtī viṣayānanekān | nārīnarendrānapi 
mohayaṃtī sāmānasemestu śubhaṃkarī śrīḥ || 

maṃtraḥ || 

oṃ śubhaṃkari paradevate mameṣṭaṃ dehi 2 śuṃbhaṃ śrī svāhā || 32 || 

asyāpi pratirūpaṃ hi prāyaḥ paiśāca bhāṣayā |
yatra kutrāpi deśesau tanmāse tattithau niśi ||

tathaiva phaladāsāsyādayutaṃ japamiṣyate |
drākṣāphalairbhaveddhomaṃ tathā siddhirbhavet tadā ||

maṃtraḥ || 

mili 2 kili 2 haleṃ śubhaṃkari kāmidaṃgaśca dehi 2 klīṃ || 24 || iti 
śubhaṃkarīvidhiḥ ||

atha śatanādāvidhiḥ ||

māsi śrāvaṇake māyāṃ rātrau dūra nadītaṭe |
navapūraparikrāṃte yayogarjanayāyute ||

japet tatra manuṃ devyāḥ sahasrāṣṭaṃ yathāvidhiḥ |
amṛtā mūlaparṇaiśca kṛte home daśāṃśataḥ ||

tato rātrau hi jāyaṃte maṃtriṇaḥ pratyayāḥ puraḥ |
vīṇā kinnarīkāyāvapinākī kūrmayaṃtrikāḥ ||

ityādinā śataṃ nādā jāyaṃtenyepi bhīṣaṇāḥ |
tataḥ sā yoginī rūpā vakṣovīṇā vinodinī ||

navanādakalāviṣṭā pratyakṣā maṃtriṇaḥ kila |
yogamudrāṃ svayaṃ tasmai dadāti kilamaṃtriṇe ||

sadyaḥ kuṃḍalinī mārgaṃ sā darśayati maṃtriṇe |

61a)

jñātasvānu bhāvo maṃtrī svānaṃdanaripūrita ||

sarvakāmamayaṃ jitvā brahmī bhūya sa tiṣṭhati ||

dhyānaṃ || 

vīṇānāda sphuradāgha bhāvavikaṃpayaṃtī kilakuṃḍale sve || sā yoginī 
viṣṇutayā śivākhyā citte madīye śatanādikāsā || 

maṃtraḥ || 

oṃ śatanāde yoginiyogaṃ dehi 2 hrīṃ hrūṃ svāhā || 16 || 

asyāpi pratimaṃtrosti puṇyaḥ pāṃḍīrabhāṣayā |
saṃsāra viṣayāśaktiṃ tyaktvā yogī bhavennaraḥ ||

dadāti tasmai sā devī kaṃthāmekāṃ manoramāṃ |
tayā sa vajradehī syāt kāla kalpaṃ hi jīvati ||

maṃtraḥ || 

śatanāde arma alamekāṃlanatu iḍḍarukuṃḍunnu śrāṃ śrīṃ hrīṃ kaḥ || iti 
śatanādāvidhiḥ || 

atha netraramyā || 

kānane karavīrāṇāṃ rātrau vaiśākhamāsi hi |
caturdaśyāṃ japed devīṃ netraramyāṃ śatatrayaṃ ||

bhaumastu vāsaraḥ proktastathā vā śukravāsaraḥ |
ghṛtākta guggulairhome devī sāpya prayacchati ||

dadāti maṃtriṇe tasmai svāṃjanaṃ netravodhakaṃ |
nidhībhūmi gataṃ vastu dūradeśagataṃ tathā ||

ālokayati sa sadyo bhavati bhūpatiḥ || 

dhyānaṃ || 

vivodhayaṃtī pihitaṃ hi vastu māyāmayī paṃkajanetra ramyā | 
pītāṃvarā svarṇasuratnamālā puroktame saṃprati netraramyāḥ ||

maṃtraḥ || 

oṃ netraramye aṃjanaṃ dehi 2 nidhidarśaya 2 paṭalaṃ dūrī kuru 2 maṃthaṃ 
svāhā || 32 || 

asyāstu pratimaṃtro hi kāśmīra deśa bhāṣayā |
tathaiva phaladaḥ proktastathā corapravodhakaḥ ||

maṃtraḥ || 

sohi tanaya nārī mohibhālaṃ malakāla vodhakara bhrīṃ dhrīṃ svāhā || iti 
netraramyāvidhiḥ ||

atha paṃkajākṣīvidhiḥ ||

vasaṃtakāle gaṃgāyāṃ bhāgīrathyāṃ niśāṃtare |
aṣṭamyāṃ caitramāse hi kṛṣṇepakṣe japennaraḥ ||

paṃkajākṣīṃ mahāvidyāṃ palāśānāṃ vanāṃtare |
atra bhaumotha vā śukro vihito vāsaro mataḥ ||

61b)

japaḥ sahasraṃ tritayaṃ pālāśairhomamiṣyate |
tato devī mahārātrau gate sati moramā || 

pratyakṣā maṃtriṇe śīghraṃ dadāti phalamuttamaṃ |
jarāmaraṇa rāhityaṃ tatkālaṃ bhakṣite sati ||

phalaṃ tasmin samāpnoti sadguru prārthanā yutaḥ ||

atha dhyānaṃ || 

ālolanetrāṃ kusumeṣu jīvasaṃdāyinīṃ saṃprati paṃkajākṣīṃ || 
dhyāyāmi sarvārthakarīṃ bhavānīṃ punarbhaveyāṃ parivārayaṃtī ||

maṃtraḥ || 

oṃ paṃkajākṣi amṛtaphalaṃ dehi 2 svīṃ svāhā || 17 ||

asyāpi pratimaṃtroyaṃ proktaścotkalabhāṣayā |
sa sadyo jvarapīḍāṃ hi haratyā vṛttibhiḥ kila ||

daśabhiḥ parijaptaśca śītapīḍāṃ nivartayat |
yatra kvāpi japaḥ proktaḥ kasmiṃścit samayetha vā ||

kṛttrimāṇi haratyāśu kṛtyādīni sa kṛnmanuḥ | 

oṃ paṃkajākṣī gomāmotheṃyājaratīya haragobhī bhūṃ bhrūṃ svāhā || iti 
paṃkajākṣīvidhiḥ || 

atha payodinīvidhiḥ || 

varṣāsucaya dāṣṭamyāṃ rohiṇī ṛṣyasaṃgamaḥ |
bhaumo vṛhaspatirvātha śukraḥ syāt tatra sādhakaḥ ||

rātrau snānavidhiṃ kṛtvā sarastīre manorame |
ayutaṃ prajaped devīṃ pāyasairhomamācaret ||

daśāṃśena tato devī sākṣāt sātu payodinī |
dadāti karakāmekāṃ maṃtriṇe toṣamāgatā ||

agnidāsya sāṃ mukhye sā kṛtā karakā yadā |
tadā vṛṣṭiḥ patet tatra tatkālaṃ śamate hi saḥ ||

dhyānaṃ ||

varṣaṃtī jalaviṃdūn hi meghamālā manoramā |
śyāmāṃvara parīdhānā me cittestu payodinī ||

maṃtraḥ || 

oṃ payodini jaladhārādhare agniṃśamaya vāṃḍavaṃśamaya ḍhrīṃ htraiṁ śrīṃ 
namaḥ || 27 || 

asyaiva pratirūpaṃ hi maṃtro vaṃgālabhāṣayā |
sa japtastatkṣaṇādeva jalavṛṣṭi karoti hi ||

vāḍavāgniṃ mahāgniṃ sthalāgniṃ sarvato mukhaṃ |
nāśayet tatkṣaṇādeva āvṛtyā siddhimāgataḥ ||

yatra kvāpi japaḥ prokto japosya jaladāgame |
ayutaṃ ca tataḥ siddhastvekā vṛtyā hi siddhidā ||

62a)

maṃtraḥ || 

aligali āhe māpayodinikyamatakari tu kari tu marakāryapānīthā uguthā ugu 
āgniṭā tu jhā u ḍhrīṃ ḍhrīṃ svāhā || iti payodinīvidhiḥ || 

atha pāṃḍavīvidhiḥ || 

vatsarādau ca yā proktā pratiśukrasya vāsare |
tasyāṃ rātrau japenmaṃtraṃ pāṃḍavyā ayutāvadhi ||

kausuṃbha kusumairhomairdaśāṃśena kṛte sati |
prasannā jagatāṃ dhātrīṃ pāṃḍavī pītavāsasā ||

pādastaṃbhaṃ karotyāśu vairiṇo dveṣakāriṇaḥ ||

dhyānaṃ || 

pītāṃvarāpītamālyā pītavarṇa priyā sadā |
pretāsanā tadā devī citte me pāṃḍavī bhavet ||

maṃtraḥ || 

oṃ pāṃḍavī vagale vagalāmukhi śatroḥ pādaṃ staṃbhaya 2 klīṃ dhrīṃ 
bhrūṃ varaṃ sphrīṃ svāhā || 22 || 

asyā hi pratimaṃtroyaṃ vidyate pāṃḍyabhāṣayā |
gatiḥ staṃbhakaraḥ sadyaḥ śukra pratipadi dhruvaṃ ||

yadā kadāpi japtavyaḥ sadyaḥ siddhikaro hi saḥ |
atra pūrvavadayutaṃ japaḥ || pūrvavat pratipadi japasya naisyatyo ukta idānīṃ 
tadvaiparītya yadā kadāpi pratipadi śukravāsare japosya vihito phalaṃ 
pūrvavadeva || 

maṃtraḥ || 

pāṃḍavi iṃdu agamaṃḍalapaṃṭī kālukuṃṭimāḍḍadrī sphrīṃ svāhā || 24 || 
iti pāṃḍavīvidhiḥ || 

atha pṛthumadhyāvidhiḥ || 

ṣaṣṭhyāṃ kṛṣṇe kārtike hi svāmikārtika saṃnidhau |
guhāyāṃ cūtavṛkṣasya tale sthitvā hi sādhakaḥ ||

bhūmiśuddhiṃ vidhāyāśu kīlakānanuropya ca |
pṛthu madhyāṃjaperdevīṃ sahasraṃ sādhakottamaḥ ||

cūtaparṇaiḥ kṛte home daśāṃśena sugaṃdhibhiḥ |
miśritairagarūdbhūte tailena ca yathāvidhiḥ ||

atra āmraparṇairagarutaila miśritairhomaḥ cakāro viśeṣaṇa dvaya 
samuccayārthaḥ ||

tato devī pṛthu madhyā prasīdati hi maṃtriṇe |
dadāti pīṭhamekaṃ hi bhāminī mohakārakaṃ ||

tatropaviṣṭopi naro narakenāpi dṛśyate |

62b)

tatpīṭhaṃ paṃcabhūtāni vahaṃti śirasi svayaṃ ||

tadā rūḍhaḥ sādhakosau jāyate khecaraḥ sadā ||

dhyānaṃ || 

unmatta gajagāṃ devīṃ sthūlāṃgīṃ kanaka priyāṃ |
kārtikeya guhākhelāṃ pṛthu madhyāṃ bhajāmyahaṃ ||

maṃtraḥ || 

pṛthu madhye mānavihastini pīṭhaṃ dehi aṃganāṃ pramohaya vāyavīya gatiṃ 
dehi 2 phūḥ phūḥ ṭhaḥ || 

asyā tu pratimaṃtrosti saihilaika svabhāṣayā |
bhāṣayā sa tu japtavya kārtikeya guhāṃtare ||

sahasra tritayaṃ tasya na homo parikīrtitaḥ |
pāṃḍukāṃsaṃ dadātyāśū mā devī maṃtriṇe kila ||

maṃtraḥ || 

pṛthu madhyadhi ilaguneṃguṇa kālukadaṃlu iṃcuḍohāhaḥ || atra saihilaikasvayā 
bhāvayeti siṃhaladeśajā bhāṣā proktā || iti pṛthumadhyāvidhiḥ || 

atha pārthivāvidhiḥ ||

nadītīre vṛṣṭikāle caturdaśyāṃ niśāṃtare |
kūlaṃ khanitvā kuharaṃ kartavyaṃ yugasaptakaṃ ||

tatrāṃdhakārapakṣe hi dīpaśūnyedarī gṛhe |
pārthivāṃ prajapenmaṃtrī sahasraṃ daśapaṃca ca ||

homaḥ kadalikākāṃḍaiḥ komalaiśca daśāṃśataḥ |
tatodhva kāle sā devī dīpajvālā sphuradruciḥ ||

dadāti maṃtriṇe śaktiṃ pṛthivyaṃtaravāriṇīṃ |
śaileṣu vivareṣūccaiḥ sughane pṛthivītale ||

kīṭavadbhramate maṃtrī yāvajjalamasau sadā |
tatra tatrātyaṃtamāścaryaṃ paśyati prīti pūrvakaṃ ||

jarāmaraṇa rāhityaṃ prāpnoti pṛthivītale ||

dhyānaṃ || 

pṛthivītalasaṃcāra śālinī vāyumālinī |
bhajāmi pārthivāṃ devīṃ tāruṇyaika pradāṃ śivāṃ ||

maṃtraḥ || 

oṃ pārthivi pṛthivītala saṃcāriṇi vāyumālini tāruṇyaṃ kuru 2 vaṃdhaṃ 
svāhā || 

asyāpi pratirūposti maṃtraḥ piṃgalabhāṣayā |
tathaiva phaladaḥ proktaḥ japo rātrau prakīrtitaḥ ||

aṣṭamyāṃ kṛṣṇapakṣe hi bhaumosmin vā sarottamaḥ ||

63a)

maṃtraḥ || 

kili 2 hili 2 mili 2 colaṃ rīṭhīṃ kuṃ svāhā || iti pārthivāvidhiḥ ||

atha paṃkavāsinī ||

vaiśākhe śuṣka sarasi kānanejana varjite |
kiṃcityaṃ kilite kiṃcijjalasthala manorame ||

saptarātraṃ japenmaṃtraṃ divasaṃ sūryamaṇḍalāt |
lakṣasaṃkhyaṃ japaḥ prokto homastatra tatpuṣpakaiḥ ||

daśāṃśena vidhātavyastatasāpaṃkavāsinī |
dadāti maṃtriṇe tuṣṭā trijagadvaśakāraṇaṃ ||

kesaraṃ ca sugaṃdhaṃ ca maṃtrī tattilakī sadā |
vasayedbhuvanaṃ sadyo rājānaṃ devatāstathā ||

dhyānaṃ || 

paṃkavāsini śive śiva iti smaravaktra nayanāṃvujalīle |
mānase mamavaśasmara devi pratyahaṃ kamalakānanasaṃsthe ||

maṃtraḥ || 

oṃ paṃkavāsini paṃkajavanivanadevate kesaraṃ dehi siddhiṃ kuru 2 klīṃ śrīṃ 
svāhā || 

asyā tu pratirūpaṃ hi maṃtraṃ saubhilla bhāṣayā |
sadyo mohana vidyaiṣā trirātramayutaṃ japet ||

tasminkāle hi divase japaḥ sarasi saṃmataḥ ||

maṃtraḥ || 

iṃdu kuṃḍa navala puru iṃcumāḍiṃcuropini daśa vaṃ vaṃ vaḥ || iti 
paṃkavāsinīvidhiḥ ||

atha varānanāvidhiḥ || 

rājyarathyādvāre bhaumavāsare saptamyāṃ kṛṣṇapakṣe | 

japedvarānanāṃ devīṃ trisahasraṃ śuciḥ sthitaḥ |
śaṃkhaiḥ kapardakai homo daśāṃśena tato mataḥ || 

tato varāṇanā devī sakṛt strībhiṣito dhruvaṃ |
dadāti maṃtriṇe caikaṃ kapardakamanuttamaṃ ||

tadā tu patato maṃtrī vāṇijyavidhi jīvanaḥ |
kapardakaṃ sthāpayeddhikanādīnāṃ kusūlake ||

tridināvadhi dhānyaṃ tayāvadvikrayakārakaḥ |
yathecchaṃ tāvadā sveta punastrettridināvadhi ||

rāvaṃdhānyāṃtare kṣiptaṃstadakṣayaṃ karoti saḥ ||

dhyānaṃ || 

sauṃdaryāmṛtasandoha sārībhūtāmivā parāṃ |
vivarddhinī sthirāṃ devīṃ sā bhajettāṃ varānanāṃ ||

maṃtraḥ || 

varāṇane vāmalocani paṇyapālini mālini 2 vrūṃ dhūṃ dhīṃ svāhā ||

asyāpi pratimaṃtrosti divyaḥ pārvata bhāṣayā |
sa tathaiva ca japtavyaḥ paṇyadvāra niśāvidhau ||

sarvaṃ dviguṇaṃ yāti paṇyadravyaṃ gṛhasthitaṃ |

63b)

maṃtraḥ || 

kālivāli sohita vaṭaya 2 tūṃdhī svāhā || iti varānanā ||

atha vidhuśreṣṭhā || 

caṃdragrahe somavāre citrānakṣatrasaṃgame |
yāvadvidhu pramoca syāt tāvanmaṃtraṃ japejjaleṃ ||

tato devī vidhuśreṣṭhālokavismayakārakaṃ |
dadāti maṃtriṇe samyak tāṭaṃkaṃ savyakarṇagaṃ ||

pūrṇacaṃdraprabhāśobhitvamāṃpūrṇāṃ karoti tat |
pratijñā vaśago yogī svabhāge kṣapayeddhi tat ||

tato devī pakṣapātātūsmiṃtadavalaṃvane |
tato kāpi vadaṃtyevamamāyāṃ caṃdramā kutaḥ ||

dhyānaṃ || 

caṃdramaṃḍalasaṃsthātāṃ vidhuśreṣṭhāṃ viyadratāṃ |
kāsmīra cārutā ṭaṃkāṃ dhyāyāmi śivavallabhāṃ ||

maṃtraḥ || 

vidhuśreṣṭhe viyadgate mānaṃ pūraya karṇatā ṭaṃkaṃ dehi 2 thaṃ dhrūṃ 
hsrīṃ svāhā || 

asyāpi pratirūpaṃ hi maṃtro vaideha bhāṣayā || 

maṃtraḥ || 

cādajīvani cāṃdanirīrapanī dīpamālakhaṃmī dehi hsrīṃ hsrīṃ svāhā || atra 
japatithi kālasyānuktaṃ tvena pūrvoktānyeva tithikāla phalāni || iti vidhuśreṣṭā 
|| 

atha vāmalocana ||

vāmāyāḥ saṃgamāt pūrvaṃ prajapedvāmalocanāṃ |
śatamātraṃ pūrṇamāsyāṃ viśākhāditya saṃgame ||

sadyaḥ prasannā devī sā vīryā staṃbhaṃ dadāti hi |
apikāṃtāśatāsaṃgame nāsau skhalati mānavaḥ || 

dhyānaṃ || 

rati devī rati prītiṃ kāmakīrtiṃ manoramāṃ |
mama kāmapradāṃ sadyaḥ prabhaje vāmalocanāṃ ||

maṃtraḥ || 

īlīṃ bhīraṃ vaṃ vāma locane vīryaṃ staṃbhaya 2 nādaṃ mā kuru 2 svāhā || 

asyaiva pratirūpaṃ hi maṃtraḥ śikharibhāṣayā |
mahānadī taṭe japto veśyā vidrāvaye kṣaṇāt ||

pūrvavajjapasaṃkhyā syāddhomaḥ padmairihoditaḥ || 

maṃtraḥ || 

vāmalocanimāye ma isadāre gaṇaṃ hāṃ haṃ svāhā || iti vāmalocanā || 

atha citrākṣī || 

akṣa?yākhyā tṛtīyāyāṃ uddiśya jalakuṃbhake |

64a)

yamaṃ varuṇamiṃdraṃ ca taṣṭhīrasya tu saṃsthitaṃ ||

kuṃbhāpūraṇa kāle hi madhyāhne prajapenmanuṃ |
atha brahmaviṣṇvīśāye pūrvakuṃbhadevatāḥ ||

tānsarvānadhiruhyaiṣā japtavyā cāpagā taṭe |
triśataṃ ca japaḥ prokto homaḥ sīvaphalena hi ||

tato ghaṭamukhādevī pratyakṣā vadati sphuṭaṃ |
akṣayaṃ kurute dravyaṃ maṃtriṇe nātra saṃśayaḥ ||

tṛtīyā somasaṃyuktā tṛtīyā ravi saṃyutā |
citrā ṛkṣa bhavedyogastadāsau japa ucyate ||

atra cendrādayo devāḥ pūrvaṃ kuṃbhasthānadhiruhyatiṣṭhatītyekā kalpanā | 
brahmaviṣṇvavīśeti nipāta | te ye devatā kuṃbhetānādhiruhyatiṣṭhatītya 
parāvarṇanā || 

dhyānaṃ || 

iṃdrādi pretamaulisthāṃ kalaśāṃkaramālinīṃ || 
citrākṣīṃ citraveṣāṃtāṃ saṃbhajet parameśvarīṃ || 

maṃtraḥ || 

citrākṣi citrarūpe iṃdrādi pretasaṃsthe prasīda 2 śrīṃ svāhā || 

asyāpi pratimaṃtrosau jñātavyaḥ kolabhāṣayā | 
madhyāhne sa tu japtavyastattithau tatphalapradaḥ || 

maṃtraḥ || 

citraṃ cakhusīmāradhana apārabhaurīṃ svāhā || 16 || iti citrākṣī ||

atha citrakaṃṭhī || 

vasaṃte śuklapakṣe hi caitre māse niśāvidhau |
caturdaśyāṃ japenmaṃtra citrakaṃṭhe phalapradaṃ ||

japaḥ sahasra tritayaṃ homo daśaguṇo mataḥ |
madhūka kusumaiḥ paścāddhomosau parikīrtitaḥ ||

tato devīmudaṃyātā dadāti kilamaṃtriṇe |
kokilasvaramatyaṃta mohanaṃ jagatāmapi ||

api pakṣī mṛgādīnāṃ mohanaṃ susvaro mataḥ ||

dhyānaṃ || 

cūtāṃkuraṃ karṇayuge vahaṃtī vāmaṃ ca ramyāramaṇī śivasya || 
sā mānase me sadā śubhāsyā trailokya pūjyā kila citrakaṇṭhī || 

maṃtraḥ || 

citrakaṃṭhī citranādasvaraṃ dehi 2 bhīṃ rīṃ svāhā || 17 || 

asyaiva pratimaṃtro hi prāyaśo marubhāṣayā |
tathaiva phaladaḥ proktaḥ tatkāle parisevitaḥ ||

maṃtraḥ || 

sāmhārogalūṃ citrakeli vāṃsaṃ svāhā || iti citrakaṃṭhī || 

64b)

atha cihnagamyā || 

citrāyāṃ kṛṣṇapakṣe hi rātrau siddhipradāṃ japet |
caturthyāṃ cihnagamyātāmayutaṃ caṃdravāsare ||

na homo nāpi pūjyānyā devī sākṣāt priyaṃvadā |
tato dadāti tasmai sā maṃtriṇe varamuttamaṃ ||

navarātrau gṛhe samyak divyānnaṃ yāvadīpsitaṃ |
tāvad dadāmihe maṃtri divyabhogānapi dhruvaṃ ||

dhyānaṃ || 

kalaśamamṛtapūrṇaṃ pāṇināsaṃ vahaṃtī subhaga kamalamālāṃ vibhratī 
cāru kaṇṭhī || mama hṛdaya manojñā sarvadā rātriramyā phalatu mama 
saṃbhogāt sarvadā cihnagamyā || 

maṃtraḥ || 

devikamale cihna gamye prasīda śrīṃ svāhā || 

asyāpi pratirūpaṃ hi maṃtraṃ vaṃgālabhāṣayā |
sa rātrau vaṭamūleṣu japtavyaḥ kila maṃtriṇā ||

japto śatamātraṃ hi tataḥ priya devatā |
nityaṃ tasmai dadātyāśu divyabhogāṃ manoramāṃ ||

maṃtraḥ || 

cihnagamyā śataradevī śatarasevyāmotheṃ dehi 2 pāra hu huṃ || iti cihnagamyā 
||

atha trilocanā ||

trilocanā mahādevī dvādaśyāṃ śanivāsare |
japedrātrau sahasraṃ hi homosya tu samāhitaḥ ||

nārikelairdaśāṃśena kartavyo vaṃśavṛddhi kṛt |
tato devī maṃtriho hi dadāti phalamuttamaṃ ||

tatphalādānataṃstasya patnī putravatī bhavet |
api vaṃdhyāpi sā nārī jāyate putra śālinī ||

asyā hi pratirūpaṃ hi maṃtraṃstrigulabhāṣayā |
tathaiva sa tu japtavyo mṛtaputravatsalā dhruvaṃ ||

jīvet putrā bhavennārī maṃtro jāpyastasyayā kilaṃ ||

maṃtraḥ || 

māmamma ili vindu iṃdu vadakisodhadhaṃ || iti trilocanāvidhiḥ || 

śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ || śrīdevyuvāca || 

mahācīna kramācāraḥ sūcito na prakāśitaḥ |
idānīṃ kathayeśāna yadi snehosti māṃ prati ||

65a)

iti pṛṣṭaḥ purā devyā kailāsaśikhare haraḥ |
ciṃtayā māsa manasā kiṃcidā kalite kṣaṇaḥ ||

iyamutkaṃṭhitā bhūyo yanmāṃ prerayati priye |
cīnācāra kramaṃ vaktuṃ tatprakāśya kathaṃ mayā ||

iti guptataraḥ sopasācāraḥ siddhidāyakaḥ |
strīṇāṃ caṃcalayā vuddhyā kathaṃ goptaṃ hi śakyate ||

iti saṃciṃtya manasā punarāha maheśvarī |
mahācīna kramācāraṃ vrūhi me parameśvara ||

śrīśiva uvāca || 

alaṃ yatnairalaṃ yatnairalaṃ yatnairmaheśvari |
cīnācārakramaṃ śrotuṃ viraktā bhava pārvati ||

eṣa eva mahācāro na prakāśyaṃ kadācana |
guhyādguhyataraṃ sākṣāt tatvajñānamayaḥ śive ||

strī svabhāvena bhavatī saśvanmāṃ paripṛcchasi |
lakṣavāraṃ vāritāsi tathāpi śrotumicchasi ||

śrīpārvatyuvāca ||

yadi cīna kramācāraṃ name kathayasi prabho |
prāṇatyāgaṃ kariṣyāmi puratastena saṃśayaḥ ||

ityuktaḥ satataṃ śaurayo rudraḥ kāruṇiko mahān |
mahācīna kramācāraṃ gadituṃ saṃpracakrame ||

sarvadā gopya evāyamācāraḥ siddhidāyakaḥ |
tavānurodho devāhaṃ kathayāmi maheśvari ||

brahmaṇe mānasaḥ putro vasiṣṭhotīva saṃyamī |
tārāmārādhayā māsa purānīlācale muniḥ ||

japansatāriṇīṃ vidyāṃ kāmākhyā yonimaṃḍale |
gamayāmāsa varṣāṇāmayutaṃ dhyāna tatparaḥ ||

varṣeṣu tena tatraiva ciramārādhitā satī |
nānugrahaṃ cakārāsau tārāsaṃsāratāriṇī ||

athāsau pitaraṃ gatvā brahmāṇaṃ parameṣṭhinaṃ |
kopeṇa jvalito vidyāṃ tatyājayaturaṃtike ||

dvādaśādityasaṃkāśaṃ tapobhirjvalitaṃ muniḥ |

65b)

brahmāsānu nayaṃ prāha śṛṇu putravaco mama ||

tatvajñānamayīṃ vidyāṃ tārāṃ bhuvanatāriṇīṃ |
ārādhayatvaṃ suciraṃ manuvignena cetasā ||

asyāḥ prasādādevāhaṃ bhuvanāni caturdaśa |
sṛjāmi caturo vedān kalpayāmi ca līlayā ||

etāmeva samārādhya vidyāṃ bhuvanatāriṇīṃ |
tāmārādhyamahaṃ viṣṇurbhuvanaṃ pālayatyasau ||

saṃhārakāle ca haro rudra mūrtidharaṃ paraṃ |
tāmeva rudra saṃpūjya saṃharatyakhilaṃ jagat ||

ityuktā brahmaṇo yogī vasiṣṭhaḥ sādhakottamaḥ |
svaputre kathayāmāsa sarvamārādhanaṃ kramaṃ ||

vasiṣṭha uvāca ||

devatāmādi bhūtatvaṃ sarvavidyāmaya prabho |
kathaṃ dakṣadurārādhyāvidyā mahyamiyaṃ tvayā ||

sahasraṃ vatsarānpūrvamiyamārādhitā prabho |
nīlācale nivasatā haviṣyaṃ bhuṃjatā mayā ||

tathāpi tātatāriṇyāḥ karuṇāmayinā bhavat |
tato gaṃḍūṣa mātraṃ tu kāle kāle pivan jalaṃ ||

ārādhayāmitāṃ devīṃ vatsarāṇāṃ sahasrakaṃ |
tatopi yadi naivā bhūttāruṇyāḥ karuṇāmayi ||

tadāhameka pādena tiṣṭhannīlā calopari |
paraṃ samādhimāsthāya nirāhāro dṛḍhavrataḥ ||

tāmeva kevalaṃ dhyāyan japaṃstāmeva sarvadā |
ati vāhitavān varṣa sahasrāṣṭakaṃmuttamaṃ ||

evaṃ daśasahasraṃ tu varṣāṇā mahamīśvarīṃ |
kāmākhyā yonimāśritya samārādhitavānprabho ||

athāpyanugrahastasyāstathāpi na hi dṛśyate |
atalpajāmiduḥsādhyāṃ vidyāmenāṃsu duḥkhitaḥ ||

iti tadvacanaṃ śrutvā brahmāloka pitāmahaḥ |
uvāca sāṃtvarya putra vasiṣṭhaṃ munināṃvaraṃ ||

brahmovāca ||

vasiṣṭhavatsa gacchatvaṃ punarnīlācalaṃ prati |
tatrāsthito mahādevīmārādhaya dṛḍhavrataḥ ||

kāmākhyā yonimāślitya japaṃstu parameśvarīṃ |

66a)

acirāddevate siddhirbhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ||

etasyāḥ sadṛśī kācidvidyā na hi jagat traye |
imāṃ tyaktvā punarvidyāmanyāṃ kāṃtvaṃ grahīṣyasi ||

iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā praṇamya pitaraṃ muniḥ |
punarjagāma kāmākhyā yonimaṃḍalasannidhiṃ ||

tatra gatvā munivaraḥ pūjā saṃbhāva tatparaḥ |
ārādhayan mahāvidyāṃ vasiṣṭhoti jitendriyaḥ ||

athārādhayatastasya sahasraṃ parivatsarāḥ |
jagmustārāṃ mahādevīṃ pādaika jānuvartinaḥ ||

tathāpitaṃ pratiprītā yadyannābhūnmaheśvarī |
tadā doṣeṇa mahatā prajajvālamunīśvaraḥ ||

tato jalaṃ samādāya tāṃ saptamupacakrame |
etasminneva kāle tu ruṣṭamālokyataṃ muniṃ ||

ca cāla vasudhā sarvā sa śailavana kānanāḥ |
hāhākāro mahānāsīddevī deveṣu sarvataḥ ||

tatovabhūva puratastārā saṃsāratāriṇī |
vasiṣṭhastāṃ samālokya śaśāpātīva dāruṇaḥ ||

tato devī vasiṣṭhena śaptā na phaladā kvacit |
cīnācāraṃ vinā naiva prasīdati kadācana ||

uvāca sādhaka śreṣṭhamananīyatu dhāriṇī |
roṣeṇa dāruṇamanākathaṃ māmaśayedbhavān ||

madīyārādhanācāraṃ vuddharūpī janārdanaḥ |
eka eva vijānāti nānyakaścana tatvataḥ ||

bṛthaivāyāsa bahulaḥ kāloyaṃ gamitastvayā |
viruddhācāra śīlena mama tatvamajānatā ||

tadvuddharūpiṇo viṣṇoḥ sannidhiṃ yā hi saṃprati |
teno yadiṣṭācāreṇa māmārādhaya suvrata ||

tadaivāsu prasannasyāṃ tvayi vatsa na saṃśayaḥ |

ityācārasāratantre prathamaḥ paṭalaḥ ||

śiva uvāca || 

tataḥ praṇamyatāṃ devīṃ vasiṣṭhosau mahāmuniḥ |
jagāmācāra vijñāna vāṃchayā vuddharūpiṇaṃ ||

tato gatvā mahācīne deśe sa muni puṃgavaḥ |
dadarśa himavat pārśve sādhakeśvara sevitaṃ ||

66b)

nirlajjaghanabhāvena rūpayauvanaśālinā |
madirāmatta cittena vilāsollāśatena ca ||

śṛṃgārarasaveśena jaganmohanakāriṇā |
bhayalajjā vihīnena devī dhyāna pareṇa ca ||

kāminīnāṃ sahasreṇa pariṇāritamīśvaraṃ |
madirāpāna saṃjāta raktamanthara locanaṃ ||

dūrādeva vilokyainaṃ vasiṣṭho vuddharūpiṇaṃ |
vismayena samāviṣṭaḥ smaran saṃsāratāriṇīṃ ||

kimidaṃ kriyate karma viṣṇunā vuddharūpiṇā |
vedavādaviruddho yamācāraḥ sammato mama ||

iti ciṃtayatastasya vasiṣṭhasya mahātmanaḥ |
ākāśavāṇī prahāśumaiva ciṃtaya suvrata ||

ācāraḥ paramo yo yatāriṇī sādhake mune |
etadviruddhācārasya mate nāsau prasīdati ||

yadi tasyāḥ prasādatvamacireṇābhivāṃchasi |
etena cīnācāreṇa tadā tāṃ bhaja suvrata ||

ākāśavāṇīmākarṇya romāṃcita kalevaraḥ |
vasiṣṭho daṃḍavad bhūmau papātātīva harṣitaḥ ||

athotthāyācireṇāsau kṛtāṃjalipuṭo muniḥ |
jagāma viṣṇoḥ sa vidhaṃ buddharūpasya pārvati ||

athāsau na samālokya madirāmadavihvalaḥ |
prāha vuddhaḥ prasannātmā kimarthaṃ tvamihāgataḥ ||

atha vuddhaṃ praṇamyāha bhakti naśro mahāmuniḥ |
yadukta tāriṇī devyā nijārādhana hetave ||

śrutvā tu bhagavān vuddhastatvajñānamayo hariḥ |
vasiṣṭhaṃ prāhatajñānaṃ cinācāre'dhikāravān ||

aprakāśyastu tāriṇyā ācāraḥ sarvadā mune |
tava bhaktivasādasmin na prakāśyaṃ kadācana ||

buddha uvāca ||

athācāravidhiṃ vakṣye devyāḥ sarvasamṛddhidā |
yasyānuṣṭhānamātreṇa bhavāddhaunanimajjati ||

samastaśokaśamanamānaṃdāddhi vivardhanaṃ |
tatvajñānamayaṃ sākṣādvimukti phaladāyakaṃ ||

67a)

snānādirmānasaḥ sauco mānasaḥ pravaro japaḥ |
pūjanaṃ mānasaṃ divyaṃ mānasaṃ tarpaṇādikaṃ ||

sarva eva śubhaḥ kālonāśubho vidyate kvacit |
no viśeṣo divārātrau na saṃdhyāyāṃ divāniśi ||

vastrāsanastāna geha haṭṭe sparśādi vāriṇaḥ |
śuddhinaṃ cācaredatra nirvikalpaṃ manaścaret ||

nātraśuddhyādyapekṣāsti na cāmedhyādi dūṣaṇaḥ |
sarvathā pūjayed devī yamasnātaḥ kṛtabhojanaḥ ||

mahāniśā śucaudeśe valimaṃtreṇa dāpayet |
strī dveṣo naiva kartavyo viśeṣāt pūjanaṃ mahaṃ ||

tāsāṃ niṃdāṃ prahāraṃ ca kauṭilyama priyaṃ tathā |
sarvathā naiva kartavyamanyathā siddhirodhakṛt ||

striyo devāḥ striyaḥ prāṇā striya eva vibhūṣaṇaṃ |
strīkuleṣu sadā bhāvyamanyathā svastriyāmapi ||

taddhastaracitaṃ dravyaṃ mahādevyai nivedayet |
mahācīna kramajatā veṣṭhitaḥ sādhakottamaḥ ||

rātrau yadi japenmaṃtraṃ durlabhaṃ tasya kiṃ bhavet |
mahācīna kramalatā veṣṭite na ca yatphalaṃ ||

tasyāpi ṣoḍaśāṃśena kalā nārhaṃti keśavaḥ |
śavāsanādhikaphalaṃ latāgehe praveśanaṃ ||

śāśānālayamāgatya muktakeśo digamvaraḥ |
mahācīnakramalatāveṣṭito muktimāpnuyāt ||

japasthāne mahāśaṃkhaṃ niveśyordhaṃ japaṃ caret |
diklāniyamo nātra sthityādi niyamo na ca ||

na japet kālaniyamo nārcādiṣu valiṣvapi |
svecchācāropi gaditaḥ pracared dṛṣṭamānasaḥ ||

kṛtārthaṃ manyamānastu saṃtuṣṭo nijamānase |
sugaṃdhi śveta lauhitya kusumairarcayet kulaiḥ ||

vilvaiḥ kuru vakāraiśca tulasī varjitaḥ śubhaiḥ |
ekaliṃga śmaśāne vā śūnyāgāre catuḥpathe ||

67b)

tatrasthā sādhayedyogī tārāṃ bhuvanatāriṇīṃ |
tāriṇī dakṣiṇā kālī suṃdarī bhairavī tathā ||

mahācīnakrameṇetāḥ siddhyā eva na saṃśayaḥ |
suṃdarī bhairavī devyāḥ prakāropīha vidyate ||

tāriṇī dakṣiṇā siddhernnaiva cīnakramaṃ vinā |
mahācīna kramācāraḥ paraḥ sādhakasattamaḥ ||

tāriṇīṃ prajapan vidyāṃ kulakoṭīḥ samuddharet |
nadaṃti pitarastasya gāthāgāyaṃti te mudā ||

apinaḥ sa kule jātaḥ kulajñānī bhaviṣyati |
sa dhanyaḥ kulavijñānī sa kaviḥ sa ca paṃḍitaḥ ||

sa kulīnaḥ sa sukṛtī sadṛśī sa ca sādhakaḥ |
sa brāhmaṇaḥ sa vedajñaḥ sognihotrī sa dīkṣitaḥ ||

sa tīrthapīṭhe sanyāsī sanirāśī sa sarvagaḥ |
vrati sa somapāyī sa sa yaśasvī sa vai manuḥ ||

sa vaiṣṇavaḥ savai śaivaḥ sa ca gāṇapataḥ smṛtaḥ |
mahācīnakramācāraistāriṇīṃ yaḥ sadā bhajet ||

ityācāratamtre dvitīyaḥ paṭala ||  

śrīśiva uvāca || 

iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā harervuddhaśarīriṇaḥ |
vasiṣṭhastaṃ punaḥ prāha kṛtāṃjalipuṭo muniḥ ||

vasiṣṭha uvāca || 

bhagavan devadeveśa tatvajñānamayaḥ prabho |
mahācīna kramācāraḥ kathito bhavatā mama ||

pradhānastvayamevāsti madirāyoṣideva ca |
etayoḥ kiṃ pradhānaṃ tadvrūhi me parameśvara ||

śrībhagavānuvāca ||

etasmin paramācāra tulyameva dvayaṃ mune |
prādhānyaṃ yoṣitāṃ kiṃtu devānāṃ ca na saṃśayaḥ ||

yato hi yoṣitāṃ dehe sa devādhiṣṭhitā śivā |
ataḥ pūjāsu sarvāsu tāsāṃ prādhānya mucyate ||

vasiṣṭha uvāca ||

vrūhi devavidhānajña sarvajñānamaya prabho |

68a)

yathā yoṣitsu saṃpūjyā kṛtā sādhakasattamaiḥ ||

śrībhagavānuvāca || 

yonipīṭhe maṃtrapīṭhe yaṃtrapīṭhe ca pārvatī |
tridhā bhinnā mahāmāyā pūjyate sādhakottamaiḥ ||

sarveṣāmeva pīṭhānāṃ pradhānaṃ yoni pīṭhakaṃ |
tatra saṃpūjitā devī jhaṭityeva prasīdati ||

aṇimādyaṣṭa siddhīnāṃ kāraṇaṃ paramaṃ mune |
yonipūjā vidhisamyag mama sarvārthasādhanaṃ ||

nadī kāpālinī veśyā rajakī nāpitāṃgaṇā |
brāhmaṇī śūdrakanyā ca tathā gopālakanyakā ||

mālākārakī veśyā nava kanyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |
athavā sarvajaṃtūnāṃ vidagdhā lakṣaṇānvitāḥ ||

ānīyānuttamā bhadrāmeteṣāmeva nāyikāṃ |
suṃdarī yauvanonmattāṃ nirlajjāṃ cāruhāsinīṃ ||

kṛtvā digamvarī tāṃ ca gaṃdhakuṃkumacandanaiḥ |
anuliptāṃ muktakeśīṃ tatastadyonimaṃḍale ||

gurupaṃkti samārādhya pūjayitvā ṣaḍaṃgakaṃ |
pīṭhe pūjāṃ vidhāyātha tanmadhye pūjayecchivāṃ ||

tatra cāvāhanaṃ nāstijavinyāso na vā mune |
upacāraiḥ pūjayitvā arghyaṃ datvā tataḥ punaḥ ||

japtvā liṃge bhairavaṃ ca pūjayitvā maheśvaraṃ |
gaṃdhaiśca sākṣataiḥ puṣpairhomaṃ kuryādataḥ paraṃ ||

dharmādharmairhavirdīpte ātmāgnau manasāsrucā |
suṣumṇā vartmanā nityamakṣavartīrjuhomyahaṃ ||

svāhāṃto homa maṃtroyaṃ pratipratya hutirmune |
pūrṇāhutiṃ japāṃte ca juhuyāda munāmune ||

prakāśāpsarahastābhyāmavalaṃvyonmanī srucā |
dharmādharma phalāsneha pūrṇe vahnau juhomyahaṃ ||

svāhāṃtoyaṃ bhavenmaṃtro ghorapātaka muktidaḥ |

68b)

pūjākālaṃ vinānaiva paśyecchakti digaṃvarīṃ ||

pūjākālaṃ vinānaiva sudhāpeyā ca sādhakaiḥ |
āyudhā hīyate dṛṣṭvā pītvā ca paśutāṃ vrajet ||

sauśamanyāṃ kulācāre brāhmaṇaḥ prapivetsurāṃ |
anyatra kāmataḥ pītvā prāyaścittī bhavennaraḥ ||

bhārgaveṇa purā satyāṃ śrutvā devīstu vāruṇīṃ |
brahmāloka guruḥ sākṣāt prayayau bhārgavāṃtikaṃ ||

prasamnādhāvaracitāṃ brahmācārāmṛta samānayo |
devānāmamṛtaṃ brahmastadidaṃ laukikī surā ||

brahmajñānamayo devī kulācāreṇa jāyate |
sautrāmanyāṃ ca devendrastṛpyate surayaiva hi ||

seyaṃ surātvayā brahmantasyāḥ śāyuṃ pramucyatāṃ |
brahmāṇaṃ praṇipatyāha tato sau bhṛgunaṃdanaḥ ||

madvākyaṃ viphalaṃ nasyāttvadvākyaṃ ca pitāmaha |
amoghaṃ ca kariṣyāmi tadarthaṃ niyamaṃ kṛtaḥ ||

sautrāmastyāṃ kulācāre surāśāpa vimuktaye |
maṃtratrayaṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣvaika manāprabho ||

ekameva paraṃbrahma sthūlasūkṣmamayaṃ dhruvaṃ |
kacodbhavāṃ brahmahatyāṃ tetate nāśayāmyahaṃ ||

sūryamaṇḍalasaṃbhūte varuṇālaya saṃbhave |
amāvījamaye devī śukraśāpādvimucyatāṃ ||

devānāṃ praṇavo vījaṃ brahmān yajñamayaṃ yadi |
tena saṃpadyate devi brahmahatyāṃ vyapohatu ||

ityuktvā brahmaṇo trīṇi bhārgavaḥ praṇipatyataṃ |
jagāmabhavanaṃ devi brahmā svabhavanaṃ yayau ||

brahmajñānī kulācāre surāpītvā skhalanmuhuḥ |
patitasya tu tasyāṃge lagaṃti yadire navaḥ ||

tāvat kālaṃ ranusaṃkhyaṃ devī loke mahīyate |
pītvā pītvā punaḥ pītvā patitvā ca mahītale ||

69a)

utthāya ca punaḥ pītvā punarjanma na vidyate |
pītvāliga kulācāre pramadāṃ yauvanonvitāṃ ||

koṭi janmārjitaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇādeva nāśayet |
pītvā pītvā japitvā ca muktaṃ koṭi kulaiḥ saha ||

brahmaloke vaseddevīṃ satyaṃ satyaṃ na saṃśayaḥ |
tatraiva vāptimāpnoti na punarjāyate bhuvi ||

pītvā ca pūjayed devīmīśatvaṃ labhate dhruvaṃ |
tatraiva layamāpnoti punarnnaiva nivartate ||

pītvāgni hotre bhūtvā ca trailokyaiśvarya bhājanaṃ |
jāyate sādhakaḥ śreṣṭo mahābhogī mahāsukhī ||

pītvā yogī bhojayitvā sohaṃ haṃsastataḥ paraṃ |
svāheti jāyate vīro jīvanmuktojamatraye ||

cirajīvī jarāyukto vimuktaḥ sarvapātakaiḥ |
valāmiti valāṃcāpi siddhitva samavāpya ca ||

ityevaṃ kathitaṃ tulyaṃ yathā pūjyā digaṃvarī |
pūjayitvā sakṛddevīṃ mucyate sarvapātakaiḥ ||

evaṃ devīmarcayitvā kimasādhyaṃ jagattraye |
haro prakupite vāpi pūjayitvā digamvarīṃ ||

sṛṣṭisthitilayādīnāṃ kartāro jagadīśvarāḥ |
yogebhyo ghorarūpeṣu pūjayitvā vimucyate ||

aputro labhate putraṃ daridro dhanavān bhavet |
ārabhya śuklapratipadyāvat paṃcadaśī bhavet ||

pratyahaṃ pūjayed yastu tithi saṃkhyā digaṃvarī |
maṃtrasiddhirbhavet tasya satyaṃ satyaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ||

vīrasādhana karmāṇi duḥkhasādhyāni kevalaṃ |
susamaṃsādhanaṃ hyetat tava snehāt prakāśitaṃ ||

gopanīyaṃ prayatnena putrebhyopi na darśayet |
ityeṣa kathitastubhyaṃ pūjāvidhiranuttamaḥ ||

69b)

sādhanaṃ sarvathā caivaṃ gopayenmātṛjāravat |


ityācārasāratamtre tṛtīyaḥ paṭalaḥ || 


vasiṣṭha uvāca || 

kuleśayāni pātrāṇi piśitānāṃ ca lakṣaṇaṃ |
kuladravyasya nirmāṇaṃ vada māhātmyameva ca ||

avidhānena yatpāpaṃ sa vidhānena yatphalaṃ |
tatsarvaṃ śrotumicchāmi vadame karuṇā nidhe ||

śrībhagavānuvāca ||

mune śṛṇu pravakṣyāmi yanmāṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi |
tasya smaraṇamātreṇa tridaśaiḥ samatāṃ vrajet ||

ādhāreṇa vinābhraṃśo na ca tṛpyaṃti mātaraḥ |
tasmādvidhivadādhāraṃ kalpayet kulanāyakaḥ ||

athavā vartulākāraṃ kuryādvṛti manoharaṃ |
svarṇarūpyaśilākūrma kapālānālāṃvu ca mṛnmayaṃ ||

kuladravyaṃ pravakṣyāmi mune śṛṇu samāhitaḥ |
aṃbhasāṃ dvādaśaprasthaṃ prasthārdha taktameva ca ||

taṃḍulānāṃ catuḥprasthaṃ dviprasthaṃ payasastathā |
muṣṭimātrāṃkuraṃ deyamekasmin yojayedghaṭe ||

śītādevahita sthāne sthāpayeddivasa dvayaṃ |
tato vahnau samāropya yanmāna sadṛśaṃ pacet ||

avaropya parāśītāmavasthā tāṃ nayedbudhaḥ |
payaprasthena piṣṭvā tu hastābhyāṃ melayet tataḥ ||

samyak sarmavyatakreṇa payasāloḍyamelayat |
eṣā paiṣṭhīti vikhyātā pūjitā devadānavaiḥ ||

kulapūjāvināsvārthaṃ yaḥ karotīha durmatiḥ |
prayāti narakaṃ ghoramekaviṃśatibhiḥ kulaiḥ ||

devānpitṝnsamabhyarcya mune śāstrokta vartmanā |
guruṃ smaranpivanmadyaṃ khādanmāṃsaṃ na doṣabhāk ||

sevato vratasukhārthāya madyādīn sa ca pātakī |
prāśayed devatā prītyai svābhilāṣa vivarjitaḥ ||

70a)

śvapacopi kulajñānī brahmaṇādati ricyate |
yaḥ kaulikaḥ kulajñānaṃ na paśyati na vaṃdyati ||

dhik tasya jīvanaṃ loke dhik dhik tasya ca pauruṣaṃ |
te vaṃdyāḥ puṇyakarmīṇasteṣāṃ tāste ca yoginaḥ ||

yeṣāṃ citte bhāgyavaśāt kulajñānaṃ prakāśate |
te vaṃdyāste mahātmānaste kṛtārthā narottamāḥ ||

yeṣāmutpādyate citte kulajñānamayoditaṃ |
trāsitāhi mayā pūrvaṃ paśavaḥ śāstrakoṭibhiḥ ||

kuladharmaṃ na jānaṃti tatvajñānābhimāninaḥ |
paśuśāstrāṇi sarvāṇi mayaiva kathitāni vai ||

smṛtyuktareṇa valamaṃtre ca mohanāya durātmanā |
mahāpaśa prayuktānāṃ te svavāṃchābhi jāyate ||

teṣāṃ tu sadgatirnnāsti kalpakoṭi śatairapi |
vahavaḥ kaulikaṃ dharmaṃ śrutvā jñānavit svakāḥ ||

niṃdatīhasuvuddhaiva pārasparya vimohitaḥ ||

vasiṣṭha uvāca || 

madyapānena manujā yadi sidhyaṃti kevalaṃ |
madyapānaratāḥ sarve siddhiryatne ca pāravāḥ ||

strīsaṃbhogena lokānāṃ yadi mokṣo bhavediha |
sarvepi jaṃtavo loke muktāsyuḥ strīniṣevaṇāt ||

vuddha uvāca ||

atra śṛṇūttaraṃ putrakuladharmā mahālayaṃ |
mokṣaṃ dadāti bhūtānāmetaddharma pravartināṃ ||

vṛthāpānaṃ yat kriyate surāpānaṃ taducyate |
tanmahāpātakāyaiva vedādiṣu nirūpitaṃ ||

vasiṣṭa uvāca ||

tanmukhācchrotu micchāmi kuladharmaṃ viśeṣataḥ |
etasya hi viśeṣajñastvat samonāstikaścana ||

tasya dharmasya māhātmyaṃ sarvadharmottamasya ca |
vadame parameśāna yadi testi kṛpāmayi ||

śrībhagavānuvāca ||

70b)

mune śṛṇu pravakṣyāmi yanmāṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi |
tasya śravaṇamātreṇa yoginīnāṃ priyo bhavet ||

śivabrahma guhādīnāṃ yanmayā kathitaṃ purā |
kathayāmi tavasnehācchṛṇuṣvekāgramānasaḥ ||

pāraṃparya kramāyeta matigopyaṃ mahadbhutaṃ |
akathyaṃ paramārthena tathāpi kathayāmite ||

sarvebhyaścottamā vedāḥ vedebhyo vaiṣṇavaṃ paraṃ |
vaiṣṇavāt paramaṃ śaivaṃ śaivāddakṣiṇamuttamaṃ ||

dakṣiṇāduttamaṃ vāmaṃ vāmāt siddhāṃtamuttamaṃ |
siddhāṃtāduttamaṃ kaulaṃ kaulātparataraṃ na hi ||

guhyādguhyatamaṃ devi sārātsāraṃ paraṃtaraṃ |
mathitvā jñānamaṃthena vedāgama mahārṇavaṃ ||

sarvadharma tavajñānaṃ sarvadharma samuddhṛtaḥ |
ekataḥ sakalā dharmāḥ yajñāstīrtha vratādayaḥ ||

ekataḥ kuladharmoyaṃ sarvayajñādhika priye |
praviśaṃti yathā nadyaḥ siṃdhau navaśatomitaḥ ||

tathaiva samayā sarve pratiṣṭhāḥ kulameva hi |
yathā hasti pade līnaṃ sarvaprāṇi padaṃ bhavet ||

darśanāni ca sarvāṇi kula eva tathā mune |
yathā marataraṃgiṇyā na samāḥ sakalāpagāḥ ||

tathaiva samayāḥ sarve kuladharmeṇano samāḥ |
meru sarṣapayoryadvat sūrya khadyotayoryathā ||

tathāsya samayasyāsya kulasya mahadaṃtaraṃ |
asti cet jñānavān kaścin matsamo bhuvimānavaḥ ||

tathaiva kuladharmeṇa samosti bhuvana traye |
janmabhirvahubhirdhyānāt tapobhirmunisattama ||

mokṣaṃ labhaṃte tu vudhā jīvanmuktāstu kaulikāḥ |
satyaṃ satyaṃ punaḥ satyaṃ satyameva na saṃśayaḥ ||

vahunā kimihoktena śṛṇutvamavadhānataḥ |
na kaulena samo dharmaḥ satyametadvadāmite ||

71a)

yogīcennaiva bhogī syād bhogī cennaiva yogavān |
yogabhogātmakaṃ kaulaṃ tasmāt sarvādhikaṃ tvidaṃ ||

ityācārasāratantre caturthaḥ paṭalaḥ ||

śrībhagavānuvāca ||

samayāṣṭakaṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇuṣvaika mahāmune |
yena vijñānamātreṇa siddhirbhavati sādhakaḥ ||

ghātayed gopayed vāpī niṃdayen na vilokayet |
pūjayed bhāvayeccaiva varjayen na jugupsayet ||

kāmaṃ krodhaḥ samātsaryaṃ vikāraṃ cendriyod bhavaṃ |
nidrāṃ lajjāṃ daurmanasyaṃ ghātayedaṣṭaka priye ||

maṃtramudrākṣa sūtrastu yoginī vīrasaṃbhavaṃ |
bhairavāgamamācārametat sarvaṃ tu gopayet ||

devaṃ guruṃ surāṃ vidyāṃ sādhakaṃ yoṣitāṃ tathā |
śubhāśubhaṃ karmaciraṃ niṃdayen naiva kadācana ||

kanyāśakti paśukrīḍāṃ nagnastrīṃ prakaṭastanīṃ |
dyūtavigraha pāpārthī kulīnaṃ na vilokayet ||

guruṃ devī tathā sādhu na śakti cātmamavyayaṃ |
śakti tatsādhikān sarvān pūjayecca prayatnataḥ ||

gurorvākyopadeśaṃ ca saddattatīrtha devatāḥ |
svadharmaṃ ca kulācāraṃ sadā tatvena bhāvayet ||

agamyāgamanaṃ caiva dhūrtagoṣṭhīṃ ca caṃcalaṃ |
anṛtaṃ pāpagoṣṭī ca varjayet siddhasādhakaḥ ||

viṇmūtraṃ śoṇitaṃ kledaṃ hīināṃgo piśitaṃ surāṃ |
kapālaharaṇaṃ caiva aṣṭau naiva jugupsayet ||

ityevaṃ samayācāraṃ yaḥ karotīha sādhakaḥ |
yadvā na labhate vastu tatrāsti bhuvanatraye ||

śrīdevyuvāca ||

deva deva mahādeva jagatpralayakāraka |
kulācāreṇa maṃvāmvai kathaṃ siddhirbhavet prabho ||

yadi tanmadirāpānaṃ yat parastrī niṣevanaṃ |
adharmakaraṇācchiddhi sarvaṃ me saṃśayaṃ prabho ||

71b)

śiva uvāca ||

sādhu pṛṣṭo'smi deveśi kathayāmi śṛṇuṣva me |
purā dāruvane ramye munayaḥ sādhakāḥ parāḥ ||

parastriyaṃ dharṣayaṃti madyaṃ khādaṃti nityaśaḥ |
taṃ dṛṣṭvānucitaṃ karma brahmāmāṃsamupasthitaḥ ||

devadeva mahādeva sṛṣṭisthitilayātmaka |
etadāruvane pāyānmadyapānaratāstathā ||

parastrīyaṃ dharṣayaṃti madyaṃ khādati mohitāḥ |
digaṃvarāśca muṃḍāśca gatireṣā kathaṃ bhavet ||

iti brahmavacaḥ śrutvā tamuvāca ahaṃ priye |
pitāmaha na jānāsi cīnācārakramaṃ bhavān ||

ugratārāṃ mahāvidyāmete nityaṃ jayaṃti hi |
pūjayaṃti ca tāmeva cīnācāraparāyaṇāḥ ||

sādhakāḥ sarva evete mahākaulā mahāśayāḥ |
jīvanmuktiṃ gatāḥ sarve devī bhaktiparāyaṇāḥ ||

parastrīdharṣaṇāccaiva madyapānācca nityaśaḥ |
aśvamedhādapyadhika labhaṃte phalamuttamaṃ ||

etāstu niṃdanmohācca mahāpātaka vātmavān |
ito dūraṃ prayāhitvaṃ na māṃ spṛśa pitāmaha ||

ityaiva muktasamayā brahmāloka pitāmahaḥ |
paraṃ vismayamāpannaḥ saṃśayā viṣṭamānasaḥ ||

kimidaṃ śaṃbhunā proktaṃ vedācāravahiṣkṛtaṃ |
iti saṃciṃtayan maunaṃ prāyapaṃkajasaṃbhavaḥ ||

tato vaikuṇṭhamāsādya śrīviṣṇuṃ parameśvaraṃ |
kṛtāṃjali puṭo bhūtvā sarvamevamuvācasaḥ ||

devadeva mahāviṣṇo saṃsārasthiti kāraka |
chiṃdhi me saṃśayaṃ deva mahāṃtaṃ manasi sthitaṃ ||

tvadanyaḥ saṃśayasyāsyacchettā kaścinna vidyate |
tīrthaparyaṭanāyadyadgataṃ dāruvanaṃ mayā ||

72a)

tatra sarve munigaṇāḥ parastrīdharṣaṇe ratāḥ |
madirāpānasaṃjāta sadā ghūrṇitalocanāḥ ||

ramamānī parastrībhirnirlajjā sarva eva hi |
evaṃ tān sudurācārān dṛṣṭvā kailāsavāsinaṃ ||

mahādevamavocaṃ tat sarvameva dayānidhe |
pāpācārānapi munīn prasaṃśaṃ sa maheśvaraḥ ||

śraddhayā parayāviṣṭastānuddiśya punaḥ punaḥ |
uvāca sādhavaste vai jīvanmukto mahāśayāḥ ||

tānniṃditvā mahāpāpa jajuḥ dūramito yataḥ |
tato haṃ vismayāviṣṭaḥ prāptastvāṃ jagadīśvara ||

etanme saṃśayaṃ chiṃdhi cet kṛpāmapi vartate |
evaṃ sa brahmaṇā proktā viṣṇuḥ sarveśvaraḥ prabhuḥ ||

bhaktyā paramayāyuktastān munīnpraṇatāmyahaṃ |
uvāca ca vidhātāraṃ tatvajñānamayaṃ vacaḥ ||

tvayā dāruvane dṛṣṭvā munayo ye pitāmahaḥ |
tārāmārādhayaṃte tu sarve sādhakasattamāḥ ||

parastriyaṃ dharṣayaṃti madyaṃ khādaṃti nityaśaḥ |
nirvāṇaṃte tu yāsyaṃti bhagavatyāḥ prasādadaḥ ||

cīnācāraṃ samāśritya munayaste mahāśayāḥ |
tatvajñānamayā sarve viharaṃti mahītale ||

tvamāśugaccha tatraiva tān prasādaya padmaja |
teṣu vyaṣṭiṣu bhavato brahmatvamapi yāsyasi ||

mahādevena yat proktaṃ tasya me tanna saṃśayaḥ |
āvayosana saṃspṛśya sādhakānyo vinindati ||

śrīśiva uvāca ||

tato viṣṇuṃ praṇamyāsau parameṣṭhī tvarānvitaḥ |
gatvā dāruvanaṃ sarvān praṇanāma munīśvarān ||

tuṣṭāva parayā bhaktyāstatrairvahu vidhairapi |
teṣāṃ prasādaya māsādya kṛtakṛtyo bhavadvidhiḥ ||

72b)

śrīdevyuvāca ||

mahācīna kramācāraṃ tato vuddhādi vāśu ca |
vasiṣṭhaḥ sa kimakarottanme vrūhi maheśvara ||

śrīśiva uvāca ||

mahācīna kramācāra tato vuddhyādi vāpyasaḥ |
nīlācalaṃ samāsādya kulācāra parāyaṇaḥ ||

tatokṣamālāṃ yuvatīṃ cāṃḍālīnu mayenmuniḥ |
japan saṃsādhayāmāṃsatārāṃ mukti pradāmimāṃ ||

madirābhipānamattābhirmadirā madaghūrṇitaḥ |
tārāmārādhayāmāsa kṛta kṛtyo bhavat tadā ||

sākṣādbhūtā mahādevī tārā saṃsāratāriṇī |
tamuvāca vasiṣṭhatvaṃ varānvṛṇu yathepsitān ||

vasiṣṭha uvāca ||

tāre devi jaganmātaḥ jñānavijñānadāyini |
varameva vṛṇetvannaḥ prasannā dehi hime śive ||

mahācīna kramācārairyastvāṃ saṃpūjayiṣyati |
sarvadā tasyārcakasya sākṣātvaṃ hi bhaviṣyasi ||

śrīdevyuvāca ||

cīnācāreṇa yaḥ kaścit tārāṃ māṃ pūjayiṣyati |
sa me putra tayāgatya satyaṃ satyaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ||

iha bhogān varān bhuktvā bṛhaspatirivāparaḥ |
aṃte yāsyati matpārśvaṃ yatra me gaṇanāyakaḥ ||

rūpayauvanasaṃpanno rudrakanyāgaṇaiḥ saha |
vihariṣyaṃtyasau vīro yāvaccaṃdrārkatārakaṃ ||

tavāpi bhavitā vatsa yoga siddhiranuttamā |
aṇimāḥ siddhayastvaṃ me bhaviṣyaṃti niraṃtaraṃ ||

iti labdhavarastasyā vasiṣṭhosau mahāmuniḥ |
nakṣatralokamāsādya adyāpi dyotate divi ||

eṣate kathito devi cīnācāraḥ sudurlabhaḥ |
samācaran sādhakendro bhuktimuktiṃ ca viṃdati ||

etat sarvaṃ prayatnena gopitavyaṃ tvayā priye |

73a)

yathā hyanyo na labhate tathārpaṃ ca maheśvari ||

svayoniriva deveśi goptavya paśusannidhau |
yo bhaktaḥ sādhako jñānī tasmai vaktavyameva hi ||

ityācārasāratantre paṃcamaḥ paṭalaḥ ||

śrīśiva uvāca ||

athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi rahasyaṃ śṛṇu pārvati |
yonimaṇḍalamāsādya mūlamaṃtra japet tu yaḥ ||

ṣaṇmāse siddhimāpnoti vināhomārcanādibhiḥ |
yonimudrāṃ vijānāti mūlavidyāṃ śṛṇoti yaḥ ||

tasyā cirādaṣṭa siddhistannāti yanna sādhayet |
yadi bhāgyavasādeva yonimudrāṃ vilokayet ||

praṇamya daṇḍavadbhūmau manasā japamācaret |
bhagarūpā mahādevī yoginī yonirūpiṇī ||

tasmādyatnena maṃtrajño mahāmudrā samarpayet |
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ maṃgale śanivāsare ||

yoginī kuru vaṃdaiśca saṃsthitā yonimaṃḍale |
yonimaṃḍala tatvajñaḥ kuladravyaparāyaṇaḥ ||

sa rudra iti vijñeyaḥ sarvaśāstreṣu niścitaṃ |
yonau pūjāṃ nācaraṃśca māṃsaṃ madhye tathā madhu ||

kuladravyāṇi caitāni bhakṣayet kulakaulikaḥ |
madirānaṃda sānaṃdo māṃsamudrāśanonavā ||

paṃcatatvaṃ na seveta sa kathaṃ kulakaulikaḥ |
madyaṃ māṃsaṃ tathā matsyaṃ mudrāṃ maithuna karma ca ||

na sevate yadā devī sa kathaṃ kulakaulikaḥ |
paṃcatatvaṃ vinānāsti śaktīnāṃ bhukti muktiṣu ||

tasmāt sarvaprayatnena paṃcatatvaṃ nivedayet |
devīṃ saṃpūjayitvā tu tasyāṃ saṃbhakṣayen naraḥ ||

niṣevya paṃcatatvāni sarvadānaṃdamānasaḥ |
kulajñānāṃ melanena viharet kulabhairavaḥ ||

73b)

saṃsthāpyamāme kulajāṃ kulapūjārato bhavet |
deyaṃ tasmai madyamāṃsaṃ khādyaṃ tanmukhataḥ priye ||

praviśya yonimudrāṃ ca japen maṃtramananyadhīḥ |
ātmānaṃ bhairavaṃ matvā yoniṃ bhagavatīṃ tathā ||

bhairavācara saṃpannaḥ praviśedyoni maṃḍale |
āliṃgya yuvatīṃ gāḍhaṃ saṃcuṃvyādharameva ca ||

daṃtakṣataṃ nakhāghātaṃ tatra tatra vinirdiśet |
kulodbhavena dravyeṇa pūjayet tarpayeccayaḥ ||

sa eva sādhakajñānī kulajñānī na saṃśayaḥ |
yadi gacched bhagavati kapaṭaṃ caiva kārayet ||

devī guṇavatī tasya sarvaṃ nāśayati dhruvaṃ |
yā śaktiḥ sā mahādevī kevalānaṃdarūpinī ||

tadyoge naiva mukta syāt sādhako vīrarūpadhṛk |
iti jñātvā japed vidyāṃ kevalaṃ bhāvatatparaḥ ||

jāti sa bandha vuddhiṃ ca na kadāpi ca sādhakaḥ |
ciṃtayet taṃ ca deveśi narakaṃ pratipadyate ||

ucchiṣṭaṃ bhakṣayet tāsāṃ dadyānnocchiṣṭameva hi |
śaktyucchiṣṭaṃ pived dravyaṃ vīrocchiṣṭaṃ tu carvaṇaṃ ||

śaktivīra prasādena kinna sidhyati bhūtale |
ānaṃdapūrṇa hṛdayo viharet kulabhairavaḥ ||

raktacaṃdanadigdhāṃgastāṃvūlapūritānanaḥ |
raktamālyāṃvaradharo rakta kopīṇa bhūṣaṇaḥ ||

śaktimākṛṣya yatnena kulācārarato bhavet |
tasmād yatnena maṃtrajño tāvacchakti parāyaṇaḥ ||

evaṃ taṃtraṃ ca maṃtraṃ ca gopayen mātṛjāravat |
mohāt prakāśādacirādadhoyāti na saṃśayaḥ ||

ityācārasāratantre rahasyakathane ṣaṣṭhaḥ paṭalaḥ ||

śrīdevyuvāca || 

devadeva mahādeva mahākāruṇika prabho |
yoginīnāṃ sadāsevyaṃ kaulānāṃ valapuṣṭidaṃ ||

74a)

manaścāṃcalya haraṇaṃ kiṃ samādhi phalapradaṃ |
vadasva tada śeṣeṇa yadyahaṃ tava vallabhā ||

śrīśiva uvāca ||

akathyate taccārvaṃgi devāsura nareṣvapi |
kathayāmi tava prītyā guhyādguhyataraṃ mahat ||

śrutvā tvayāpi goptavyaṃ yatnena paśusaṃkaṭe |
valo nāma mahānāsīdasurāvalavān purā ||

jitvā suragaṇān sarvānindrobhūt svayameva saḥ |
tataḥ palāyitāḥ sarve bhayodvignā divaukasaḥ ||

puraṃdaraḥ purodhānaṃ maṃtrayitvā suniścitaṃ |
nānyosti tasmādasmākaṃ trātā śrīmadhusūdanāt ||

iti saṃciṃtya sarve te prayayuḥ parameśvaraṃ |
saṃstūyamānamṛṣibhiḥ siddhakinnarasevitaṃ ||

tāṃ dṛṣṭvā puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ praṇamed daṇḍavadbhuvi |
ūcuḥ prāṃjala yaścaite devāḥ śakra purogamāḥ ||

namostu haraye tubhyaṃ sarvaduḥkhaṃ ca hāriṇe |
surāṇāmārtināśāya sarveśāya namo namaḥ ||

namastrimūrtaye tubhyaṃ sṛṣṭisthityaṃta kāriṇi |
guṇātītāya śuddhāya paratopi parāya ca ||

sarvātmane nanastestu sarvaśakti yutāyate |
sarvajñāya sarvalokasākṣiṇe iti stutvā ||

sakalaṃ tadvṛttāṃtaṃ nivedaya śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ | 
sarve trāhi nastaṃ nihatya ca durācāro valamukhā yathāyātya ciraṇate ||

rakṣā smākaṃ ca śakrasya tathā kartutva marhasi |
śrutvedaṃ vacanaṃ teṣāmidamāha puraṃdaraṃ ||

vṛttāṃtametajjānāmi valasyāsya durātmanaḥ |
brāhmaṇā samayā vāpi na sa vadhyaḥ śivena vā ||

tvayi vadhyaḥ sa bhavitā sa durātmāna saṃśayaḥ |
etat sarvaṃ maheśāya nivedaya puraṃdaraḥ ||

sa eva bhagavān sarvametajjānāti śaṃkaraḥ |
tāvat tilaṣite sarvaṃ sa vidhāsyāti gamyatāṃ ||

74b)

prasādyatāṃ ca yatnena tvayāsau bhaktavatsalaḥ |
atha praṇamya śaktastvaṃ sa māyāto mamāṃtikaṃ ||

āgatya śuddhabhāvosau praṇamya ca kṛtāṃjaliḥ | 

tuṣṭuve vividhaistotrairbhakti gadgadabhāṣitaṃ mādhyānoparatamīśvaraṃ ||

stotra pāthairvahuvidhai manudbhavanināditaiḥ |
mahadbhiḥ parito jñātaṃ sarvatadeva śeṣataḥ ||

asya vadhya savalodurātmāsau bhaviṣyati |
sa vidhya bhedvijñāya śakramāhūya sannidhiṃ ||

tasmai tatparamaṃ jñānaṃ datvāroc midaṃ vacaḥ |
trailokyavijayājñāṃ etat trailokya durlabhaṃ ||

aśeṣapāpaśamanaṃ parātmā svaprakāśakaṃ |
akhaṃḍānaṃdanilayamadvaitaparamāspadaṃ ||

manasthairyaḥ karaṃ roga śokasaṃtāpanāśanaṃ |
valapuṣṭikaraṃ samyak yogasiddhikaraṃ mahat ||

niṣevyatāmiyaṃ saṃvit sthīyatāṃ ca matāṃtike |
tato gatvā vatsarāṃte sa vale jeṣyate tvayā ||

ityemukta samayā prāṃjaliścedamavravīt ||

śakra uvāca ||

devadeva mahādeva sarvajña sarvatatvavit |
vidhinākena sevyoyaṃ ko vā maṃtraviśodhane ||

tarpaṇasvīkṛtau maṃtraḥ savide kṛpayā vibho |
sarvametadaśeṣeṇa sāṃgopāṃga vadasva me ||

śrīśiva uvāca ||

śṛṇu śakra mahābhāga sarvametad vadāmi te |
śrutvā gopaya yatnena tadevācara nityaśaḥ ||

trailokyavijayākṣyāpānāmāni prathama kramāt |
kathayāmi tava snehādati guptāni sarvataḥ ||

trailokyavijayā siddhimāsotha śuddhimūlikā |
jñānaṃ ca samvidā śyāmā bhaṃgā gaṃjāraśāyaṇā ||

yogadā yogasaṃsevyā yogamārgāpradarśinī |
brahmāṇī brahmasaṃbhūtā brahmānaṃdapradāyinī ||

vāgdevatā vaśaṃkarī vijayā vijayapradā |

75a)

samādhirivadājñāna nāśinītvekaviṃśatiḥ ||

śvetaraktapītakṛṣṇapuṣpabhedaiścaturvidhā |
śvetapuṣpa brāhmaṇī sā kṣatriyā raktapuṣpikā ||

pītapuṣpā tu vaiśyā sā śūdrā tu kṛṣṇapuṣpikā |
ākṛṣṇampatrāṇye teṣā sa vijānīyā prayatnataḥ ||

bharjitāni ghṛtenaiva cūrṇitāni śilātale |
trikaṭu triphalā śṛṃgī kuṣṭaṃ dhanyāka saiṃdhavaṃ ||

śaṭhī tālī sa patraṃ carūkkalaṃ nāgakesaraṃ |
yavānī dvayamethī ca jīrakatvayameva ca ||

etāni samabhāgāni raudraśuṣkāni cūrṇayet |
gṛhītvā cūrṇameteṣāṃ saṃviccūrṇaṃ tu tatsamaṃ ||

uye ca samaṃ datvā sitātanmiśrayed guḍaṃ |
miśrayitvā caturthāṃśa samaṃ madhu ghṛtaṃ tathā ||

punaḥ śilātale piṣṭvā triṣugaṃdho pravartayet |
svarṇādi pātre purataḥ sthāpayitvā tataḥ kramāt ||

caturbhirmanubhistāsāṃ śodhanaṃ ca samuccaret |
niveśya tatra pālyagnaṃ yathāvidhi viśodhayet ||

oṃ samvide brahmasaṃbhūte brahmaputri sadā naghe |
bhairavānāṃ ca tṛptyarthaṃ paritrā bhava sarvadā ||

oṃ brāhmaṇyai namaḥ svāhā || brāhmaṇī śodhanamanuḥ || 

oṃ siddhimūli kriye devi hīnavodha pravodhini | 
rājāprajāvaśakarī śatrūkaṃṭha triśūlinī || 

oṃ kṣatriyāyai namaḥ svāhā || śodhayeda parā tataḥ || 

ajñāne dhanadīptāgne jvālāgni brahmarūpiṇī |
ānaṃdasyāhuti prītiṃ samyak jñānaṃ prayacchame ||

oṃ hrīṃ vaiśyāyai namaḥ svāhā || śūdrāṃ śodhayet tataḥ || oṃ namasyāmi 
yogamārarjapradarśinī || 

trailokya vijaye mātaḥ samādhi phaladā bhava || 

klīṁ śūdrāyai namaḥ svāhā || oṃ amṛte amṛtodbhave amṛtavaṣiṇi ||

75b)

amṛtamākarṣayākarṣasiddhiṃ dehi amukaṃmeva vaśamānaya svāhā || 

iti paṭhitvā tatra ānaṃdabhairavānaṃdabhairavyormaṃtravayat || 

śivasomo mātṛkāṃtaṃ kālabhūvaruṇānanā |
vāmakarṇasamāyuktaṃ vāyumūrdhendu saṃyutaṃ ||

anaṃdabhairavāyeti śikhāmaṃtraṃ tato vadet |
ānaṃdabhairavāpyā tu mānaṃda bhairavīṃ śṛṇu ||

pūrvavadvījamālikhya caṃdraṃ hitvādimaṃlayet |
karṇe vāmākṣi saṃyojya sudhā devyai dṛśoḥ * * ||

mūlamaṃtraṃ saptavāraṃ tasyopari niyojayet |
āvāhanyādi mudrāṃ ca dhenu yonī tataḥ paraṃ ||

digvaṃdhanaṃ choṭikābhiḥ tālatrayapuraḥsaraṃ |
divyadṛṣṭyā tathā pārṣṇighātairvighnān vighātayet ||

sāyudhā tarpayed brahmaraṃdhre mūlaṃ japanmanuṃ |
guruṃ padmasahasrāre tathā saṃketamudrayā ||

tridhā vā tarpayed bhaktyā sakṛdvāpi nijecchayā |
paramākhyaṃ guruṃ tatra parāpara guruṃ tataḥ ||

taṃtreṇānaṃdabhairavyostarpayecca manuṃ smaran |
hṛdaye tarpayed devīṃ mūlena tatvamudrayā ||

samvidātri sakṛdvāpi tilamudgapramāṇayā |

aiṁ aiṁ vada 2 vāgvādini mama jihvāgre sthirī bhavaḥ sarvaṃ satvaravaśaṃkari 
svāhā || ityakau juhuyān mukhe | mukhāmṛteradicaine svīkuryāt tataḥ || 

dugdhāṃ tu ghṛtamādhvīkasai karairnavalena vā | 
sitayātha gudenāpi paṃkena kadalena vā ||

yadyadvā madhuraṃ dravyaṃ pakvāmraṃ panasādikaṃ |
tena sarveṇa vijayāṃ svīkuryāt sādhakottamaḥ ||

dugdha yogena vijayā kevalānaṃdadāyinī |
mahātejaskarī cakṣurdoṣādi vinivāriṇī ||

ghṛtena medhāmādhatte vāgdevī vaśakāriṇī |
pratibhā muttamādhattedhiṣaṇāṃ cāti nirmalaṃ ||

76a)

kaphadoṣānaśeṣāṃśca madhunā saha nāśayet |
saiṃdhavena mahāvahni pradāsyāllavaṇena ca ||

sitayātha guḍenāpi śūlāmla pittanāśinī |
atisāropaśamanī śvāsakāśa pramardinī ||

āmavāta samudbhūta grahaṇī vinivāriṇī |
sarvairvā madhurairyuktā sarvāmayavināśinī ||

valapuṣṭipradā caiva madhurasvaradāyinī |
jñānavijñānadā nityaṃ śīlamārgaprakāśinī ||

vahunātra kimuktena kevalācit prakāśinī | 

prakāśitā tava snehāt sarvamānaveṣu gopitā |
atha svīkṛtya saṃciṃtya sahasrāre guruṃ yajet || 

pādukāmaṃtramuccārya caturthyaṃtaṃ nivedayet |
paṃcabhūtottha vījaiśca gaṃdhādi paṃcakaṃ diśet ||

praṇame daṃḍavadbhūmau japtvā śrīgurupādukāṃ |
iṣṭadaivatvatanmaṃtraṃ prajapan viharet kṛtī ||

evamadyāt tataḥ śakra pratyahaṃ vatsaraṃ tataḥ |
tejasvī valavān vāgmī medhāvī priyadarśanaḥ ||

rūpayauvanasaṃpanno nānāguṇasamāśrayaḥ |
bhaviṣyati na saṃdeho dravyasyāsya niṣevaṇāt ||

saṃvidaḥ kevalāyā tu sevanāt kiṃ prasidhyati |
saṃvidāsārayormadhye samvidaikagarīyasi ||

saṃvit prayogate nehaṃ kartavyaḥ sādhakottamaḥ |
ekakālaṃ dvikālaṃ vā trikālaṃ paṃcakālakaṃ ||

tolakaṃ vā tadardhe vā tolaka dvayameva ca |
na ca nyūnādhikāmātrā yathā bhavaṃti nityasaḥ ||

nyūnādhikā yā mātrā yā phalaṃtakṣanna jāyate |
tasmāt pramāṇamātrā hi kartavyā siddhimicchatā ||

etat te kathitaṃ sarvaṃ vijayākalpamuttamaṃ |
prasādādacirādanyaṃ vāṃchitaṃ te bhaviṣyati ||

76b)

ityuktaḥ samayā śakto nirbhavānaṃdamārdavaiḥ |
bhaktyā paramayā yuktastatkartumupa cakrame ||

saṃvatsaraṃ pratidinaṃ prayatastrikālaṃ śakro niṣevya vijayāṃ vidhinā 
vasiṣṭha || jitvā valāsuramabhūtha devarāja prāpapya viśvaśamanasya sa 
labdhakāmaḥ || etadrahasyamuditaṃ paramaṃ nigūḍhaṃ kutrāpi naiva 
kamanīyamidaṃ kadācit || utkaṃṭhayā tava mayānanu pūrvavṛttaṃ devitvamapi 
vidhinā pravidhīyatā tat || 

ityācārasāratantre haragaurīsaṃvāde paramarahasyātirahasyakathane 
saṃvidākalpe saṃvicchodhanasvīkāravidhiḥ samāptaḥ paṭalaḥ ||

atha samayācāraḥ || 

śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ || 

pārvatyuvāca || 

bhagavan guṇaguṇādhāra sarvatra karuṇānidhe |
idānīṃ śrotumicchāmi samayācāramuttamaṃ || 1 ||

yatpurā samayācāraṃ pūrvāmnāyeṣu kīrtitam |
puṇyaśca śrotumicchāmi ṣaḍāmnāyeṣu kīrtitaṃ || 2 ||

kiṃ nāma samayānātha tasyaścaraṇamuttamam |
tasya saṃketa vijñānaṃ vāṃchitaṃ phalamaśnute || 3 ||

pūrvāmnāyādi cāmnāyādevatāya prakīrtitāḥ |
pṛthak pṛthak kṛte nātha punarvrūhi maheśvara || 4 ||

āmnāyādhiṣṭhitānāṃ ca devatāṃ ca pṛthak pṛthak |
japamālāsanānāṃ ca teṣāṃ vada dayānidhe || 5 ||

bhairava uvāca ||

śṛṇu devi pravakṣyāmi guhyād guhyataraṃ mahat |
samayācārasaṃketaṃ tatvaṃ paramadurlabhaṃ || 6 ||

pūjanādiṣu yaḥ kālo devatā ye pṛthak pṛthak |
sa kālaḥ samayo nāma ye jñātvā'mṛtamaśnute || 7 ||

kāleṣvācaraṇaṃ devi yasya devasya yadvidhiḥ |
taṃ nāma samayācāraṃ devānāmapi durlabhaṃ || 8 ||

77a)

saṃkīrtanāt punardevī rahasyānāṃ rahasyakaṃ |
samayācārasaṃketaṃ nāmnā tatra prakīrtitaṃ || 9 ||

athavā samayācārāt samayācāramucyate |
samayā gopanīyānāṃ sadā gopyā prakīrtitāḥ || 10 ||

vidhinā samayā devī ye bhuṃjaṃti ca sādhakaḥ |
te narāstadgatā nityaṃ bhogaṃ kṛtvā sadā bhuvi || 11 ||

ityevaṃ samayānāmnā siddhagaṃdharvasevitāḥ |
asyā vidhānakathanādidṛtaṃtraṃ prakīrtitaṃ || 12 ||

idānī ya ca yā devī kiṃ nāma samayā bhuvi |
kathitaṃ vidhinā bhadre tat śṛṇuṣva varānane || 13 ||

asya śrīvāgvādinī maṃtrasya brahmā ṛṣirdevī vijayāśaktirgāyatrīcchaṃdo 
vāgvādinī devatā 1 vījaṃ 2 kīlakaṃ 3 śaktiḥ śrīvāgvādinī prītyarthe jape 
viniyogaḥ || 

etairaṃganyāsaṃ kṛtvā saṃvidgṛhītvā evaṃ paṭhanīyaṃ maṃtraṃ || 

aiṁ vada 2 vāgvādinī sāṃ svāhā || ityanena saptābhimaṃtritaṃ bhakṣayet || 

athavā aiṃ jaya 2 vijaya evaṃ brahmasvarūpiṇī sarvajana me vaśamānayet 
yanayā svāhā || ityanena vā japitvā bhakṣayet || 

athānaṃtarato devi samayāstotramuttamaṃ |
yena śrutvā siddhi mūlībhakṣitā phaladā bhavet || 20 ||

saṃvide brahmasaṃbhūte brahmaputri sadā naghe |
bhairavānaṃda hetustu sa paṭhitvā sadā bhava || 21 ||

namāmi yāminī nāthāṃ lekhālaṃkṛtamastakam |
bhavānīṃ bhavasaṃtāpapavirvāṇa sudhānidhim || 22 ||

siddhimūlī śriyo devī hi na vodhapravodhini |
rājāprajāvaśakarī kālakaṃṭhī triśūlinī || 23 ||

ajñāneṃdhana dīptāyā jñānāgni jvālarūpiṇī |
ānaṃdādyāhutiḥ samyak jñānaṃ prayacchati || 24 ||

77b)

daṃḍādirūḍha paripūrita bhogamokṣa śuṃḍakrameṇa madanaṃ 
jayakāminīnām |
ārādhayāmi vahuśatru parājayaṃti viśveśvarīṃ tribhuvane vijayeti devīm || 25 ||

ānaṃdānaṃdinī vaṃde sadānande pada dvayaṃ |
ullāsa kadalīkaṃde svacchaṃde vodharūpiṇī || 26 ||

kavayati kavitā laharīṃ kurute tatvārtha darśanaṃ puṃsāṃ |
apaharati durita nilayaṃ kiṃ kiṃ na karoti saṃvidullāsaḥ || 27 ||

saṃvidāsamayormadhye saṃvideva garīyasī |
bhakṣitābhavanāśāya nirgaṃdhā vodharūpiṇī || 28 ||

susaṃvit chūlinī devī vijayā sa cidaṃ kuru |
vaiṣṇavī tulasī tuṃgā tejo vallīraseśvarī || 29 ||

vimarśādvaitaratvaṃtaṃ vīralakṣmīrmahodarī |
samayā modinī caiva siddhamaulī mahauṣadhī || 30 ||

mātulānī jñānarūpā siddhavidyā sarasvatī |
yāni caitāni nāmāni sevayet siddhimūlikām || 31 ||

samāpnoti parāṃ vidyāṃ bhuktimuktiṃ ca viṃdati |
pāṃḍityaṃ sukavitvaṃ ca maṃtrasiddhiṃ sa viṃdati || 32 ||

samayāṃ gopayed yastu śiṣyabhyaścāpi suṃdari |
vinā na samayā devi bhuktiṃ muktiṃ kathaṃ labhet || 33 ||

vinā samayā devi sāmarthyaṃ naiva jāyate |
sāmarthaṃ sahito devi kāryāṇi sādhayet || 34 ||

vinā samayā pūjāṃ na kutrāpi śubhodayī |
brāhme muhūrte cotthāya pakṣitā pāpanāśinī || 35 ||

tathā sūryodayo jāte madhyāhne bhakṣitā tathā |
tathā parāhne vidhivat sarvapāpavināśani || 36 ||

ardharātrau viśeṣeṇa vāṃchitārtha phalapradaḥ |
vinā tu samayā devi japapūjādikaṃ caret || 37 ||

navasiddhimavāpnoti abhicārāya kalpayet |
apamṛtyuharānūnaṃ rogaśokavināśinī || 38 ||

78a)

duṣṭaśatrupraśamanī sarvalokaniraṃjanī |
siddhayo hyaṇimādyāśca tasya haste sadaiva hi || 39 ||

kāyikaṃ vācikaṃ cāpi mānasaṃ caiva duḥkṛtaṃ |
etat sarvaṃ kṣayaṃ yāṃti brahmahatyādi pātakaṃ || 40 ||

samayābhaktinā yena samayādhāritāstathā |
samayāpāsitā yena rahitaḥ sarvakilviṣaiḥ || 41 ||

sa śivaḥ sa ca yogī ca sa tapasvī satī tathā |
sa eva muktimārgasthaḥ samayā yena bhakṣitā || 42 ||

bhakṣayitvā ca samayā yaṃtraṃ maṃtraṃ japennaraḥ |
samaṃstatphalamāpnoti satyaṃ satyaṃ varānane || 43 ||

vinā ca samyā devi maṃtraṃ japati nityaśaḥ |
alpāyuśca bhavet sadyo devatā kopayeddhruvam || 44 ||

dravyādikamabhāvepi nityaṃ karma na lopayet |
pramādā lopayedyastu nārakī bhavatī dhruvaṃ || 45 ||

dravyaṃ caturdaśavidhi śṛṇu devi pṛthak pṛthak |
teṣāṃ madhyena taṃ dravye dve nahye tu kadācana || 46 ||

kṣīraṃ dadhi ca takraṃ ca ghṛtaṃ kṣaudraṃ guḍaṃ tathā |
śarkarāśītalaṃ toya bhairamapyāranālakaṃ || 47 ||

āphūkaṃ samayā caiva dhattūraṃ saṃviṣaṃ tathā |
dhattūraṃ ca viṣaṃ devi dravyaṃ prāṇaprahārakam || 48 ||

anyāni yāni dravyāṇi ānaṃdārthaṃ ca bhakṣayet |
ānaṃda paramaṃ brahma parāśaktiḥ sadāśivaḥ || 49 ||

dravyaśudhyādi sakalamānaṃdārthaṃ ca bhakṣayet | 
ānande cāpamānepi bhakṣayen na kadācana || 50 ||

atipānād bhavet sadyo japapūjādi niḥphalā |
buddhināśo bhaved devi tato mātrāṃmitāṃ caret || 52 ||

sā mātrā vartate devi yayānaṃdaṃ pravartate |
ityevaṃ samayācāra kathitaśca varānane || 53 ||

78b)

dravyādiśodhanārthaṃ taṃ maṃtraṃ śṛṇu varānane |
guroḥ sakāśāt yaṃtramaṃtraṃ nityaṃ japati yo naraḥ || 54 ||

tenaiva manunāmaṃtrī ṣaḍaṃgaṃnyāsmācaret |
nyāsaṃ kṛtvā punarmaṃtrī dravyādīn maṃtrayed budhaḥ || 55 ||

saptābhimaṃtritaṃ kṛtvā phalaṃ sarvaṃ bhaveddhruvam |
guruṃ śivaṃ tathā devīṃ nivedyāṃ * ca bhakṣayet || 56 ||

kevalaṃ śivarūpohamityātmānaṃ vibhāvayet |
jīvaḥ śivaḥ śivo jīvaḥ sa jīvaḥ kevalaḥ śivaḥ || 57 ||

pāśavaddhaḥ sadājīvaḥ pāśamuktaḥ sadāśivaḥ |
sadāśivamayo bhūtvā dravyādīnāṃ cared yadi || 58 ||

sa kilviṣādi rahitaḥ sākṣādbrahmamayo bhavet |
sadāśivamayo bhūtvā paṃcamudrādikaṃ caret || 59 ||

sarvabrahmamayaṃ yasya sa ca doṣairnna lipyate |
mohād vā kāmalobhādvāyaḥ kaścidiha vartate || 60 ||

sodhamaḥ sādhakānāṃ tu nārakī bhavati dhruvam |
samayo nāma yaḥ kālo mayāyā pūrvasūcitaḥ || 61 ||

tadidānīṃ pravakṣyāmi japārthaṃ śṛṇu suṃdari |
prātamadhyāhnayoḥ kāla pradoṣaśca tṛtīyakaḥ || 62 ||

rātro prathamayāmaśca caturthaḥ parikīrtitaḥ |
paṃcamaṃ tvardharātraṃ ca paṃcakālāḥ prakīrtitāḥ || 63 ||

dinasya praharasyādau kālaḥ prathama īritaḥ |
dinasya madhye yaḥ kālo dvitīyaḥ parikīrtitaḥ || 64 ||

sūrye'ste rajanī prāpte yaḥ kālaḥ sa tṛtīyakaḥ |
brāhme muhūrtemavadhi ardharātrādanaṃtaraṃ || 66 ||

yaḥ kālo ṣaṣṭhako jñeyo devānāmapi durlabhaḥ |
śāṃtiḥ karma tathā vaśyaṃ staṃbhanaṃ dveṣakaṃ tathā || 67 ||

uccāṭanaṃ māraṇaṃ ca ṣaṭkarmāṇi śṛṇu priye |

79a)

śāṃtyarthaṃ prathamaḥ kālo madhyanye dveṣaṇe tathā || 68 ||

tṛtīyaḥ staṃbhane prokto caturtho vaśakarmaṇi |
uccāṭane paṃcamaśca ṣaṣṭho māraṇa karmaṇi || 69 ||

padmāsanaṃ svastike prokteṃ vikaṭaṃ dveṣaṇe tathā |
staṃbhane kukkuṭo vidyādvajrayedvasya karmaṇi || 70 ||

māraṇe bhadrakaṃ vidyā dāsanaṃ ṣaṭ prakīrtitaṃ ||

iti samayāstotram ||

toyaṃ yat śāṃtike proktamagni vaśye prakīrtitaḥ |
pṛthivī staṃbhane jñeyā ākāśe dveṣaṇaṃ tathā || 71 ||

vāyuruccāṭane proktāḥ punaragnirmāraṇe mataḥ |
yasya bhūto deya devī tatamaṃḍalasaṃyutam || 72 ||

tattatkarma vidhānārthaṃ kurvatā niśitātmanā |
śītāṃśu vījaṃ prathamesalisya dvitīyake || 73 ||

kṣoṇī vījaṃ tṛtīye ca vyomavījaṃ caturthakam |
paṃcamaṃ vāyuvījaṃ ca agnivījaṃ tu māraṇe || 74 ||

ityeva samayākālo bheda pūrvaprakāśitaḥ |
athedānīṃ pravakṣyāmi āmnāya phalakaṃ tathā || 75 ||

sarvāmnāyastadā jāto yadādi prācī diśi sthitaḥ |
sadāśivohaṃ bhagavānācāraḥ parikīrtitaḥ || 76 ||

evaṃ dakṣiṇa āmnāyo dakṣiṇasyādiśi sthitaḥ |
evaṃ paścima āmnāya paścimasyāṃ diśi sthitaḥ || 77 ||

evamuttara āmnāyaḥ uttarasyāṃdiśi sthitaḥ |
mukhamūrdhvaṃ kṛtaṃ devīṃ yatproktaṃ tvayi sannidhau || 78 ||

sa ūrdhvāmnāya kathito devāanāmapi durlabhaḥ |
adhomukhaṃ kṛtaṃ devi yatprokto girije priye || 79 ||

adhāmnāya ityuktaḥ satyaṃ satyaṃ varānane |
ṣaḍāmnāyaśca kathitaścautpatti kramanāmataḥ || 80 ||

yasmin yasmiṃścaye devī te te devātha prakīrtitāḥ |
te te devāḥ pravakṣyāmi sādhakānāṃ sukhāya ca || 81 ||

śrīvidyābhedasahitā vālā ca tripurā tathā |
bhuvaneśvarī annapūrṇā pūrvāmnāye prakīrtitāḥ || 82 ||

vasinī vagalā devī tvaritena phalapradā |
mahiṣāsurasaṃhaṃtrī mahālakṣmīśca dakṣiṇā ||

79b)

yasmin devān pravakṣyāmi sādhakānāṃ sukhāya ca || 83 ||

śrīvidyā bhedasahitā vālā ca tripurā ca yā |
bhuvaneśī annapūrṇā sarvāmnāye prakīrtitaḥ || 84 ||

mahāsarasvatī vidyā tathā vāgvādinī ca yā |
pratyaṃgirā bhavānī ca paścimāmnāya devatā || 85 ||

kālikā bheda sahitā tārā bhedaiśca saṃyutā |
māaṃgī bhairavīcchinnā tathā dhūmāvatī matā || 86 ||

uttarāmnāya kathitā śīghrakārya phalapradā |
samasta bheda sahitā devatāya prakīrtitāḥ || 87 ||

dvāviṃśatyakṣarī nāma dakṣiṇāmnāya saṃjñikāṃ |
parā prāsāda maṃtraśca ūrdhvārdhāya prakīrtitaḥ || 88 ||

nāgaśaktyādayo vidyā adhomnāye prakīrtitaḥ |
ūrdhvāmnāyoścādhaśca kevalaṃ mokṣadorbhavet || 89 ||

dharmārtha kāmamokṣārtha āmnāyānye prakīrtitāḥ |
yathokta vidhināva bhakṣe kṛtvā phalamavāpnuyāt || 90 ||

sarvāmnāyadi sarveṣāṃ vidhānārthāpya suṃdari |
kṛtvā yenāśu labhate phalarāśikayoḥ paraṃ || 91 ||

ṣaṭkarma phaladātṝṇāṃ sarvāmnāye prakīrtitaḥ |
uttarāmnāya deveśi teṣāmāśu phalaprada || 92 ||

snātaḥ śuklāṃvaro vīraḥ śuddhaveṣadharā tathā |
devapūjārato nityaṃ tathā ca viparo divā || 93 ||

naktaṃ dravyādikaṃ sarvaṃ yathā lābhena cottamaṃ |
vidhivat kriyate śaktyā saha sarvaphalaṃ bhavet || 94 ||

pūrvāmnāyādi sarveṣāṃ mālāṃ śṛṇu vadāmyahaṃ |
japtā yenāśu labhate phalairdevaiḥ sudurlabham || 95 ||

akṣamālā prathamato mātṛkāraṇa rūpiṇī |
atha muktamayī vāpi mokṣa phalapradāyini || 95 ||

sarvasiddhikarāmālā sarvarājyavaśaṃkarī |

80a)

pravālamālā vaśyārthe sarvakārya phalapradā || 96 ||

māṇikya racitāmālā sāmrājya phaladāyinī |
putrajīvakajāmālā lakṣmīrvidyā pradāyinī || 97 ||

padmākṣamālā racitā yaśo lakṣmīśca jāyate |
suvarṇaraupyamayīmālā sphaṭikī sarvakāmadā || 98 ||

raktacaṃdanajāmālāvaśya bhogapradāyinī |
rudrākṣanirmitā mālā sarvakāmaphalapradā || 99 ||

sarvamālā prapūjārthaṃ caṃdanādi pralepitā |
samāśritya japed vidyāṃ yathokta phalamaśnute || 100 ||

etāmālāśca subhagā paṃcāmnāyeṣu pūjitā |
uttarāmnāye yā mālā girije te vadāmyaham || 101 ||

atharvaṇamayī mālā sarvotkṛṣṭā matā ca yā |
mahāśaṃkhamayī cātha vāṃchitārtha phalapradā || 102 ||

sphāṭikai racitācārtha rudrākṣa phalasaṃbhavā |
svarṇādi ratnaparyaṃtaṃ racitaṃ phaladā matā || 103 ||

guṃjāmālā tathā kāryā vāṃchitārtha phalapradā |
uduṃvara phalasyaiva sūkṣmasya ca kṛtā ca yā || 104 ||

ityādi mālā deveśi kurvīta vidhivannaraḥ |
athedānīṃ pravakṣyāmi yaṃtrasya vidhimuttamaṃ || 105 ||

bhūrye ṣaḍvarṣa paryaṃtaṃ tāmre dvādaśameva ca |
rukme ca ṣaḍva ca * mahāśaṃkhe sahasrakam || 106 ||

svarṇe ca sphaṭike caiva varṣasaṃkhyā na vidyate |
sahasā kārya sidhyarthaṃ sthāpayet sphaṭikopari || 107 ||

yathokta vidhinālikhya yathoktaṃ pūjanaṃ sadā |
vāṃchitaṃ labhate maṃtrī nānyathā labhate phalam || 108 ||

āsanāni pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu devi vadāmyahaṃ |
meṣāsanaṃ tu vaśyārthe ākarṣe vyāghracarma ca || 109 ||

80b)

śāṃtau mṛgājinaṃ śastaṃ mokṣeṣu vyāghracarmaṇi |
gocarma staṃbhane devi staṃbhane ca gavājinaṃ || 110 ||

carmoṣṭrasya tu uccāṭe dveṣe śvānasya carma ca |
māraṇe mahiṣaṃ vidyāt kramoddiṣṭaṃ tu vā caret || 111 ||

sarvakāmapradaṃ devi vastrapaṭṭāsanaṃ tathā |
ūrṇāsanaṃ kaṃbalādyaṃ sarvakarma supūjitaṃ || 112 ||

duḥkhadāridryaśamanaṃ vidyākāṭhāsanaṃ priye |
svarṇādi raktajaṃ devi mahāsaubhāgyavardhanam || 113 ||

śṛṇu devi viśeṣeṇa cottarāmnāyamāsanam |
yenāśu labhate puṇyaṃ phalaṃ caiva sudurlabham || 114 ||

savāsanaṃ tu subhage mṛtamuṃḍāsanaṃ tathā |
sā darśāsanakaṃ cāpi maithunāsanakaṃ tathā || 115 ||

kṛta maithunakaṃ cāpi vāṃchitārtha phalapradaṃ || 116 ||

japasthānādi deveśi siddhitīrthāniyāni ca |
siddhipīṭhaṃ siddhikṣetre girau devālaye tathā || 117 ||

vaṭavṛkṣe viśvavṛkṣe raṃbhāyā vipinepi vā |
nadyāditīre vā kuryādguhā parvatamastake || 118 ||

śṛṇu devi viśeṣeṇa uttarāmnāya hetave |
veśyāgṛhe śmaśāne vā gatvā maithuna samācaret || 119 ||

japādikaṃ tato devi kṛtvā su labhate phalaṃ |
athavā svagṛhe rātrau bhaktimānyaḥ samācaret || 120 ||

sa prāpnoti phalaṃ sarvaṃ ciṃtā bhayavivarjitaḥ |
athedānīṃ pravakṣyāmi bhagapūjāṃ samāsataḥ || 121 ||

gurau sakāśāt yanmaṃtraṃ nityaṃ japati sādhakaḥ |
tenaiva manunāmaṃtrī bhagapūjāṃ karoti ca || 122 ||

tadā tu bhagamadhye tu ciṃtayed brahmarūpiṇīṃ |
śivo bhūtvā smared dehe tvātmānaṃ ca vibhāvayet || 123 ||

śaktiḥ sā tanmayī vidyāttavāvai maithunaṃ caret |
yathokta kurute devi prāpyate paramaṃ padam || 124 ||

yāni kalpita maṃtrāṇi kathitāni varānane |

81a)

jñātavyā yadvidhā devi sarvataṃtreṣu niścitaṃ || 125 ||

maṃtrāḥ kecit prakathyaṃte kaścid vidyā prakīrtitāḥ |
urṇāmadevatā maṃtrā vidyā strīnāma tat smṛtā || 126 ||

napuṃsakā bhavaṃtyete maṃtrāḥ sarvasamīritaḥ |
pumāṃso huṃ phaḍaṃtāsyuḥ vājāṃtāsyuḥ striyo matāḥ || 127 ||

napuṃsakā namoṃtāsyustrividhājātibhiḥ punaḥ |
graṃthanaṃ ca vidarbhaśca saṃpuṭo rodhanaṃ tathā || 128 ||

yogaḥ phalavadityeke kathitā phaṭ su karmasu |
nāmavarṇāśca vidhinā maṃtrāṇāṃtaritāstathā || 129 ||

kuryādgraṃthanaṃ nāma śāṃti karmaṇi śasyate |
maṃtrārṇa dvaya madhyasthe sādhyānāmākṣaraṃ likhet || 130 ||

vidarbharāṣa vijayo vaśya karmaṇi śasyate |
ādāvaṃte ca maṃtrasyānnāmnosau saṃpuṭasmṛtaḥ || 131 ||

praśastastaṃbhane devi yathoktaṃ kriyate yadi |
nāmna adyaṃta madhyeṣu maṃtrasthodrodanaṃ mataṃ || 132 ||

vidveṣaṇa vidhāneṣu praśastamidamīritaṃ |
maṃtrasyāṃte bhaven nāma yogaḥ proccāṭane mataḥ || 133 ||

ante nāmno bhaven maṃtraḥ pallavo māraṇe mataḥ |
āgataḥ śivavaktrācca gataśca girijāmukhe || 134 ||

tena āgama taṃtrāṇi kathitāni varānane |
pāṇikāni ca śāstrāṇi kathitānyāgamasya ca || 135 ||

tāni tāni prakathyaṃte lokācārāṇi suṃdari |
ācāraḥ kathito yastu tayā ca kṛtavānbhuvi || 136 ||

tasyācārasya nāmnā ca kulācāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ |
paṃcamudrādi rahito dakṣiṇācārasaṃjñakaḥ || 137 ||

nānāmaṃtrāṇi deveśi yāmalāni pṛthak pṛthak |
aparāṇi ca sarvāṇi maṃtrāṇāṃ hṛdayāṇi ca || 138 ||

samāsataḥ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu devi vadāmyahaṃ || 138 ||

81b)

catuḥṣaṣṭhīni taṃtrāṇi yāmalānyaṣṭa suṃdari |
amarāṇi ca trīṇi syuḥ kathayāmi śubhānane || 139 ||

taṃtrāṇi vahudhā devi mayā pūrvaṃ prakāśitaṃ |
yāmalānyatra vakṣyāmi amarāṇi tathā punaḥ || 140 ||

viṣṇubrahmaśivānāṃ ca yāmalāni pṛthak pṛthak |
śaktergaṇapateścaiva kārtike yasya pṛthak pṛthak || 141 ||

sūryacaṃdramasoścaiva kathitāni varānane |
uḍḍīśaḍāmaraṃ nāma bhūtaḍāmarakaṃ tathā || 142 ||

śaktiḍāmarakaṃ nāma amarāṇi ca pārvati |
kathaṃ cādya pravakṣyāmi taṃtrāṇi ca varānane || 143 ||

catuṣaṣṭhi ca taṃtrāṇi vikhyātaṃ vāmakeśvare |
tasmānnoktāni taṃtreṣu kulācāra guru śṛṇu || 144 ||

āgamācāranipunaḥ sarvaśāstrabhṛtāṃvara |
suveṣadhāri dakṣaśca satyavaktā priyaṃvada || 145 ||

eva lakṣaṇa saṃyuktaścāgamasya gururmataḥ |
śiṣyastvayi guṇairyukto gurubhaktirataḥ sadā || 146 ||

dharmakarmādi yuktaśca gurumaṃtra parāyaṇaḥ |
satyamabdhirgurau maṃtre devapūjana tatparaḥ || 147 ||

guruṇoddiṣṭamārgeṇa kṛtavuddhirudāradhīḥ |
evaṃ lakṣaṇasaṃyukto śiṣyaścāpi parīkṣakaḥ || 148 ||

māyā nindādi rahitaścālasyādi vivarjitaḥ |
samayācārasaṃpanno dhanāḍhyaśca triyāvaraḥ || 149 ||

śrīsadāśiva uvāca || 1

dravyaṃ pūjāṃ pravakṣyāmi pūjakābhīṣṭa siddhayet |
jñātvā maṃtraṃ vinā samyak phalamāpnoti pūjane || 150 ||

madyaṃ māṃsaṃ tathā matsyaṃ mudrā maithunameva ca |
makārāḥ paṃca śubhage sāṃga karmasu hetave || 151 ||

yā surā sarvamaṃtreṣu kathitā bhuvi durlabhā |
tathānāma bhaved devi tīrthaṃ yadjñāna durlabhaṃ || 152 ||

82a)

paśūnāṃ bhakṣa yogyānāṃ māṃsaṃ devi vinirmitam |
devimaṃtre ca vidhivat tasyoktā siddhiruttamāḥ || 153 ||

māṃsa bhakṣaṇe kathitāa ye matsyāśca varānane |
te rahasye mayā proktā mīnāḥ siddhipradāyakāḥ || 154 ||

guḍādi madhye nikṣipya kurvaṃti dyuti vardhinī |
mudrā tāṃ vidhi prāhuścaṇakādīṃśca bharjitān || 155 ||

yāroṭikāpolikā ca bhayeṣu kathitā śubhā |
tasyānāma bhaved devi mudrāmukti pradāyinī || 156 ||

bhage liṃgasya yogena maithunaṃ yadbhavet priye |
tasya nāma bhaved devi paṃcamaṃ parikīrtitam || 157 ||

prathamaṃ tu bhaven madye māṃse cāpi dvitīyakaṃ |
matsye hyapi tṛtīyaṃ syānāma mudrā caturthakaṃ || 158 ||

paṃcame maithunaṃ vidyā paṃcaite nāma tat smṛtā |
paṃcānāṃ paṃcanāmānimakārāṇi varānane || 159 ||

prathamasya dvitīyasya tṛtīyasya caturthayoḥ |
paṃcamasya tathā devimakārāḥ paṃcadurlabhāḥ || 160 ||

paṃcamaṃ devi sarveṣu mama prāṇo bhavet priye |
paṃcamena vinā devi caṃḍīmaṃtraṃ vṛthā japet || 161 ||

yadi sarvamakāreṣu bhrāṃtiṃ ca kurute priye |
tasya siddhiḥ kathaṃ devi śaktimaṃtraṃ japet kathaṃ || 162 ||

paṃcamena vinā devi bhuktimuktiḥ kathaṃ bhavet |
paṃcamena vinā devi kathaṃ ca phaladā bhavet || 163 ||

paṃcamena vinā devi yadā naṃdo bhaveddhruvaṃ |
tannāma mokṣo viduṣāṃ anudhānāṃ ca pātakaṃ || 164 ||

ānaṃdaṃ paramaṃ brahmamakārānaṃdasūcakaṃ |
tathā viśeṣato devi paṃcamaṃ parikīrtitaṃ || 165 ||

bhagasya smaraṇe puṇyaṃ bhagasya darśane tathā |
bhagasya pūjane puṇyaṃ bhagasya paṃcame tathā || 166 ||

bhagasya paṃcame devi yatsukhaṃ samajāyate |

82b)

na tatsukhaṃ japairhomairnnadānaistapasā tathā || 167 ||

paṃcamasya kṛte devi yatpuṇyaṃ samajāyate |
na tatpuṇyasamaṃ devi koṭi tīrthādi darśanaṃ || 168 ||

japahomastathādānaṃ dīkṣāyogādi kalpanā |
kṛtapaṃcamabhaktasya kalāṃ nārhaṃti ṣoḍaśīṃ || 169 ||

trayodaśābdādūrdhvaṃ hi paṃcaviṃśati vārṣikīṃ |
aprasūnā viśeṣeṇa paṃcamārhā bhavet priye || 170 ||

aprasūtā viśeṣeṇa prasūtā vā prasūtikā |
avaśyaṃ paṃcamaṃ kuryācchaktimātraṃ maheśvari || 171 ||

paṃcame ca kṛte devi yat kuryāt pūjanādikaṃ |
tadakṣayaṃ labhet puṇyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā || 172 ||

guruṃ saṃtoṣayet tatra yat patnī vā sutā divā |
nānābharaṇavastrādyaistathā dravyeṇa suṃdari || 173 ||

paṃcamārthā yathā śaktistasyāṃ kuryācca paṃcamaṃ |
tasyāstotraṃ prakuryācca viśeṣeṇa śṛṇu priye || 174 ||

dravyeṇa bhūṣaṇaiścaiva vasanā liṃganādibhiḥ |
snānārthaṃ devatānāṃ ca rahasyaṃ paramaṃ śṛṇu || 175 ||

yena snāte kṛte devi devatā suprasīdati |
rātrau paṃcamakāreṣu kṛtvā paṃcamamuttamam || 176 ||

bhagamadhyeṣu yaddravyaṃ gṛhnīyācca prayatnataḥ |
tasyā kuṃḍodbhavaṃ toyaṃ vijñeyaṃ bhuktimuktidam || 177 ||

labhate bhāgya yogeṇa devatānāṃ ca durlabhaṃ |
tasmin kiṃcijjalaṃ kṣiptvā tāmrapātreṣu dhārayet || 178 ||

taṃ dravyaṃ snānamātreṇa devatā suprasīdati |
striyo rajaśca prathama yasminvayasi jāyate || 179 ||

gṛhīyātrāśu śubhage brahmādīnāṃ ca durlabhaṃ |
svayaṃbhū kusumaṃ nāma devatānāṃ ca prītaye || 180 ||

yadi bhāgyavasād devi labhate kusumaṃ tvidam |
tattasvadevatānāṃ ca prakuryāt snānamuttamaṃ || 181 ||

vāṃchitaṃ labhate maṃtrī satyaṃ satyaṃ varānane |

83a)

svagururdattamaṃtreṇa ṣaḍaṃganyāsamācaret || 182 ||

śaktidehe svadehe vā paṃcamaṃ kārayet tataḥ |
tato japādikaṃ kuryāccākṣayaṃ labhate phalam || 183 ||

idaṃ rahasyaṃ kathitaṃ devatā snāna hetave |
ṣaḍāmnāyeṣu taṃtreṣu rahasyamidamīritam || 184 ||

uttarāmnāya maṃtreṣu prakuryācca viśeṣataḥ |
jīvatī bhartarī nārīṇāṃ paṃcamaṃ kārayet priye || 185 ||

tasyā bhagasya yadravyaṃ taccakuṃḍodbhavamucyate |
mṛte bhartari nārīṇāṃ paṃcamaṃ kārayed yadi || 186 ||

tasyā bhagasya yaddravyaṃ tacca golodbhavaṃ mṛtaṃ |
kuṃḍagolodbhave dravyaṃ abhāve śṛṇu suṃdari || 187 ||

kathaṃ snānaṃ prakuryācca devatātoṣa hetave |
yasya kasya taroḥ puṇyaṃ gṛhīcāśu prayatnataḥ || 188 ||

teṣā madhye dvayaṃ grāhyaṃ hastābhyāṃ manasā tadā |
ubhayoḥ paṃcamaṃ tatra kurvīta vidhivannaraḥ || 189 ||

raktacaṃdana ghṛṣṭena jalai caiva kṣipet tadā |
tajjalena prakurvīta devatā snānamuttamaṃ || 190 ||

vāṃchitaṃ phalamāpnoti satyaṃ satyaṃ varānane |
vallī puṣpāṇi sarvāṇi taroḥ puṣpāṇi yāni ca || 191 ||

auṣadhīṣu ca sarvāsu yāni puṣpāṇikāni ca |
tāni sarvāṇi śubhage devatābhyo niyojayet || 192 ||

sarvāmnāye ṣvadhiṣṭhānaṃ tulasī varjitāni ca |
aparājitāḥ puṣpaṃ ca dvayaṃ puṣpaṃ ca yadbhavet || 193 ||

karavīrasya yatpuṇyaṃ yatpuṣpaṃ budhvajīvakaṃ |
kamalasya ca yatpuṣpaṃ yatpuṣpaṃ paṃcakasya ca || 194 ||

viśeṣataśca yogyāni sarvapuṣpeṣu suṃdari |
patrāṇāṃ vilvapatrāṇi pūjārthe ca śu * nane || 195 ||

athedānīṃ pravakṣyāmi japārthe pīṭhamuttamaṃ |
kṛte pūrṇagiriṃ yogyaṃ tretā upāna saṃjñakaṃ || 196 ||

83b)

jālaṃdhare dvāpare tu kāmapīṭhaṃ kalauyuge |
catuḥpīṭhāni śubhage śaktideheṣu yāni tat || 197 ||

tāni catvāri vakṣyāmi guhyādguhyatarāṇi ca |
śaktiḥ sarvaśarīraṃ tu pīṭhaṃ pūrṇagiriṃ mataṃ || 198 ||

tasyāḥ śiraśca subhage uḍyānaṃ kīrtitaṃ mayā |
stanauṃ jālaṃdhare jñeyaṃ kāmapīṭhaṃ bhagasmṛtaṃ || 199 ||

sarveṣu kāmapīṭhaṃ yaddevānāmapi durlabhaṃ |
yeṣu pīṭheṣu saṃsthitvāyaṃ yaṃ yaṃ maṃtraṃ japet priye || 200 ||

tattasya phalamāpnoti devatā suprasīdati |
sarvāṃtaphalamāpnoti devatā suprasīdati || 201 ||

sarvāsāṃ validānaṃ ca devatānāṃ śṛṇu priye || 201 ||

yena kṛtvāsulabhaye yathecchaṃ phalamuttamaṃ |
nityaṃ svabhojane kāle mūlamaṃtreṇa sādhakaḥ || 202 ||

kārayed validānaṃ ca bhojanāt prathamaṃ priye |
tataścānaṃdate devi śucistadgatavān bhavet || 203 ||

valiṃ samuddhare yatnādekāṃte sthāpayet tadā |
sthāpayitvā valiṃ tatra viharecca yathā sukhaṃ || 204 ||

uttarāmnāya deveśi mātaṃgīyā prakīrtitāḥ |
tasyāṃ valiṃ bhojanāṃte vinaivācamane kṛte || 205 ||

mūlamaṃtreṇa śubhage valiṃ kṛtvā prayatnataḥ |
kiṃcijjapādikaṃ kṛtvā tata ācamanādikaṃ || 206 ||

punaścarātrau sarveṣāṃ valiṃ kṛtvā prayatnataḥ |
yathokta vidhinā kuryād yathoktaṃ phalamaśnute || 207 ||

baliśca vividho devyaḥ sātviko rājasastathā |
sātviko valarākhyāto māṃsaraktādi varjitaḥ || 208 ||

rājaso māṃsaraktādi yuktaḥ saṃprocyate priye |
sādhakāstrividhā proktā sātvikā rājasāmatā || 209 ||

tāmasāśca tathā devī teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇaṃ || 210 ||

sātvikaṃ validānādi nityaṃ kuryāt prayatnataḥ || 211 ||

84a)

rājasorājasa guṇairyukto nityaṃ śubhānane |
rājasaṃbalidānādi suveṣai rājasairyutaḥ || 212 ||
