tāmasāstāmasaguṇairoṣādi saṃyutaḥ priye |
na śraddhā balidāneṣu pūjanādiṣu suṃdari || 213 ||

na stotra paṭhane devi nāma mātreṇa sādhakaḥ |
athedānīṃ pravakṣyāmi mama maṃtrāṇi suṃdari || 214 ||

yānyatra mama maṃtrāṇi prasiddhāni svabhāvataḥ |
aghorākhya mahāmaṃtramāpaduddhāraṇaṃ tathā || 215 ||

ciṃtāmaṇiṃ tathā devi tathā mṛtyuṃjayaṃvaraṃ |
caṃḍovaraṃ ca subhage ardhanārī naṭeśvaraṃ || 216 ||

nānā taṃtreṣu deveśi mama maṃtrāṇi yāni ca |
jñātavyāni sadā bhadre ṣaḍāmnāyeṣu tāni ca || 217 ||

vāmācāreṇa vā devi japtvā phalamavāpnuyāt |
dakṣiṇācāra yogena japtvā phalamavāpnuyāt || 218 ||

viṣopataśca śubhage mama maṃtrāṇi yāni ca |
sarvāmnāyena vidhinā śīghrakāla phalapradaḥ || 219 ||

nānā pāpaharā devī maṃtrāḥ kāmadughā priye |
yaṃ yaṃ maṃtraṃ jape devi vīrastadgatamānasaḥ || 220 ||

taṃ taṃ bhāvaṃ samāsādya phalaṃ tallabhate naraḥ |
tava maṃtrāṇi deveśi mama maṃtrāṇi yāni ca || 221 ||

yāni yāni prasiddhāni tāni tāni ca tāni ca |
yathā svayaṃbhuvā devi vedāścatvāra kīrtitaḥ || 222 ||

tātavyānādi saṃsiddhāṃ paryeṇya devatāḥ |
pāraṃparyepi te jñeyā śrutāmnāyeṣu bhedataḥ || 223 ||

tathā tvayi mayā proktā ṣaḍāmnāyāśca saṃnidhau |
sa cāmnāya śruti jñeyaḥ śrutiśca vedato labhet || 224 ||

atastvayāpi girije gopanīyaḥ svayonivat |

84b)

athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi rahasyaṃ paramaṃ śubhaṃ || 225 ||

bahumaṃtrī yadā * * sādhako daiva yogataḥ |
atra kasya japaṃ kuryāt sajjanādibhireva ca || 226 ||

sarvadeva namaskāraṃ nityaṃ kuryāt prayatnataḥ |
jāpādikaṃ tatasyaiva yasya saṃgate manaḥ || 227 ||

gurorgṛhīta maṃtraṃ tu japtvā tyajati sādhakaḥ |
duṣṭācārāt pramādādvā ālasyādvāpi suṃdari || 228 ||

śaṃkayā vā gṛhītasya kathanaṃ yatra kutracit |
hīnavīryamavāpnoti maṃtrādikaṃ varānane || 229 ||

ityādi doṣanāśārthaṃ vidhānaṃ śṛṇu sāṃpratam |
prathamaṃ jananaṃ nāma jīvanaṃ tu dvitīyakaṃ || 230 ||

tṛtīyaṃ tāḍanaṃ nāma gopanaṃ daśamaṃ smṛtaṃ |
paṃcamamabhiṣekaśca vimukhī karṇaṣaṣṭhakam || 231 ||

āpyāyanaṃ saptamaṃ tu aṣṭamaṃ tarpaṇaṃ mataṃ |
navamaṃ dīpanaṃ nāma gopanaṃ daśamaṃ smṛtaṃ || 232 ||

manūnāṃ mātṛkā madhyāduddhāro jananaṃ mataṃ |
maṃtravarṇān japennityaṃ praṇavāṃtaritān kramāt || 233 ||

etajjīvanakaṃ nāma tāḍanaṃ śṛṇu dhāparaṃ |
manuvarṇān samālipya tāḍayeccaṃdanāṃbhasā || 234 ||

pratyekaṃ vāyunāmaṃtrī tāḍanaṃ nāma tat smṛtam || 235 ||

manulipya vidhānena yadā maṃtrārṇasaṃkhyayā |
aśvattha pallavairmaṃtramabhiṣiṃcedviśuddhaye || 236 ||

saṃciṃtyamanasā maṃtrī jyotirmaṃtreṇa nirdahet |
maṃtre malatraye devi vimalī karaṇe tvidam || 237 ||

tāla vyomāgni manuyuk daṃḍījyotīrthamanurmataḥ |
kuśodakena japtena pratyaṇaṃ prokṣaṇaṃ manoḥ || 238 ||

tena maṃtreṇa vidhivadetadāpyāyanaṃ śubhaṃ |
nayunā vāriṇā maṃtra tarpaṇaṃ tarpaṇaṃ bhavet || 239 ||

85a)

tāramāyā ramāyogaṃ manodvīpanamucyate |
japyamānasya gopanaṃ tvapanaṃtvaprakāśanam || 240 ||

ete ca daśasaṃskārāḥ sarvamaṃtreṣu gopitā |
etān kṛtā japen maṃtraṃ sa doṣarahitaḥ priye || 241 ||

nirguṇaṃ yatparaṃ brahma ākādi vivarjitaṃ |
sākāraṃ yad bhaved devi vahudhā tarpaṇādiṣu || 242 ||

dṛśyate tu tathā cātra rādyātvaṃ sarva dehinām |
ekamevāparaṃbrahma jyotirūpamanakṣaram || 243 ||

sākāraṃ yadi jāyeta svecchayā tu varānane |
rūpadvayaṃ tathā bhūtvā dehināṃ dehamavyayaṃ || 244 ||

bhakārāṃte ca tadbrahma liṃgākāraṃ svarūpataḥ |
kecit subhage jānaṃti liṃgākārasya rūpiṇaḥ || 245 ||

bhagākārasya seveta viduṣo jñāninaḥ sadā |
strījāti rūpā sarvatra sarvadeheṣu yā matā || 246 ||

sā śaktirūpā vijñeyā puruṣaḥ śivarūpavān |
tāsāṃ bhagastrikoṇaṃ ca kuṇḍaṃ proktaṃ tu cottamaṃ || 247 ||

puruṣasya liṃgaṃ yad devi śivo jñeyaḥ sanātanaḥ |
tatta teṣāṃ viśeṣāśca naradehe varānane || 248 ||

śaktiḥ śivaśca vijñeyo mama saṃketamuttamam |
bhagaḥ kuṃḍaṃ ca subhage śivo liṃgaṃ prakīrtitam || 249 ||

rajastu agniḥ subhage bhagamadhyeṣu kṣepaṇam |
ājyarūpaṃ mataṃ śukraṃ manohotā prakīrtitaḥ || 250 ||

phalarūpaṃ ca tatraiva eṣā saṃsārakāmanā |
evaṃ vijñāyayo maṃtrī manorūpaṃ ca brahmavit || 251 ||

nityaṃ homayitā devi tasya puṇyamanaṃtakam |
yaṃ yaṃ kāmādikaṃ devi manasā ciṃtyakārayet || 252 ||

na doṣastatra vijñeyastaṃ taṃ kāmamavāpnuyāt |
yathokta devatā cārādyathokta phalamaśnute || 253 ||

85b)

āyurlakṣmīryaśodevi kīrtiṃ ca mokṣamāpnuyāt |
asmin stotre ca samayā yāmayā parikīrtitāḥ || 254 ||

sā pūrvaṃ vijayākalpe caturthāṃsaṃprakīrtitāḥ |
imāṃ vidyāṃ ca taṃtresmin rahasyā ye prakīrtitāḥ || 255 ||

goptavyāśca prayatnena kathanīyā na kasyacit || 256 ||

gopyāgopya punargopyāgopyāgopyā punaḥ punaḥ || 256 ||

gopyāgopyā punargopyā jananījāra garbhavat |
aṃtṛśaktāśca subhage vahiḥ śaivā ca vaiṣṇavāḥ || 257 ||

evaṃ ye sādhakāloke phalamāyurnasaṃśayaḥ |
ācāro mama deveśi tavācāropi ca priye || 258 ||

divaso gopanaṃ kṛtvā rātrau caiva samācaret |
nānāśakti sahālāpairye kurvaṃti ca sādhakāḥ || 259 ||

te śīghrakālāṃ subhage phalaṃ prāptāśca mānavāḥ |
ādra śuṣkavibhāgena dvidhācāraḥ punaḥ śṛṇu || 260 ||

ādrācāraḥ sa vijñeyo makaraiḥ paṃcabhiryutaḥ |
makaraiḥ paṃcarahitaḥ śuṣkācāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ || 261 ||

kalau viśeṣato devi ādrācāra phalapradaḥ |
pūrvāmnāyeṣu kathitā nānā taṃtre ca devatāḥ || 262 ||

vidyāmaṃtra vibhāgena te devāścādrataḥ kalau |
viśeṣāt phaladā devi sādhakānāṃ jitātmanām || 263 ||

rahasyaṃ śṛṇu deveśi paramāṃ gopanaṃ sadā |
sarvāmnāyāśca kathitāstava pārśve pṛthak pṛthak || 264 ||

sarvebhyaścottarāmnāya paścāt saṃkīrtite mayā |
gopyādgopyataro guhyo guhyādguhyataro mahān || 265 ||

uttarāmnāya subhage sadā gopyaḥ prakīrtitaḥ |
yadivettvat samāloke nārī bhavati niścalā || 266 ||

86a)

matsamaḥ puruṣo devi sādhako yadi bhūtale |
bhrāṃti māyāti rahitastadā sādhayituṃ priye || 267 ||

saktaśca sādhako devi anyathā hāsyatāṃ vrajet |
āgamācārastu priye sarvadā gopanaḥ smṛtaḥ || 268 ||

uttarāmnāyo deveśi viśeṣād gopanaḥ kalau |
sādhakāstu kalau devi māyā nidrādi saṃyutaḥ || 269 ||

ajitendriyā loke yā yathoktācāravarjitāḥ |
ahaṃ vuddhiratā nityaṃ tasmādgopyādviśeṣataḥ || 270 ||

suparīkṣitāya putrāya vinītāya prakāśayet |
śraṣṭhebhaḥ sādhakebhyaśca na prakāśyaṃ kadācana || 271 ||

yadi cedvai varārohe sādhakopi prakāśayet |
siddhihānistu labhate sadā tasya prakāśanāt || 271 ||

atastu gopayed devi yaditvaṃ mama vallabhā |
uttarāmnāye yā mālā kathitā bhuvidurlabhā || 272 ||

tāsāmabhāve subhage mālāṃ śṛṇu vadāmyahaṃ |
atha varṇamayī mālā alābhe hastayarvajā || 273 ||

mahāśaṃkhamayī mālā abhāve sphāṭikī matā |
sphāṭikyāśca abhāve tu rudrākṣa phalanirmitā || 274 ||

rudrākṣamālā bhāve tu kamasya phalaiścayā |
āsanānyuttarāmnāye kathitāni śubhānane || 275 ||

sarvābhāve vyāghracarma aiṇaṃ vā kaṃvalādikaṃ |
yatra pūjā abhāve tu pratimāsu prapūjayet || 276 ||

jale agnau pṛthivyāṃ ca sūrye vā hṛdi suṃdari |
tāmre vā lekhayitvā tu nityaṃ vā sarpajet priye || 277 ||

dīpasya jyotirmadhye tu mūlamaṃtreṇa pūjayet |
sarvatra sarvapūjāṃsu mūle naiva prapūjayet || 278 ||

86b)

visarjanāṃta mūlena manasā brahmaciṃtayet |
sarvadravyādya bhāve tu ārdrakaṃ tu prakīrtitam || 279 ||

jalaṃ vā tatra kṣīraṃ vā bhakṣayet karmamācaret |
makāra paṃcābhāve tu paṃcamaṃ kārayet priye || 280 ||

abhāve paṃcame devi manasā paṃcamaṃ caret |
evaṃ śrutvā tato devi samayācāramuttamaṃ || 281 ||

sā śivā ca prasannā bhūdyāthā tathya prakāśanāt |
śivopyaṃtaḥ prasannobhūt svayaṃ ca parameśvaraḥ || 282 ||

tadā prasanna manasā uvāca girijāṃ prati |
sarvāṇyāgama taṃtrāṇi yāni yānyapi suṃdari || 283 ||

taṃtrādīṇyapi sarvāṇi vidyāmnāyādi kānyapi |
caturyugeṣu vartaṃte pārapāyopadeśataḥ || 284 ||

teṣāṃ vedayitā kecinna samarthosmi bhūtale |
kṛpayā tava deveśi kiṃcit kiṃ varṇitaṃ śubhaṃ || 285 ||

ato jñātvā mayā devi yat kiṃcidvarṇitaṃ śubhaṃ |
etatsarvaṃ tu niyataṃ sarvasvamida me priye || 286 ||

rājyaṃ deyaṃ śirodeyaṃ na deyaṃ taṃtramadbhutaṃ |
ṣaḍāmnāyeṣu kathitaṃ taṃtraṃ paramadurlabhaṃ || 287 ||

tathā gopyaṃ ca śubhage mātṛjārapadaṃ yathā |
yadi cedvai varārohe mayā tubhyaṃ prakāśitaṃ || 288 ||

atastu gopayennityaṃ yaditvaṃ mama vallabhā || 289 ||

iti śrīpārvatīśvarasaṃvāde samayācāraṃ sampūrṇam || 


śrīgurugaṇeśāya namaḥ || 

śrīmadbhairavaśekharaṃ pravilasaccaṃdrāmṛtaṃ plāvitaṃ 
kṣetrādhīśvarayoginī munigaṇaiḥ siddhaiḥ samārādhitaṃ | 
ānaṃdārṇavakaṃ parātmakamidaṃ sākṣāt trikhaṃḍāmṛtaṃ vande 
śrīprathamaṃkarāṃvujagataṃ pātraṃ viśuddhipradaṃ || 1 || 

87a)

haimaṃ mīna rasāvahaṃdathitayādattaṃ ca peyādibhiḥ kiṃciccaṃcala 
raktapaṃkajadṛśā tasmai samāveditam |
vāme svādutaraṃ viśuddhikaraṇaṃ pāṇau nidhāyātmake vaṃde pātramahaṃ 
dvitīyamadhunā naṃdaika saṃvardhanaṃ || 2 ||

sarvāmnāya kalākalāpa kalitaṃ kautūhala dyotanaṃ caṃdropendra kṛśānu 
śaṃbhu vasā brahmādibhiḥ sevitaṃ | 
dhyātaṃ devagaṇaiḥ paraṃ munivarairmokṣārthibhiḥ sarvadāḥ vaṃde 
pātramahaṃ tṛtīyamadhunā vijñānavodhakṣamaṃ || 3 ||

dravyaṃ mīnarasāvahaṃ harihara brahmādibhiḥ pūjitaṃ mudrā maithuna dharma 
karma nirataṃ kṣārāmlatiktāśritaṃ |
ācāryāṣṭaka siddhabhairava kulādhīśena saṃśodhitaṃ pāyāt 
paṃcamakāratatva sahitaṃ pātraṃ caturthaṃ namaḥ || 4 ||

sarvaṃ dharmakalāgamādhika paraṃ vedairmukhairbhāṣitaṃ devānāmapi 
durlabhaṃ sukhakaraṃ guptaṃ rahasyānvitaṃ |
ānaṃdodbhavanādaviṃdu paramā yogīna sadbhairavaṃ pītaṃ brahmamayaṃ 
sadoditakaraṃ pātraṃ bhaje paṃcamaṃ || 5 ||

chatraṃ cāmara bhadrapīṭha paramānaṃdodhikaḥ pātumāṃ rāmārājya 
manoharaṃ śubhakaraṃ saṃyojya sāmrājyadaṃ |
nānā vyādhi bhavāṃ *? kāra haraṇaṃ janmādi nirnāśanaṃ śrīmatsuṃdari 
tarpaṇādravarasaṃpātraṃ bhaje ṣaṣṭhamaṃ || 6 ||

jāgratsvapnasuṣupti tūryapurato caitanya sākṣīpradaṃ 
vidyudbhāskaracaṃdrasendra dhanuṣo jyotiḥ kalāvyādhitam |
īḍā piṃgala madhyamādi calayā satkuṇḍalī cordhagaṃ pātraṃ saptama 
pūraṇe natvarayānandādikaṃ pātumān || 7 ||

khaḍgaṃ pādukamajjanaṃ ca guṭikā sārasvataṃ yatpadaṃ 
mṛtyurvaṃcanamugrakālaharaṇaṃ dehasthitaṃ kāraṇaṃ |

87b)

vācā siddhikaraṃ manasthirakaraṃ vaśyājjagajjoṣitaṃ pātraṃ 
cāṣṭamamaṣṭasiddhikaraṇaṃ prauḍhaṃ prasannaṃ sadā || 8 ||

sarvānaṃdakaraṃ sadāśivapadaṃ dvaṃdvaikamuktipradaṃ 
sāmrājyaṃ sukhadaṃ manorathakaraṃ ajñānavidhvaṃsanaṃ |
āyuḥkīrtiyaśovivardhanakaraṃ saṃsāramohachidaṃ pātraṃ 
yannavanātha śaktijananaṃ prauḍhaḥ pratāpoditaṃ || 9 ||

iti śrīrudrayāmale tantre pātravandananavastotraṃ samāptaṃ ||


śrīgaṇeśāya namaḥ || 

atholūkakalpaḥ || 

rudrājñāpayati tena viṣṇusatvena ulūka āgaccha 2 praviśa 2 dhuna 2 ākarṣaya 2 
maṃḍala praveśaya 2 svāhā || ulūkasya śiraścaiva haritāla manaḥśilā |

anena cāṃjanaṃ kṛtvā dṛśyate sa carācaraṃ |
vidhānāni vicitrāṇi vīvarāṇi ca paśyati ||

ulūkasya vasā caiva navanītasamanvitaṃ |
gorocanasamāyuktā aṃtardhūmena pācayet ||

ajanenāṃjayennetraṃ dṛśyate sa carācaraṃ |
ulūkasya rasaṃ caiva ātmaraktasamanvitaṃ ||

trikaṭukena samāyuktaṃ aṃjayet tena cakṣuṣu |
adṛśyakaraṇaṃ sadyo nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ||

ulūkasya ca māṃsāni tagaraṃ caṃdanaṃ tathā |
kuṃkumena samāyuktaṃ peṣayedrocanā saha ||

annepānena dātavyaṃ strī vā puruṣe vaśyavā |
sarvavaśyaṃ bhavet tasya svātmaṃ sva ca parasva ca ||

ulūkasya ca pakṣāṇi viḍālasya nakhāni ca |
pādāpāṃśu samāsādya kākapakṣeṇa saiva hi ||

kaṭukīphalasamāyuktaṃ homayitvā vaśīkaraṃ |
vidveṣaśca na saṃdeho bhavate śatruṣu kṣayaṃ ||

ulūkasya tathāsthīni rājikātva ca meva ca || 

88a)

kaṭukītailasamāyuktā sodhyate sādhakottamaḥ |
mārayennātra saṃdeho sarvasyādehadhāraṇaṃ ||

atha maṃtraḥ || aṣṭottaraśataṃ japet || 

oṃ hrīṁ hraiṁ hraḥ huṃ phaṭ namaḥ || oṃ namo bhagavatyai āryatārā devyai purā 
devāsure yuddhe vivāhe vasya saṃsthitā |

tasya vāhanamatyugra ulūkonāmasottamaḥ |
tasyeṣṭe samāruhye dānavānāṃ vadhośritaḥ ||

śukra uvāca ||

kathaṃcaramate bhūmau kathamāhārameva ca |
kīdṛśaṃ karma kurute sa ca kāki tu kīdṛśī ||

alpāyuścayormatyai alpavīryastathāpare |
rogādayo na vādhyaṃte vahu kleśavaśaṃ kutaḥ ||

hitārthasarvasatvānāṃ vrūhi kāmāṃganāśanaḥ ||

īśvara uvāca ||

sādhu sādhu mahāvāho sādhakānāṃ hitāya ca |
vacanaṃ śṛṇu vakṣyāmi priyāsi tvaṃ yathākulaṃ ||

parvate himavatkūṭe vacanaṃ vahu bhayākule |
tataḥ pivati pānīyaṃ durgā durgā samukṣaye ||

tatra sthāne sthitau sau hi chubuko nāmanāmataḥ |
biḍāla sadṛśaṃ netra karṇau vāpi tathaiva ca ||

divākarastasya śatru māṃsāśī ca tathaiva ca |
divasaṃtiṣute netrau rātraucaryā samācare ||

adhunā saṃpravakṣyāmi lakṣaṇaṃ tasya tādṛśaṃ |
saubhāgyakaraṇaṃ sādhvī vidveṣoccāṭanaṃ tathā ||

cāturthikavināśīnaṃ sarvajvaravināśanaṃ |
ekāhikaṃ dvyāhikaṃ ca bhūtāpasmāranāśanaṃ ||

saṃprāṇa śamayā yāti garuḍasya ca pannaga |
ulūka cakṣurādāya gorocanasamanvitaṃ ||

vāriṇā saha dātavyaṃ vaśīkaraṇamuttamaṃ |
ulūka jihvā muddhṛtya dhartūrarasasamabhāvitaṃ ||

88b)

dhūpaṃ yasyā pradātavyaṃ vidveṣoccāṭanaṃ bhavet |
ulūkasya ca karṇau dvau piṃḍikā ca samanvitaṃ ||

sūkṣmacūrṇaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā mastake yasya nikṣipet |
atha pāneṣu bhakṣeṣu puṣpeṣu tilakeṣu ca || 

gaṃdhayukte tathāvastre yasya dadyāt kadācana |
nārī tasya vaśaṃ yāṃti svātmanena dhanena vā ||

janāḥ sarve vaśaṃ yāṃti yāvajjīvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ |
niśācarasya netre dve madhu jyeṣṭiḥkayai saha ||

haritālasya karṣau dvau kākamācī samāṃsakaiḥ |
aṃtardhūmaṃ dahet sarvaṃ chāgī mūtreṇa bhāvayet ||

netrāṇāmaṃjanaṃ dadyāccāturthika vināśanaṃ |
maṃgasya tadromāṇi yavasaktu samanvitaṃ ||

tilatailenasaṃyuktaṃ yasya dhūpaṃ pradā * yet |
bhūtagrahā ca kuṣmāṃḍāṃ ḍākinī sākinī tathā ||

nāmamātreṇa dattena kurvaṃtyā veśaṇaṃ kṣaṇāt |
palāyaṃte tato sarve daśāsu vidaśāsu ca ||

kṣayamā * stathāyāṃti siddhagaṇā mṛgā iva |
ulūka dakṣiṇaṃ pakṣaṃ śvetasūtreṇa vaṃdhayet ||

dakṣiṇe karṇamūle tu dvyāhikaṃ harati jvaraṃ |
ulūkasyottaraṃ pakṣaṃ raktasūtreṇavaṃdhayet ||

dakṣiṇe karṇamūle tu tryāhikaṃ harati jvaraṃ |
māṃgalyaṃ pucchapakṣaistu paṃcaraṃgena bhāvitaḥ ||

yasya pakṣagale vadhvā tryāhikaṃ tasya naśyati |
vadhātu dakṣiṇe vāhumaṃgalyaṃ dakṣiṇe padaṃ ||

pūrvoktaṃ cākṣayaṃ dadyā sakra vījapraṇāśanaṃ |

89a)

ulūkasya padaṃ vāmaṃbhujā vāmena baṃdhayet ||

duṣṭajvarapraśamanaṃ sarvajvaravināśanaṃ |
niśācarasya raktastu dvistrī rakta samaṃnvitaṃ ||

yasya nāma likhedbhūrje kṛṣṇasūtreṇa veṣṭayet |
śikhāgre vaṃdhayitvā tu tasya coccāṭanottamaṃ ||

tataḥ kṣīreṇasaṃkṣālya punaḥ śāṃti bhaviṣyati |
ulūksaya ca māṃsāni dhūpaṃ yasya pradāpayet ||

sarve grahā vinaśyaṃti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā |
ulūkasya tathā cāṃtraṃ lepo yasya pradāpayet ||

ekaviṃśasamāyukto sorśarogaiḥ pramucyate |
piṃḍikā kaṃḍurogaiśca mukto bhavati tatkṣaṇāt ||

sarve rogāḥ palāyaṃte siṃhasyāgre gajā iva |
ulūkasya tu pādaṃ tu śrotojanasamanvitaṃ ||

chāyāśuṣkaṃ tato kṛtvā netrāṇāmaṃjayet tu yaḥ |
dattamātreṇa tenaiva sodṛśo bhavati kṣaṇāt ||

nirmalāni ca netrāṇi sadā tasya bhavaṃti ca |
idaṃ rahasyaṃ paramaṃ na deyaṃ yasya kasyacit ||

pāpātmeṣu na dātavyaṃ dātavyaṃ bhaktavatsale |
ityau casanase śāstre kalpaṃ naktacaraṃ alaṃ ||

atha dvitīya kalpavarvaraṣyasyaliṣyate || 
varvaro rātri pakṣinī sāyomaṭate sadā ||

tasya karmaṃ ca kiṃ proktaṃ prasādaṃ kuru saṃkara ||

śiva uvāca ||

śṛṇu devi pradātavyaṃ rahasyaṃ paramaṃ priye |
niśāyāṃ ramate śopi mācuṣoṇāṃ vidyāṣu ca ||

śaunako nāma ṛṣayaḥ maṃgalo nāma saṃbhavaḥ |
tasya śrāpadadau brahmā ulūko pakṣiko bhavet ||

89b)

tasya karma pravakṣyāmi vidhānena tu pārvati |
na tithirna ca nakṣatraṃ na ca nātyopavāsanaṃ || 

na vāraṃ na japo homaṃ kālavelādivarjitaṃ |
kevalaṃ bhāvanāgamyaṃ kuryāt karmaṃ yathocitaṃ ||

ulūkaśaunakaścaiva * vārārātri pakṣikaḥ |
maṃgalasthalaśiraḥ ṣaṭnāmāni tasya ca ||

atha ulūkasya prayogaḥ || 

nāmuktāṃ mohanastaṃbhane uccāṭanaṃ rakṣaṇaṃ māraṇaṃ vaśīkaraṇa 
vyayet || yaduktaṃ ulūkasya ca netre ca rocanāgaurasarṣapā | 

kuṃkumaṃ nāgapuṣpaṃ ca samabhāgāni kārayet || 
neśaptadivasaṃ bhūṣaṃḍanidhāpayet || 

yasya dadyāmukhovāsaṃ sa vasyo maraṇāṃtakaṃ |
ulūkasya ca netre dve mārjarasya tathaiva ca ||

ekatra militaṃ kṛtvā vaktrī kuryād vicakṣaṇaḥ |
mahātailena prajvālya śmaśāne vā catuṣpathe ||

tathaiva kajjalaṃ grāhyaṃ netre tatkālamaṃjayet |
dattamātreṇa tenaiva naṣṭacchāyo bhaven naraḥ ||

ulūkacaṃcu saṃgrāhya gorocanā kuṃkumena tu |
tatsamaṃ nāgapuṣpeṣu samabhāgena cūrṇayet ||

anena tilakaṃ kuryāt trailokyaṃ vaśamānayet |
ulūkasya ca jihvāyā ajā gaṃdha manaḥśilā ||

vacācarmavaṭaṃ kuṣṭaṃ matsyā śṛṃgāvarocanaṃ |
kuṃkumaṃ cāśvalālāśu gomūtreṇa ca peṣaṇāt ||

anena tilakaṃ kuryāt rājastrīvaśamānayet |
ulūkasya śirogrāhyaṃ vāyasaścavastathā ||

ekatra dhūpadi ca tu vidveṣo jāyate kṣaṇāt |
ulūkasya ca grīvāyāṃ mārjārasya nakhastathā ||

90a)

unmattakarasaṃgrāhya niṃbakāṣṭhāsthi mānuṣaṃ |
ekatra guṭikāṃ kṛtvā śatruhāreṣu nikṣipet ||

uccāṭayen na saṃdeho yadi śatrasamopi ca |
ulūkasya tu vai kroḍaṃ matsyatailena varvapet ||

mahākekṣe dadedagdhaṃ navebhāṃḍena dāpayet |
cuhlyāgre tatkṣipet bhāṃḍaṃ yāvat saptadināni ca ||

astame divase prāpte mṛyate taṃtu tatkṣaṇāt |
ulūkasya tu pakṣāni aṃtardhūmena dāpayet ||

sūkṣmacūrṇaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā ghṛtena sahapācayet |
tenaivājñita netrastu lokānāṃ kurute vaśaṃ ||

ulūka māṃsa netre ca mahāmajjā tathaiva ca |
rocanena kṣataṃ yuktaṃ matsyatailena bhāvayet ||

tat tailaṃ grāhaye yatnāt śarīrobhyaṃjanaṃ tataḥ |
tena pṛṣṭhe vaśaṃ yāṃti yāvajjīvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ||

ulūkasya tu cāsthīni grāhayecca tathaiva ca |
ajāstu mānuṣasyāsthi tat yuktaṃ svātmane tumaṃ ||

anena lepayelliṃgaṃ pramadāni ca vaśīkaraṃ |
ulūkasya padaṃ raktaṃ anāmaraktalocanaṃ ||

likhitvā sādhyanāmnaiva yā pādyaṃ ca saṃpuṭaṃ |
bhūrjapatre tu saṃrakṣet raktasūtreṇa veṣṭayet ||

vāhukaṃṭhe śikhāyāṃ vā dhārayet taṃ vaśaṃ nayet |
ulūkasya kākapakṣāṇi sarpasyāpi ca kaṃcukīṃ ||

mūṣakaśca tathā viṣṭā guggulaṃ ghṛtameva ca |
eṣa dhūpavaraṃ coktaṃ sarvaduṣṭavināśanaṃ ||

skaṃdana nadīgaṇā sadyāpavanā brahmarākṣasā |
atigrahaśca ḍākinyā dhūponmādana nāśanaṃ ||

datta mātreṇa dhūpeṇa duṣṭārāśu palāyate |

90b)

ulūkasya ca jaṃghā ca parā ca taparīṣakaṃ ||

rocanaṃ kuṃkumaṃ caiva tilakaṃ kārayet tataḥ |
dṛṣṭamātreṇa tenaiva vaśyo bhavati garvitā ||

ulūkasya samagraṃ vai aṃtardhūpena dāpayet |
sūkṣmacūrṇaṃ tato kṛtvā chāgī mūtreṇa bhāvayet ||

yamūtra bhāvayedyala śarīre cānulepayet |
lepamātreṇa teṇaiva sadyo jvaranāśanaṃ ||

anya karma sahasrāṇi kurute nātra saṃśayaḥ |
ulūkasya śirogrāhyā hari bālamanaḥśilā ||

anenāṃ jayate cakṣuḥ paśyate sa carācaraṃ |
atha padādi tasyaiva dahyayitvā suvarṇayet ||

pādalepo pradātavya yojanānāṃ śataṃ vrajet |
ulūkasya jihvāyā kālīṣya vahumālatī ||

saṃyutaṃ tena kṛtvā ca guṭikā trilohena tu veṣṭayet |
mukhaprakṣepa mātreṇa dṛśyo bhavati tatkṣaṇāt ||

ulūkasya tu pakṣāṇi maṃtritāni ca saptadhā |
sthāpayitvānyapi dvāre yāvacchatra matadgataṃ ||

atha maṃtraḥ ||

oṃ namo kālarātri triśūlahastamahiṣavāhini rudrakapālamālākṛtaśeṣare 
āgaccha bhagavatī atulavalakāriṇī sarvakarmāṇimeva saṃkuru maheśvara 
ājñāpayati || śrīṃ śrīṃ śrīṃ phaṭ svāhā || 

ulūkasya ca viṣṭhā ca vālāmotho susaṃyutaṃ || 
dadyāt śirasi yasyaiva sa vaśyo marāṇānvitaṃ || 

ulūkasya tu liṃgāni pārāvata purīṣakaṃ |
rocanā kuṃkumairyuktaṃ tilakaṃ kārayet tataḥ ||

ulūka hṛdayaṃ grāhya gorocanasamāstute |

91)

saptavārānmaṃtrayitvā cakṣustenaivamaṃjayet ||

dṛṣṭamātreṇa tenaiva tasyaiva vaśyo bhavati tatkṣaṇaṃ ||

atha maṃtra pravakṣyāmi yaddatto śaṃbhunā mune |
sarvasiddhikaraṃ hyeta sarvasṛṣṭi pradāyakaṃ ||

oṃ namo mahāyakṣiṇī amukavaśamānaya svāhā ||

chuchuṃdarī khaṃjarīstu kṣārakoṭa prapeṣayet |
māyāmādāstu saṃyukta caturthyāṃ ca ravau dine ||

viṃdunāda sthitaṃ mūrdhni prathamaṃ vījamuktamaṃ |
paṃcamasyā dvitīyaṃ tu paṃcamasvaravedine ||

visargayuktaṃ deveśi tṛtīyaṃ varṇamuttamaṃ |
sūyamajjāṃ svaropete viṃduyuktaṃ sureśvari ||

caturthe bhavate vipra svara uṣaṣṭhe prakīrtiṇa |
oṃkārayuktaṃ ca tayā namaskāraṃ tu vinyaset ||

aṣṭākṣaramidaṃ maṃtraṃ sarvasiddhipradāyakāṃ ||

oṃ namo lohitapiṃgalāya mātaṃgarājāya strīṇāṃ rudhirastaṃbhaya 2 mudga 2 
laka 2 kīlaya 2 cili 2 svāhā || ayaṃ strīṇāmatirajonivāraṇamaṃtra || 

iti dvitīyakalpaṃ ca ulūkasya alaṃkṛtaṃ || śubhamastu ||
